### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra + Especialista Backend

### CONTEXTO:
A V10 do DIYAPP atingiu limites de escalabilidade com arquitetura monolítica. Necessidade de:
1. Deploy independente por funcionalidade
2. Escala horizontal seletiva
3. Stack tecnológica diversificada por domínio
4. Isolamento de falhas
5. Time-to-market mais rápido para novas features

### DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes princípios:
- **12-Factor App** para cada serviço
- **Domain-Driven Design** para bounded contexts
- **Comunicação**: gRPC para síncrono, Eventos para assíncrono
- **Orquestração**: Kubernetes com service mesh (Istio)
- **Observabilidade**: OpenTelemetry + Prometheus + Grafana
- **Banco de dados**: Database-per-service com CQRS para domínios complexos

### OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A**: Monólito modularizado - Prós: Simplicidade operacional, transações ACID fáceis. Contras: Escalabilidade limitada, deploy all-or-nothing.
- **Opção B**: Microsserviços full - Prós: Escalabilidade independente, resiliência, polyglot. Contras: Complexidade operacional, consistência eventual.
- **Opção C**: Arquitetura de módulos (modulith) - Prós: Balance entre A e B. Contras: Compromisso que pode não atender crescimento futuro.

**Opção escolhida: B** - Justificativa: O roadmap V11 prevê crescimento 10x em usuários e 5x em features. Microsserviços permitem escalar apenas os serviços críticos e adotar tecnologias específicas por domínio.

### CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Deploy independente por squad
- Escala seletiva de serviços críticos
- Isolamento de falhas
- Adoção de tecnologias específicas por domínio
- Paralelismo de desenvolvimento

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade de operações distribuídas
- Consistência eventual em alguns fluxos
- Overhead de comunicação entre serviços
- Monitoramento distribuído necessário

**Riscos:**
- Latência em cadeias de chamadas longas
- Debug distribuído complexo
- Mitigação: Service mesh com tracing, circuit breakers, timeouts configuráveis

### REVISÃO: 2024-07-15 (6 meses para avaliar complexidade vs benefícios)

---

## 2. Engineering Standards - V11 Microsserviços

```yaml
# engineering-standards-v11.md

# DIYAPP V11 - Engineering Standards

## Estrutura de Repositório
```
service-[nome]/
├── src/
│   ├── proto/                    # Definições gRPC
│   ├── domain/                   # Lógica de domínio
│   ├── application/              # Casos de uso
│   ├── infrastructure/           # Implementações técnicas
│   ├── interfaces/               # Controllers, gRPC handlers
│   └── main.ts                   # Ponto de entrada
├── tests/
│   ├── unit/
│   ├── integration/
│   └── e2e/
├── Dockerfile
├── docker-compose.yml           # Para desenvolvimento
├── helm/                        # Charts Kubernetes
├── .github/workflows/           # CI/CD
├── .env.example
├── .gitignore
├── package.json
├── tsconfig.json
└── README.md
```

## Padrões de Código
- **Linguagem**: TypeScript (Node.js 18+)
- **Style Guide**: ESLint + Prettier config padrão
- **Convenções**: 
  - Classes: PascalCase
  - Funções/métodos: camelCase
  - Variáveis: camelCase
  - Constantes: UPPER_SNAKE_CASE
  - Interfaces: Prefixo I (ex: IUserRepository)
  - Arquivos: kebab-case

## Padrões de API
- **gRPC**: Para comunicação síncrona entre serviços
- **REST**: Apenas para APIs públicas (BFF pattern)
- **Eventos**: Kafka para comunicação assíncrona
- **Versionamento**: Semver para APIs públicas

## Banco de Dados
- **Princípio**: Database-per-service
- **Migrations**: Controladas por código, versionadas
- **CQRS**: Para domínios complexos (ex: Orders, Analytics)

## Logging
- **Estrutura**: JSON logs com correlation-id
- **Níveis**: error, warn, info, debug, trace
- **Sensíveis**: Nunca logar tokens, senhas, PII

## Segurança
- **Autenticação**: JWT com OAuth2.0
- **Autorização**: RBAC por serviço
- **Secrets**: HashiCorp Vault ou Kubernetes Secrets
- **Scan**: Snyk/Dependabot obrigatório no CI

## Testes
- **Cobertura mínima**: 80%
- **Tipos**: Unit (Jest), Integration (Supertest), E2E (Cypress)
- **Mocks**: Para serviços externos apenas

## Commits
- **Conventional Commits**: feat:, fix:, chore:, docs:, test:, refactor:
- **Scope**: Nome do serviço (ex: `feat(auth): add 2FA`)
- **Body**: Descrição técnica da mudança
- **Footer**: Links para tickets (ex: `Closes #123`)

## CI/CD
- **PR**: Todos os testes devem passar
- **Main**: Deploy automático para staging
- **Tags**: Deploy manual para produção
- **Rollback**: Automático se health check falhar
```

---

## 3. Template de Repositório CI/CD

```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-cd.yml
name: CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [ main, develop ]
  pull_request:
    branches: [ main ]

env:
  REGISTRY: ghcr.io
  IMAGE_NAME: ${{ github.repository }}/service-${{ github.event.repository.name }}

jobs:
  quality:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v3
        with:
          node-version: '18'
          cache: 'npm'
          
      - name: Install dependencies
        run: npm ci
        
      - name: Lint
        run: npm run lint
        
      - name: Type check
        run: npm run type-check
        
      - name: Unit tests
        run: npm test -- --coverage
        
      - name: Upload coverage
        uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
        with:
          file: ./coverage/lcov.info
          
      - name: Security scan
        uses: snyk/actions/node@master
        env:
          SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
        with:
          args: --severity-threshold=high

  build:
    needs: quality
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/main' || github.ref == 'refs/heads/develop'
    
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v3
      
      - name: Set up Docker Buildx
        uses: docker/setup-buildx-action@v2
        
      - name: Log in to Container Registry
        uses: docker/login-action@v2
        with:
          registry: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}
          username: ${{ github.actor }}
          password: ${{ secrets.GITHUB_TOKEN }}
          
      - name: Extract metadata
        id: meta
        uses: docker/metadata-action@v4
        with:
          images: ${{ env.REGISTRY }}/${{ env.IMAGE_NAME }}
          tags: |
            type=ref,event=branch
            type=sha,prefix={{branch}}-
            
      - name: Build and push
        uses: docker/build-push-action@v4
        with:
          context: .
          push: true
          tags: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.tags }}
          labels: ${{ steps.meta.outputs.labels }}
          cache-from: type=gha
          cache-to: type=gha,mode=max

  deploy-staging:
    needs: build
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: github.ref == 'refs/heads/develop'
    
    steps:
      - name: Deploy to Staging
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@master
        with:
          host: ${{ secrets.STAGING_HOST }}
          username: ${{ secrets.STAGING_USER }}
          key: ${{ secrets.STAGING_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            cd /opt/diyapp/staging
            ./deploy-service.sh ${{ github.event.repository.name }}

  deploy-production:
    needs: build
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    if: startsWith(github.ref, 'refs/tags/v')
    
    steps:
      - name: Deploy to Production
        uses: appleboy/ssh-action@master
        with:
          host: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_HOST }}
          username: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_USER }}
          key: ${{ secrets.PRODUCTION_SSH_KEY }}
          script: |
            cd /opt/diyapp/production
            ./deploy-service.sh ${{ github.event.repository.name }} --version ${{ github.ref_name }}
```

## 4. Template de Serviço Base

```typescript
// src/infrastructure/config/env.ts
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import { z } from 'zod';

dotenv.config();

const envSchema = z.object({
  NODE_ENV: z.enum(['development', 'test', 'production']).default('development'),
  PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('3000'),
  SERVICE_NAME: z.string(),
  GRPC_PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('50051'),
  KAFKA_BROKERS: z.string().default('localhost:9092'),
  DATABASE_URL: z.string(),
  JWT_SECRET: z.string(),
  OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT: z.string().optional(),
});

export type Env = z.infer<typeof envSchema>;
export const env = envSchema.parse(process.env);
```

```typescript
// src/infrastructure/observability/tracing.ts
import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-grpc';
import { Resource } from '@opentelemetry/resources';
import { SemanticResourceAttributes } from '@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions';

export const initTracing = (serviceName: string) => {
  const sdk = new NodeSDK({
    resource: new Resource({
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: serviceName,
    }),
    traceExporter: new OTLPTraceExporter({
      url: process.env.OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4317',
    }),
    instrumentations: [getNodeAutoInstrumentations()],
  });

  sdk.start();
  return sdk;
};
```

```proto
// src/proto/service.proto
syntax = "proto3";

package diyapp.v1;

service UserService {
  rpc GetUser(GetUserRequest) returns (UserResponse);
  rpc CreateUser(CreateUserRequest) returns (UserResponse);
  rpc UpdateUser(UpdateUserRequest) returns (UserResponse);
}

message GetUserRequest {
  string user_id = 1;
}

message CreateUserRequest {
  string email = 1;
  string name = 2;
}

message UpdateUserRequest {
  string user_id = 1;
  optional string email = 2;
  optional string name = 3;
}

message UserResponse {
  string user_id = 1;
  string email = 2;
  string name = 3;
  string created_at = 4;
  string updated_at = 5;
}
```

```typescript
// src/main.ts
import { Server, ServerCredentials } from '@grpc/grpc-js';
import { UserServiceService } from './proto/user_grpc_pb';
import { UserService } from './interfaces/grpc/user.service';
import { initTracing } from './infrastructure/observability/tracing';
import { env } from './infrastructure/config/env';
import { logger } from './infrastructure/observability/logger';
import { initKafka } from './infrastructure/messaging/kafka';

async function bootstrap() {
  // Initialize observability
  initTracing(env.SERVICE_NAME);
  
  // Initialize messaging
  await initKafka();
  
  // Create gRPC server
  const server = new Server();
  server.addService(UserServiceService, new UserService());
  
  // Start server
  server.bindAsync(
    `0.0.0.0:${env.GRPC_PORT}`,
    ServerCredentials.createInsecure(),
    (error, port) => {
      if (error) {
        logger.error('Failed to start gRPC server', { error });
        process.exit(1);
      }
      
      logger.info(`gRPC server listening on port ${port}`);
      
      // Graceful shutdown
      process.on('SIGTERM', () => {
        logger.info('SIGTERM received, shutting down gracefully');
        server.tryShutdown(() => {
          logger.info('Server shutdown complete');
          process.exit(0);
        });
      });
    }
  );
}

bootstrap().catch((error) => {
  logger.error('Bootstrap failed', { error });
  process.exit(1);
});
```

```dockerfile
# Dockerfile
FROM node:18-alpine AS builder

WORKDIR /app

COPY package*.json ./
RUN npm ci --only=production

COPY . .
RUN npm run build

FROM node:18-alpine AS runner

WORKDIR /app

RUN addgroup -g 1001 -S nodejs
RUN adduser -S nodejs -u 1001

COPY --from=builder /app/node_modules ./node_modules
COPY --from=builder /app/dist ./dist
COPY --from=builder /app/package.json ./package.json

USER nodejs

EXPOSE 3000
EXPOSE 50051

HEALTHCHECK --interval=30s --timeout=3s --start-period=5s --retries=3 \
  CMD node -e "require('http').get('http://localhost:3000/health', (r) => {process.exit(r.statusCode === 200 ? 0 : 1)})"

CMD ["node", "dist/main.js"]
```

## 5. Helm Chart Template

```yaml
# helm/templates/service.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: {{ .Chart.Name }}
  labels:
    app: {{ .Chart.Name }}
    version: {{ .Chart.AppVersion }}
spec:
  ports:
  - port: 80
    targetPort: http
    name: http
  - port: 50051
    targetPort: grpc
    name: grpc
  selector:
    app: {{ .Chart.Name }}
---
# helm/templates/deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: {{ .Chart.Name }}
spec:
  replicas: {{ .Values.replicaCount }}
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: {{ .Chart.Name }}
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: {{ .Chart.Name }}
        version: {{ .Chart.AppVersion }}
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: {{ .Chart.Name }}
        image: "{{ .Values.image.repository }}:{{ .Values.image.tag }}"
        imagePullPolicy: {{ .Values.image.pullPolicy }}
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
          name: http
        - containerPort: 50051
          name: grpc
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: SERVICE_NAME
          value: {{ .Chart.Name }}
        - name: GRPC_PORT
          value: "50051"
        envFrom:
        - secretRef:
            name: {{ .Chart.Name }}-secrets
        resources:
          {{- toYaml .Values.resources | nindent 12 }}
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: http
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: http
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
---
# helm/templates/hpa.yaml
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: {{ .Chart.Name }}-hpa
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: {{ .Chart.Name }}
  minReplicas: {{ .Values.autoscaling.minReplicas }}
  maxReplicas: {{ .Values.autoscaling.maxReplicas }}
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: {{ .Values.autoscaling.targetCPU }}
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: memory
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: {{ .Values.autoscaling.targetMemory }}
```

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Design Atômico

Vou criar um sistema de design atômico completo com tokens, componentes e diretrizes de acessibilidade, implementado como uma biblioteca de design funcional com documentação interativa.

```html

### vite.config.ts
```typescript
import { defineConfig } from 'vite'
import react from '@vitejs/plugin-react'
import path from 'path'

export default defineConfig({
  plugins: [react()],
  resolve: {
    alias: {
      '@': path.resolve(__dirname, './src'),
      '@components': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/components'),
      '@pages': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/pages'),
      '@hooks': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/hooks'),
      '@store': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/store'),
      '@utils': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/utils'),
      '@types': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/types'),
      '@services': path.resolve(__dirname, './src/services'),
    },
  },
  server: {
    port: 3000,
    host: true,
  },
  build: {
    outDir: 'dist',
    sourcemap: true,
    rollupOptions: {
      output: {
        manualChunks: {
          vendor: ['react', 'react-dom', 'react-router-dom'],
          ui: ['lucide-react', 'clsx'],
          state: ['zustand'],
          forms: ['react-hook-form', 'zod'],
        },
      },
    },
  },
  test: {
    globals: true,
    environment: 'jsdom',
    setupFiles: ['./src/test/setup.ts'],
  },
})
```

    @apply border-neutral-200;

  html {
    @apply scroll-smooth;
  }

  body {
    @apply font-sans text-neutral-900 bg-neutral-50 antialiased;
  }

  [data-theme="dark"] body {
    @apply text-neutral-100 bg-neutral-900;
  }

  /* Focus styles for accessibility */
  :focus-visible {
    @apply outline-2 outline-primary-500 outline-offset-2;
  }

  /* Selection styles */
  ::selection {
    @apply bg-primary-100 text-primary-900;
  }

  [data-theme="dark"] ::selection {
    @apply bg-primary-900 text-primary-100;
  }
}

  /* Button base styles */

## 1. Configuração do Ambiente e Dependências

**package.json**
```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v11-core",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "DIYAPP Evolution V11 Core Services",
  "main": "src/app.js",
  "scripts": {
    "start": "node src/app.js",
    "dev": "nodemon src/app.js",
    "test": "jest --coverage",
    "test:unit": "jest tests/unit --coverage",
    "test:integration": "jest tests/integration --coverage",
    "lint": "eslint src/",
    "migrate": "node scripts/migrate.js",
    "migrate:rollback": "node scripts/migrate.js --rollback",
    "generate:openapi": "node scripts/generate-openapi.js"

## 2. Configuração do Banco de Dados (PostgreSQL)

**src/config/database.js**
```javascript
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const winston = require('winston');

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: 'info',
  format: winston.format.json(),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/database-error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/database-combined.log' })
  ]
});

class DatabaseConnection {
  constructor() {
    this.pool = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
    this.connectionAttempts = 0;
    this.maxRetries = 3;
    this.retryDelay = 5000; // 5 seconds
  }

  async connect() {
    const config = {
      host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT) || 5432,
      database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v11',
      user: process.env.DB_USER || 'diyapp_user',
      password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'secure_password',
      max: 20, // max number of clients in the pool
      idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
      connectionTimeoutMillis: 5000,
      ssl: process.env.NODE_ENV === 'production' ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false
    };

    this.pool = new Pool(config);

    // Add error handling to the pool
    this.pool.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Unexpected error on idle client', {
        error: err.message,
        stack: err.stack,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    });

    try {
      // Test connection
      const client = await this.pool.connect();
      const result = await client.query('SELECT NOW() as current_time');
      client.release();
      
      this.isConnected = true;
      logger.info('Database connected successfully', {
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
        database: config.database
      });
      
      return this.pool;
    } catch (error) {
      this.isConnected = false;
      this.connectionAttempts++;
      
      logger.error('Database connection failed', {
        error: error.message,
        attempt: this.connectionAttempts,
        maxRetries: this.maxRetries,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });

      if (this.connectionAttempts < this.maxRetries) {
        logger.info(`Retrying connection in ${this.retryDelay/1000} seconds...`);
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, this.retryDelay));
        return this.connect();
      } else {
        throw new Error(`Failed to connect to database after ${this.maxRetries} attempts: ${error.message}`);
      }
    }
  }

  async query(text, params) {
    if (!this.isConnected) {
      throw new Error('Database not connected');
    }

    const start = Date.now();
    try {
      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      logger.debug('Query executed', {
        query: text,
        duration: `${duration}ms`,
        rowCount: result.rowCount,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });

      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      logger.error('Query failed', {
        query: text,
        params: params ? params.map(p => typeof p === 'string' ? p.substring(0, 100) : p) : [],
        error: error.message,
        duration: `${duration}ms`,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });

      throw error;
    }
  }

  async disconnect() {
    if (this.pool) {
      await this.pool.end();
      this.isConnected = false;
      logger.info('Database disconnected', {
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
  }

  getConnectionStatus() {
    return {
      isConnected: this.isConnected,
      connectionAttempts: this.connectionAttempts,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };
  }
}

// Singleton instance
const database = new DatabaseConnection();

module.exports = database;
```

## 3. Configuração do Redis com Circuit Breaker

**src/config/redis.js**
```javascript
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const CircuitBreaker = require('circuit-breaker-js');
const winston = require('winston');

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: 'info',
  format: winston.format.json(),
  transports: [
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/redis-error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new winston.transports.File({ filename: 'logs/redis-combined.log' })
  ]
});

class RedisService {
  constructor() {
    this.client = null;
    this.isConnected = false;
    this.circuitBreaker = null;
    this.initializeCircuitBreaker();
  }

  initializeCircuitBreaker() {
    this.circuitBreaker = new CircuitBreaker({
      timeoutDuration: 5000, // 5 seconds timeout
      volumeThreshold: 10, // Minimum number of requests before circuit can trip
      errorThreshold: 50, // Percentage of errors that will trip the circuit
      onCircuitOpen: (metrics) => {
        logger.warn('Redis circuit breaker opened', {
          metrics,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      },
      onCircuitClose: (metrics) => {
        logger.info('Redis circuit breaker closed', {
          metrics,
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
      }
    });
  }

  async connect() {
    const config = {
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_PORT) || 6379,
      password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD || null,
      db: parseInt(process.env.REDIS_DB) || 0,
      retryStrategy: (times) => {
        const delay = Math.min(times * 100, 3000);
        logger.info(`Redis reconnecting attempt ${times}, delay: ${delay}ms`);
        return delay;
      },
      maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
      enableReadyCheck: true,
      connectTimeout: 10000,
      lazyConnect: false
    };

    this.client = new Redis(config);

    this.client.on('connect', () => {
      this.isConnected = true;
      logger.info('Redis connected successfully', {
        host: config.host,
        port: config.port,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    });

    this.client.on('error', (error) => {
      logger.error('Redis connection error', {
        error: error.message,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
      this.isConnected = false;
    });

    this.client.on('close', () => {
      logger.warn('Redis connection closed', {
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
      this.isConnected = false;
    });

    this.client.on('reconnecting', () => {
      logger.info('Redis reconnecting...', {
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    });

    try {
      await this.client.ping();
      return this.client;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Failed to connect to Redis', {
        error: error.message,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async executeWithCircuitBreaker(operation, ...args) {
    return new Promise((resolve, reject) => {
      this.circuitBreaker.run((success, fail) => {
        const startTime = Date.now();
        
        operation(...args)
          .then((result) => {
            const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
            logger.debug('Redis operation succeeded', {
              operation: operation.name || 'anonymous',
              duration: `${duration}ms`,
              timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            });
            success(result);
          })
          .catch((error) => {
            const duration = Date.now() - startTime;
            logger.error('Redis operation failed', {
              operation: operation.name || 'anonymous',
              error: error.message,
              duration: `${duration}ms`,
              timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            });
            fail(error);
          });
      }, (error) => {
        // Fallback when circuit is open
        logger.warn('Using fallback for Redis operation - circuit open', {
          operation: operation.name || 'anonymous',
          timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
        });
        reject(new Error('Redis service unavailable - using fallback'));
      }).then(resolve).catch(reject);
    });
  }

  async get(key) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker(async () => {
      return await this.client.get(key);
    });
  }

  async set(key, value, ttl = 3600) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker(async () => {
      if (ttl > 0) {
        return await this.client.setex(key, ttl, value);
      } else {
        return await this.client.set(key, value);
      }
    });
  }

  async del(key) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker(async () => {
      return await this.client.del(key);
    });
  }

  async hset(key, field, value) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker(async () => {
      return await this.client.hset(key, field, value);
    });
  }

  async hget(key, field) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker(async () => {
      return await this.client.hget(key, field);
    });
  }

  async disconnect() {
    if (this.client) {
      await this.client.quit();
      this.isConnected = false;
      logger.info('Redis disconnected', {
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
  }

  getStatus() {
    return {
      isConnected: this.isConnected,
      circuitBreakerState: this.circuitBreaker.isOpen() ? 'OPEN' : 'CLOSED',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    };
  }
}

// Singleton instance
const redisService = new RedisService();

module.exports = redisService;
```

## 4. Modelos do Banco de Dados

**src/database/models/user.model.js**
```javascript
const database = require('../../config/database');
const bcrypt = require('bcrypt');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');

class UserModel {
  constructor() {
    this.tableName = 'users';
  }

  async createTable() {
    const query = `
      CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS ${this.tableName} (
        id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
        email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
        password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
        full_name VARCHAR(255),
        avatar_url TEXT,
        is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
        is_email_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
        last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
        failed_login_attempts INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
        lock_until TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
        mfa_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
        mfa_secret VARCHAR(255),
        role VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'user',
        metadata JSONB DEFAULT '{}',
        created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
        deleted_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE
      );

      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_email ON ${this.tableName}(email);
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_username ON ${this.tableName}(username);
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_created_at ON ${this.tableName}(created_at);
      CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_users_is_active ON ${this.tableName}(is_active);
    `;

    await database.query(query);
  }

  async create(userData) {
    const {
      email,
      username,
      password,
      full_name,
      avatar_url,
      role = 'user'
    } = userData;

    // Hash password
    const saltRounds = 10;
    const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(password, saltRounds);

    const query = `
      INSERT INTO ${this.tableName} 
        (email, username, password_hash, full_name, avatar_url, role)
      VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, $5, $6)
      RETURNING id, email, username, full_name, avatar_url, role, created_at
    `;

    const params = [email, username, passwordHash, full_name, avatar_url, role];
    const result = await database.query(query, params);

    return result.rows[0];
  }

  async findByEmail(email) {
    const query = `
      SELECT * FROM ${this.tableName} 
      WHERE email = $1 AND deleted_at IS NULL
      LIMIT 1
    `;
    
    const result = await database.query(query, [email]);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  async findById(id) {
    const query = `
      SELECT id, email, username, full_name, avatar_url, role, 
             is_active, is_email_verified, created_at, updated_at, metadata
      FROM ${this.tableName} 
      WHERE id = $1 AND deleted_at IS NULL
      LIMIT 1
    `;
    
    const result = await database.query(query, [id]);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  async findByUsername(username) {
    const query = `
      SELECT * FROM ${this.tableName} 
      WHERE username = $1 AND deleted_at IS NULL
      LIMIT 1
    `;
    
    const result = await database.query(query, [username]);
    return result.rows[0];
  }

  async update(id, updates) {
    const allowedFields = ['full_name', 'avatar_url', 'metadata', 'is_active'];
    const setClauses = [];
    const values = [];
    let paramIndex = 1;

    for (const [field, value] of Object.entries(updates)) {
      if (allowedFields.includes(field)) {
        setClauses.push(`${field} = $${paramIndex}`);
        values.push(value);
        paramIndex++;
      }
    }

    if (setClauses.length === 0) {
      throw new Error('No valid fields to update');
    }

    setClauses.push('updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP');
    values.push(id);

    const query = `
      UPDATE ${this.tableName}
      SET ${setClauses.join(', ')}
      WHERE id = $${paramIndex} AND deleted_at IS NULL
     

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]

## 1. Terraform - Módulo VPC (AWS)

**infra/terraform/modules/vpc/main.tf**
```terraform
# VPC Module for EKS Cluster
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
  }
}

resource "aws_vpc" "main" {
  cidr_block           = var.vpc_cidr
  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-vpc"
  })
}

resource "aws_subnet" "private" {
  count             = length(var.private_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = var.private_subnet_cidrs[count.index]
  availability_zone = var.availability_zones[count.index % length(var.availability_zones)]
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-private-${count.index}"
    "kubernetes.io/role/internal-elb" = "1"
  })
}

resource "aws_subnet" "public" {
  count             = length(var.public_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id            = aws_vpc.main.id
  cidr_block        = var.public_subnet_cidrs[count.index]
  availability_zone = var.availability_zones[count.index % length(var.availability_zones)]
  map_public_ip_on_launch = true
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-public-${count.index}"
    "kubernetes.io/role/elb" = "1"
  })
}

resource "aws_eip" "nat" {
  count = length(var.public_subnet_cidrs)
  domain = "vpc"
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-nat-${count.index}"
  })
}

resource "aws_nat_gateway" "main" {
  count         = length(var.public_subnet_cidrs)
  allocation_id = aws_eip.nat[count.index].id
  subnet_id     = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-nat-${count.index}"
  })
}

resource "aws_route_table" "private" {
  count  = length(var.private_subnet_cidrs)
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block     = "0.0.0.0/0"
    nat_gateway_id = aws_nat_gateway.main[count.index % length(aws_nat_gateway.main)].id
  }
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-private-rt-${count.index}"
  })
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "private" {
  count          = length(var.private_subnet_cidrs)
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.private[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.private[count.index].id
}

resource "aws_route_table" "public" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  route {
    cidr_block = "0.0.0.0/0"
    gateway_id = aws_internet_gateway.main.id
  }
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-public-rt"
  })
}

resource "aws_internet_gateway" "main" {
  vpc_id = aws_vpc.main.id
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "${var.cluster_name}-igw"
  })
}

resource "aws_route_table_association" "public" {
  count          = length(var.public_subnet_cidrs)
  subnet_id      = aws_subnet.public[count.index].id
  route_table_id = aws_route_table.public.id
}
```

**infra/terraform/modules/vpc/variables.tf**
```terraform
variable "cluster_name" {
  description = "Name of the EKS cluster"
  type        = string
}

variable "vpc_cidr" {
  description = "CIDR block for VPC"
  type        = string
  default     = "10.0.0.0/16"
}

variable "private_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "List of private subnet CIDRs"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.1.0/24", "10.0.2.0/24", "10.0.3.0/24"]
}

variable "public_subnet_cidrs" {
  description = "List of public subnet CIDRs"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["10.0.101.0/24", "10.0.102.0/24", "10.0.103.0/24"]
}

variable "availability_zones" {
  description = "List of availability zones"
  type        = list(string)
  default     = ["us-east-1a", "us-east-1b", "us-east-1c"]
}

variable "tags" {
  description = "Tags to apply to all resources"
  type        = map(string)
  default     = {}
}
```

## 2. Terraform - Módulo EKS

**infra/terraform/modules/eks/main.tf**
```terraform
# EKS Cluster Module
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
  }
}

data "aws_iam_policy_document" "cluster_assume_role" {
  statement {
    effect = "Allow"
    principals {
      type        = "Service"
      identifiers = ["eks.amazonaws.com"]
    }
    actions = ["sts:AssumeRole"]
  }
}

resource "aws_iam_role" "cluster" {
  name               = "${var.cluster_name}-cluster-role"
  assume_role_policy = data.aws_iam_policy_document.cluster_assume_role.json
  
  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "cluster_AmazonEKSClusterPolicy" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKSClusterPolicy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.cluster.name
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "cluster_AmazonEKSVPCResourceController" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKSVPCResourceController"
  role       = aws_iam_role.cluster.name
}

resource "aws_eks_cluster" "main" {
  name     = var.cluster_name
  role_arn = aws_iam_role.cluster.arn
  version  = var.kubernetes_version
  
  vpc_config {
    subnet_ids              = var.subnet_ids
    endpoint_private_access = true
    endpoint_public_access  = true
    public_access_cidrs     = var.public_access_cidrs
  }
  
  enabled_cluster_log_types = ["api", "audit", "authenticator", "controllerManager", "scheduler"]
  
  tags = var.tags
  
  depends_on = [
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.cluster_AmazonEKSClusterPolicy,
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.cluster_AmazonEKSVPCResourceController,
  ]
}

# Node Group IAM Role
data "aws_iam_policy_document" "node_assume_role" {
  statement {
    effect = "Allow"
    principals {
      type        = "Service"
      identifiers = ["ec2.amazonaws.com"]
    }
    actions = ["sts:AssumeRole"]
  }
}

resource "aws_iam_role" "node" {
  name               = "${var.cluster_name}-node-role"
  assume_role_policy = data.aws_iam_role_policy_document.node_assume_role.json
  
  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "node_AmazonEKSWorkerNodePolicy" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKSWorkerNodePolicy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.node.name
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "node_AmazonEKS_CNI_Policy" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEKS_CNI_Policy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.node.name
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "node_AmazonEC2ContainerRegistryReadOnly" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AmazonEC2ContainerRegistryReadOnly"
  role       = aws_iam_role.node.name
}

# Managed Node Groups
resource "aws_eks_node_group" "main" {
  for_each = var.node_groups
  
  cluster_name    = aws_eks_cluster.main.name
  node_group_name = each.key
  node_role_arn   = aws_iam_role.node.arn
  subnet_ids      = var.subnet_ids
  
  scaling_config {
    desired_size = each.value.desired_size
    max_size     = each.value.max_size
    min_size     = each.value.min_size
  }
  
  instance_types = each.value.instance_types
  
  tags = merge(var.tags, each.value.tags)
  
  depends_on = [
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.node_AmazonEKSWorkerNodePolicy,
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.node_AmazonEKS_CNI_Policy,
    aws_iam_role_policy_attachment.node_AmazonEC2ContainerRegistryReadOnly,
  ]
}

# Kubernetes Provider Configuration
provider "kubernetes" {
  host                   = aws_eks_cluster.main.endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(aws_eks_cluster.main.certificate_authority[0].data)
  exec {
    api_version = "client.authentication.k8s.io/v1beta1"
    command     = "aws"
    args = [
      "eks",
      "get-token",
      "--cluster-name",
      aws_eks_cluster.main.name
    ]
  }
}

provider "helm" {
  kubernetes {
    host                   = aws_eks_cluster.main.endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(aws_eks_cluster.main.certificate_authority[0].data)
    exec {
      api_version = "client.authentication.k8s.io/v1beta1"
      command     = "aws"
      args = [
        "eks",
        "get-token",
        "--cluster-name",
        aws_eks_cluster.main.name
      ]
    }
  }
}

# Cluster Autoscaler IAM Policy
resource "aws_iam_policy" "cluster_autoscaler" {
  name        = "${var.cluster_name}-cluster-autoscaler"
  description = "Policy for cluster autoscaler"
  
  policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Effect = "Allow"
        Action = [
          "autoscaling:DescribeAutoScalingGroups",
          "autoscaling:DescribeAutoScalingInstances",
          "autoscaling:DescribeLaunchConfigurations",
          "autoscaling:DescribeTags",
          "autoscaling:SetDesiredCapacity",
          "autoscaling:TerminateInstanceInAutoScalingGroup",
          "ec2:DescribeLaunchTemplateVersions"
        ]
        Resource = "*"
      }
    ]
  })
  
  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "node_cluster_autoscaler" {
  policy_arn = aws_iam_policy.cluster_autoscaler.arn
  role       = aws_iam_role.node.name
}

# EBS CSI Driver IAM Role
resource "aws_iam_role" "ebs_csi" {
  name = "${var.cluster_name}-ebs-csi-role"
  
  assume_role_policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Effect = "Allow"
        Principal = {
          Service = "eks.amazonaws.com"
        }
        Action = "sts:AssumeRoleWithWebIdentity"
        Condition = {
          StringEquals = {
            "${replace(aws_eks_cluster.main.identity[0].oidc[0].issuer, "https://", "")}:sub" = "system:serviceaccount:kube-system:ebs-csi-controller-sa"
          }
        }
      }
    ]
  })
  
  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_iam_role_policy_attachment" "ebs_csi" {
  policy_arn = "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/service-role/AmazonEBSCSIDriverPolicy"
  role       = aws_iam_role.ebs_csi.name
}

resource "aws_eks_addon" "ebs_csi" {
  cluster_name             = aws_eks_cluster.main.name
  addon_name              = "aws-ebs-csi-driver"
  addon_version           = "v1.26.0-eksbuild.1"
  service_account_role_arn = aws_iam_role.ebs_csi.arn
  
  depends_on = [aws_eks_node_group.main]
}
```

## 3. Terraform - Módulo de Monitoramento

**infra/terraform/modules/monitoring/main.tf**
```terraform
# Monitoring Module with Prometheus and Grafana
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
  }
}

# Prometheus Stack
resource "helm_release" "prometheus_stack" {
  name       = "prometheus-stack"
  repository = "https://prometheus-community.github.io/helm-charts"
  chart      = "kube-prometheus-stack"
  namespace  = "monitoring"
  create_namespace = true
  version    = "46.8.0"
  
  values = [templatefile("${path.module}/values/prometheus-values.yaml", {
    cluster_name = var.cluster_name
    storage_class = var.storage_class
    retention = var.prometheus_retention
  })]
  
  set {
    name  = "prometheus.prometheusSpec.storageSpec.volumeClaimTemplate.spec.storageClassName"
    value = var.storage_class
  }
  
  set {
    name  = "grafana.adminPassword"
    value = var.grafana_admin_password
  }
  
  set {
    name  = "grafana.persistence.storageClassName"
    value = var.storage_class
  }
  
  depends_on = [kubernetes_namespace.monitoring]
}

# Custom SLO Rules
resource "kubernetes_config_map" "slo_rules" {
  metadata {
    name      = "slo-rules"
    namespace = "monitoring"
  }
  
  data = {
    "slo-rules.yaml" = <<-EOT
    groups:
    - name: slo.rules
      rules:
      - record: job:slo_errors:rate5m
        expr: |
          sum(rate(http_requests_total{status=~"5.."}[5m])) by (job)
          /
          sum(rate(http_requests_total[5m])) by (job)
      
      - record: job:slo_requests:rate5m
        expr: sum(rate(http_requests_total[5m])) by (job)
      
      - record: job:slo_error_budget:remaining
        expr: |
          (1 - job:slo_errors:rate5m) * 100
      
      - alert: ErrorBudgetBurnRateHigh
        expr: |
          job:slo_errors:rate5m > 0.01
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "High error budget burn rate for {{ $labels.job }}"
          description: "Error rate {{ $value }} exceeds 1% threshold"
      
      - alert: APILatencyHigh
        expr: |
          histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(http_request_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > 0.3
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity: warning
        annotations:
          summary: "High API latency for {{ $labels.job }}"
          description: "P95 latency {{ $value }}s exceeds 300ms threshold"
      
      - alert: LLMLatencyHigh
        expr: |
          histogram_quantile(0.95, rate(llm_request_duration_seconds_bucket[5m])) > 8
        for: 5m
        labels:
          severity

### [Sessão Paralela: PM]
Vou definir os KPIs de sofisticação e UX Premium para a V11.

**Problema identificado:** Como medir se a V11 realmente entregou uma experiência premium e sofisticada além da funcionalidade básica?

**Público-alvo:** Usuários avançados que já dominam o DIYAPP e buscam eficiência profissional.

**Resultado esperado:** 3 KPIs mensuráveis que capturem "sofisticação" (eficiência, precisão) e "UX Premium" (satisfação, fluidez).

**Critérios de aceite:**
1. Cada KPI deve ser quantificável (número ou porcentagem)
2. Deve ter linha de base da V10 para comparação
3. Deve direcionar features específicas no backlog

**KPIs propostos:**

1. **Task Completion Speed** (Sofisticação)
   - Métrica: Tempo médio para concluir tarefa complexa (ex: criar workflow de 5 passos)
   - Baseline V10: [medir com usuários-teste]
   - Meta V11: Redução de 40%
   - Direciona: Atalhos de teclado, templates inteligentes, autocomplete

2. **Error Recovery Rate** (UX Premium)  
   - Métrica: % de erros que usuário consegue corrigir sem consultar documentação
   - Baseline V10: [medir em sessões de teste]
   - Meta V11: Aumentar para 85%
   - Direciona: Mensagens de erro claras, undo/redo robusto, assistente contextual

3. **Flow State Score** (Sofisticação + Premium)
   - Métrica: NPS segmentado apenas para tarefas > 10 minutos
   - Baseline V10: NPS geral atual
   - Meta V11: NPS ≥ 60 para tarefas longas
   - Direciona: Interface não intrusiva, progresso visível, redução de interrupções

**Priorização backlog V11 (baseado nos KPIs):**
1. Sistema de undo/redo ilimitado (afeta Error Recovery Rate)
2. Atalhos de teclado personalizáveis (afeta Task Completion Speed)  
3. Modo foco que esconde UI não essencial (afeta Flow State Score)
4. Preview em tempo real de alterações (afeta todos os KPIs)

Vou passar essa análise para a equipe técnica implementar o sistema de coleta dessas métricas.

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Design

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com tokens, componentes e wireframes de alta fidelidade para os 3 fluxos principais, seguindo os princípios de UX baseado em evidências.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-design-system/
├── index.html                    # Dashboard principal do Design System
├── design-tokens.json           # Tokens de design em formato JSON
├── style-guide.html             # Guia de estilo visual
├── components/                  # Componentes do Design System
│   ├── buttons.html
│   ├── forms.html
│   ├── navigation.html
│   └── feedback.html
├── wireframes/                  # Wireframes de alta fidelidade
│   ├── dashboard.html
│   ├── project-creation.html
│   └── collaboration.html
├── prototypes/                  # Protótipos navegáveis
│   ├── dashboard-prototype.html
│   ├── project-creation-prototype.html
│   └── collaboration-prototype.html
├── css/
│   ├── design-tokens.css        # Tokens CSS custom properties
│   ├── components.css           # Estilos dos componentes
│   └── wireframes.css           # Estilos específicos dos wireframes
└── js/
    ├── design-system.js         # Lógica do Design System
    └── prototypes.js            # Interatividade dos protótipos
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```javascript
// DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Technical Architecture Specification
// Arquitetura: Tech Lead Senior Squad
// Data: 2024-01-15
// Status: Aceita

// ============================================================================
// ARQUITETURA V11 - DECISÕES TÉCNICAS
// ============================================================================

// ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microfrontends com BFF (Backend for Frontend)
// ADR-002: Stack de Monitoramento e Observabilidade
// ADR-003: Padrões de Código e Qualidade
// ADR-004: Plano de Migração V10 → V11

// ============================================================================
// 1. DECISÃO DE ARQUITETURA - ADR-001
// ============================================================================

/**
 * Architecture Decision Record - ADR-001
 * Título: Adoção de Microfrontends com BFF Pattern
 * Data: 2024-01-15
 * Status: Aceita
 * Autores: Tech Lead, Especialista Infra, Especialista Frontend
 */

const ADR_001 = {
  contexto: {
    problema: "A V10 apresenta acoplamento forte entre frontend e backend, dificultando deploy independente e causando latência em operações complexas",
    forcas: [
      "Necessidade de deploy independente por squad",
      "Performance crítica em operações de dashboard",
      "Manutenibilidade do código frontend",
      "Escalabilidade horizontal"
    ]
  },
  
  decisao: "Implementar arquitetura de Microfrontends com BFF (Backend for Frontend) usando Module Federation do Webpack 5",
  
  opcoesConsideradas: [
    {
      nome: "Monolito com API REST tradicional",
      pros: ["Simplicidade inicial", "Menor complexidade operacional"],
      cons: ["Acoplamento forte", "Deploy bloqueante", "Escalabilidade limitada"],
      descartada: true
    },
    {
      nome: "Microfrontends puros (sem BFF)",
      pros: ["Desacoplamento completo", "Deploy independente"],
      cons: ["N+1 requests no frontend", "Segurança complexa", "Cache difícil"],
      descartada: true
    },
    {
      nome: "Microfrontends com BFF (ESCOLHIDA)",
      pros: [
        "Deploy independente por feature",
        "BFF otimiza requests para o frontend",
        "Segurança centralizada no BFF",
        "Cache por contexto de usuário"
      ],
      cons: ["Complexidade aumentada", "Necessidade de mais serviços"],
      justificativa: "Balanceia autonomia das squads com performance e segurança"
    }
  ],
  
  consequencias: {

      "Squads podem fazer deploy independentemente",
      "Performance otimizada via BFF aggregation",

// 2. CHECKLIST DE MIGRAÇÃO V10 → V11
// ============================================================================

class MigrationChecklist {
  constructor() {
    this.phases = {
      preparacao: [
        "✅ Documentar todas as APIs existentes na V10",
        "✅ Mapear dependências entre módulos",
        "✅ Identificar dados compartilhados entre features",
        "✅ Definir boundaries dos microfrontends",
        "✅ Setup do repositório monorepo com Lerna/Nx"
      ],
      
      infraestrutura: [
        "✅ Configurar Module Federation no Webpack 5",
        "✅ Implementar BFF base com Express.js",
        "✅ Setup do service mesh (Consul/Nomad)",
        "✅ Configurar API Gateway (Kong/Traefik)",
        "✅ Implementar service discovery"
      ],
      
      migracaoModulos: [
        "✅ Extrair módulo de Autenticação como microfrontend",
        "✅ Extrair módulo de Dashboard como microfrontend",
        "✅ Extrair módulo de Configurações como microfrontend",
        "✅ Implementar shared components library",
        "✅ Configurar build pipeline independente por MF"
      ],
      
      bffImplementation: [
        "✅ Implementar GraphQL layer no BFF",
        "✅ Configurar cache por usuário (Redis)",
        "✅ Implementar rate limiting por feature",
        "✅ Setup de circuit breaker para microservices",
        "✅ Configurar request aggregation"
      ],
      
      testesEMonitoramento: [
        "✅ Implementar contract testing (Pact)",
        "✅ Setup de e2e tests com Cypress",
        "✅ Configurar APM (DataDog/NewRelic)",
        "✅ Implementar distributed tracing",
        "✅ Setup de health checks"
      ],
      
      deploy: [
        "✅ Configurar blue-green deployment",
        "✅ Setup feature flags (LaunchDarkly)",
        "✅ Implementar canary releases",
        "✅ Configurar rollback automático",
        "✅ Documentar runbooks de emergência"
      ]
    };
  }
  
  getProgress() {
    const total = Object.values(this.phases).flat().length;
    const completed = Object.values(this.phases)
      .flat()
      .filter(item => item.startsWith('✅')).length;
    
    return {
      total,
      completed,
      percentage: Math.round((completed / total) * 100)
    };
  }
}

class MonitoringPlan {
  constructor() {
    this.apmStack = {
      primary: 'DataDog', // Alternativa: NewRelic
      fallback: 'Prometheus + Grafana',
      
      metrics: {
        application: [
          'response_time.p95',
          'error_rate',
          'throughput',
          'apdex_score',
          'memory_usage',
          'cpu_usage',
          'gc_pause_time'
        ],
        
        business: [
          'active_users',
          'conversion_rate',
          'feature_usage',
          'user_satisfaction'
        ],
        
        infrastructure: [
          'container_memory_usage',
          'pod_restarts',
          'node_cpu_utilization',
          'disk_io',
          'network_latency'
        ]
      },
      
      alerts: {
        severityLevels: {
          P0: { responseTime: '15min', channels: ['PagerDuty', 'Slack #critical'] },
          P1: { responseTime: '1h', channels: ['Slack #alerts', 'Email'] },
          P2: { responseTime: '4h', channels: ['Slack #notifications'] },
          P3: { responseTime: '24h', channels: ['Dashboard'] }
        },
        
        conditions: {
          responseTime: 'p95 > 2s por mais de 5min',
          errorRate: '> 1% por mais de 10min',
          memoryLeak: 'memory growth > 10% por hora',
          downtime: 'health check failed 3x consecutivas'
        }
      }
    };
    
    this.loggingStrategy = {
      levels: {
        ERROR: 'Erros de sistema e exceções não tratadas',
        WARN: 'Comportamentos inesperados mas recuperáveis',
        INFO: 'Eventos de negócio significativos',
        DEBUG: 'Informações para troubleshooting',
        TRACE: 'Logs detalhados de execução'
      },
      
      structuredLogging: {
        format: 'JSON',
        requiredFields: [
          'timestamp',
          'level',
          'message',
          'service',
          'trace_id',
          'user_id',
          'correlation_id'
        ],
        
        sensitiveData: {
          masked: ['password', 'token', 'credit_card', 'ssn', 'api_key'],
          neverLogged: ['private_key', 'master_key']
        }
      },
      
      retention: {
        hotStorage: '7 dias (Elasticsearch)',
        warmStorage: '30 dias (S3)',
        coldStorage: '1 ano (Glacier)',
        compliance: '7 anos (archival)'
      }
    };
    
    this.distributedTracing = {
      implementation: 'OpenTelemetry',
      exporters: ['Jaeger', 'DataDog'],
      
      spans: {
        minimumDuration: '10ms',
        samplingRate: {
          production: '10%',
          staging: '50%',
          development: '100%'
        }
      },
      
      correlation: {
        headers: [
          'x-request-id',
          'x-correlation-id',
          'x-b3-traceid',
          'x-b3-spanid'
        ]
      }
    };
    
    this.slaSloSli = {
      availability: {
        sla: '99.95%',
        slo: '99.97%',
        sli: 'uptime_checks / total_checks'
      },
      
      latency: {
        sla: 'p95 < 2s',
        slo: 'p95 < 1.5s',
        sli: 'requests_below_threshold / total_requests'
      },
      
      errorRate: {
        sla: '< 0.5%',
        slo: '< 0.1%',
        sli: 'successful_requests / total_requests'
      }
    };
  }
  
  getDashboardConfig() {
    return {
      overview: [
        { title: 'System Health', metrics: ['error_rate', 'response_time.p95', 'throughput'] },
        { title: 'Resource Usage', metrics: ['cpu_usage', 'memory_usage', 'disk_io'] },
        { title: 'Business Metrics', metrics: ['active_users', 'conversion_rate'] }
      ],
      
      microfrontends: [
        { mf: 'auth', metrics: ['login_success_rate', 'auth_latency', 'token_validation_errors'] },
        { mf: 'dashboard', metrics: ['data_loading_time', 'chart_rendering_time', 'cache_hit_rate'] },
        { mf: 'settings', metrics: ['config_save_success', 'preference_update_latency'] }
      ],
      
      bff: [
        { endpoint: 'graphql', metrics: ['query_complexity', 'resolver_time', 'cache_efficiency'] },
        { endpoint: 'rest', metrics: ['endpoint_availability', 'aggregation_time'] }
      ]
    };
  }
}

export type Theme = keyof typeof themes;

// ============================================
// 2. HOOKS DO DESIGN SYSTEM
// ============================================

// src/design-system/hooks/useTheme.ts
import React from 'react';

type ThemeContextType = {
  theme: 'light' | 'dark';
  toggleTheme: () => void;
  setTheme: (theme: 'light' | 'dark') => void;
};

const ThemeContext = React.createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export const useTheme = (): ThemeContextType => {
  const context = React.useContext(ThemeContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useTheme must be used within a ThemeProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

export const ThemeProvider: React.FC<{ children: React.ReactNode }> = ({ children }) => {
  const [theme, setTheme] = React.useState<'light' | 'dark'>(() => {
    // Verificar preferência do sistema ou localStorage
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('diyapp-theme');
    if (saved === 'light' || saved === 'dark') return saved;
    
    const prefersDark = window.matchMedia('(prefers-color-scheme: dark)').matches;
    return prefersDark ? 'dark' : 'light';
  });

  React.useEffect(() => {
    // Aplicar tema ao documento
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', theme);
    localStorage.setItem('diyapp-theme', theme);
  }, [theme]);

  const toggleTheme = () => {
    setTheme(prev => prev === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light');
  };

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={{ theme, toggleTheme, setTheme }}>
      {children}
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
};

// ============================================
// 3. COMPONENTES BASE
// ============================================

// src/design-system/components/Button/Button.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { colors, spacing, typography } from '../../tokens';
import { useTheme } from '../../hooks/useTheme';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

export interface ButtonProps extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

const Button: React.FC<ButtonProps> = ({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  disabled = false,
  leftIcon,
  rightIcon,
  fullWidth = false,
  className = '',
  onClick,
  type = 'button',
  ...props
}) => {
  const { theme } = useTheme();
  const isDark = theme === 'dark';
  
  const baseStyles = {
    display: 'inline-flex',
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    fontWeight: typography.fontWeight.semibold,
    fontFamily: typography.fontFamily.sans,
    borderRadius: '0.375rem',
    border: '1px solid transparent',
    cursor: disabled || isLoading ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
    transition: 'all 150ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
    outline: 'none',
    width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
    position: 'relative',
    overflow: 'hidden',
  };

  const sizeStyles = {
    sm: {
      fontSize: typography.fontSize.sm,
      padding: `${spacing[2]} ${spacing[3]}`,
      gap: spacing[2],
    },
    md: {
      fontSize: typography.fontSize.base,
      padding: `${spacing[3]} ${spacing[4]}`,
      gap: spacing[3],
    },
    lg: {
      fontSize: typography.fontSize.lg,
      padding: `${spacing[4]} ${spacing[6]}`,
      gap: spacing[4],
    },
  };

  const variantStyles = {
    primary: {
      backgroundColor: colors.primary[600],
      color: '#ffffff',
      borderColor: colors.primary[600],
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: colors.primary[700],
        borderColor: colors.primary[700],
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${colors.primary[100]}`,
      },
    },
    secondary: {
      backgroundColor: isDark ? colors.neutral[700] : colors.neutral[200],
      color: isDark ? colors.text.dark.primary : colors.text.light.primary,
      borderColor: isDark ? colors.neutral[600] : colors.neutral[300],
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? colors.neutral[600] : colors.neutral[300],
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${isDark ? colors.neutral[600] : colors.neutral[200]}`,
      },
    },
    outline: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: isDark ? colors.text.dark.primary : colors.text.light.primary,
      borderColor: isDark ? colors.neutral[600] : colors.neutral[300],
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? colors.neutral[800] : colors.neutral[100],
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${isDark ? colors.neutral[700] : colors.neutral[200]}`,
      },
    },
    ghost: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: isDark ? colors.text.dark.primary : colors.text.light.primary,
      borderColor: 'transparent',
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? colors.neutral[800] : colors.neutral[100],
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px ${isDark ? colors.neutral[700] : colors.neutral[200]}`,
      },
    },
    danger: {
      backgroundColor: colors.semantic.error,
      color: '#ffffff',
      borderColor: colors.semantic.error,
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: '#dc2626',
        borderColor: '#dc2626',
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        boxShadow: `0 0 0 3px #fecaca`,
      },
    },
  };

  const disabledStyles = {
    opacity: 0.5,
    cursor: 'not-allowed',
  };

  const handleClick = (e: React.MouseEvent<HTMLButtonElement>) => {
    if (!disabled && !isLoading && onClick) {
      onClick(e);
    }
  };

  const buttonStyles = {
    ...baseStyles,
    ...sizeStyles[size],
    ...variantStyles[variant],
    ...(disabled || isLoading ? disabledStyles : {}),
  };

  return (
    <button
      type={type}
      style={buttonStyles}
      className={`diyapp-button ${className}`}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      onClick={handleClick}
      aria-busy={isLoading}
      aria-disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      {...props}
    >
      {isLoading && (
        <span
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            left: 0,
            top: 0,
            right: 0,
            bottom: 0,
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
            justifyContent: 'center',
            backgroundColor: 'inherit',
          }}
          aria-hidden="true"
        >
          <span
            style={{
              width: '1em',
              height: '1em',
              border: '2px solid currentColor',
              borderTopColor: 'transparent',
              borderRadius: '50%',
              animation: 'spin 1s linear infinite',
            }}
          />
        </span>
      )}
      
      <span
        style={{
          display: 'inline-flex',
          alignItems: 'center',
          gap: sizeStyles[size].gap,
          opacity: isLoading ? 0 : 1,
        }}
      >
        {leftIcon && <span className="button-icon-left">{leftIcon}</span>}
        {children}
        {rightIcon && <span className="button-icon-right">{rightIcon}</span>}
      </span>
    </button>
  );
};

// src/design-system/components/Button/index.ts
export { Button };
export type { ButtonProps, ButtonVariant, ButtonSize };

// src/design-system/components/Button/Button.test.tsx
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import { Button } from './Button';

describe('Button', () => {
  it('renders with default props', () => {
    render(<Button>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('type', 'button');
  });

  it('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn();
    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click</Button>);
    fireEvent.click(screen.getByRole('button'));
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  it('shows loading state', () => {
    render(<Button isLoading>Loading</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
  });

  it('is accessible with keyboard', () => {
    render(<Button>Accessible</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: 'Enter', code: 'Enter' });
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: ' ', code: 'Space' });
    // Should trigger click on Enter/Space
  });
});
