### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# src/api/performance_middleware.py
"""
Middleware de performance e resiliência para APIs
Implementa cache estratégico, circuit breakers e retry policies
"""

import time
import json
import hashlib
from functools import wraps
from typing import Any, Callable, Optional, Dict, Tuple
import redis
from redis.exceptions import RedisError
import requests
from requests.exceptions import RequestException, Timeout
from tenacity import retry, stop_after_attempt, wait_exponential, retry_if_exception_type
from circuitbreaker import circuit
import logging

# Configuração de logging
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# Cliente Redis (singleton)
_redis_client = None

def get_redis_client() -> redis.Redis:
    """Obtém ou cria cliente Redis com configuração de pool de conexões"""
    global _redis_client
    if _redis_client is None:
        _redis_client = redis.Redis(
            host=os.getenv('REDIS_HOST', 'localhost'),
            port=int(os.getenv('REDIS_PORT', 6379)),
            password=os.getenv('REDIS_PASSWORD'),
            decode_responses=True,
            socket_connect_timeout=5,
            socket_timeout=5,
            retry_on_timeout=True,
            max_connections=50
        )
        # Testa conexão
        try:
            _redis_client.ping()
            logger.info("Redis conectado com sucesso")
        except RedisError as e:
            logger.error(f"Falha ao conectar com Redis: {e}")
            _redis_client = None
    return _redis_client

class CircuitBreakerConfig:
    """Configuração de Circuit Breaker"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        failure_threshold: int = 5,
        recovery_timeout: int = 30,
        expected_exception: tuple = (RequestException, Timeout, RedisError)
    ):
        self.failure_threshold = failure_threshold
        self.recovery_timeout = recovery_timeout
        self.expected_exception = expected_exception

class CacheConfig:
    """Configuração de cache"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        ttl: int = 300,  # 5 minutos default
        key_prefix: str = "api_cache",
        enabled: bool = True
    ):
        self.ttl = ttl
        self.key_prefix = key_prefix
        self.enabled = enabled

class RetryConfig:
    """Configuração de retry com backoff exponencial"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        max_attempts: int = 3,
        min_wait: float = 1.0,
        max_wait: float = 10.0,
        retry_on: tuple = (RequestException, Timeout)
    ):
        self.max_attempts = max_attempts
        self.min_wait = min_wait
        self.max_wait = max_wait
        self.retry_on = retry_on

def performance_monitor(endpoint_name: str):
    """
    Decorator para monitoramento de performance
    Registra latência P50/P95/P99 e error rate
    """
    def decorator(func):
        @wraps(func)
        async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            start_time = time.time()
            correlation_id = kwargs.get('correlation_id', 'unknown')
            
            try:
                result = await func(*args, **kwargs)
                duration = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000  # ms
                
                # Log de sucesso com métricas
                logger.info(json.dumps({
                    "level": "info",
                    "correlation_id": correlation_id,
                    "endpoint": endpoint_name,
                    "duration_ms": round(duration, 2),
                    "status": "success",
                    "latency_bucket": _get_latency_bucket(duration)
                }))
                
                # Métricas para monitoramento (seriam enviadas para Prometheus/StatsD)
                _record_metrics(endpoint_name, duration, "success")
                
                return result
                
            except Exception as e:
                duration = (time.time() - start_time) * 1000
                
                # Log de erro
                logger.error(json.dumps({
                    "level": "error",
                    "correlation_id": correlation_id,
                    "endpoint": endpoint_name,
                    "duration_ms": round(duration, 2),
                    "status": "error",
                    "error_type": type(e).__name__,
                    "error_message": str(e)
                }))
                
                # Métricas de erro
                _record_metrics(endpoint_name, duration, "error")
                
                # Re-lança exceção para tratamento superior
                raise
                
        return wrapper
    return decorator

def _get_latency_bucket(duration_ms: float) -> str:
    """Categoriza latência em buckets para análise P50/P95/P99"""
    if duration_ms < 100:
        return "p50"
    elif duration_ms < 200:
        return "p95"
    elif duration_ms < 1000:
        return "p99"
    else:
        return "slow"

def _record_metrics(endpoint: str, duration: float, status: str):
    """Registra métricas para monitoramento (simulação)"""
    # Em produção, enviaria para Prometheus/StatsD
    pass

def cached_endpoint(
    cache_config: CacheConfig = None,
    key_builder: Callable = None
):
    """
    Decorator para cache estratégico de endpoints
    """
    if cache_config is None:
        cache_config = CacheConfig()
    
    def decorator(func):
        @wraps(func)
        async def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            # Se cache desabilitado, executa direto
            if not cache_config.enabled:
                return await func(*args, **kwargs)
            
            # Constrói chave de cache
            if key_builder:
                cache_key = key_builder(*args, **kwargs)
            else:
                cache_key = _build_cache_key(func.__name__, kwargs)
            
            full_key = f"{cache_config.key_prefix}:{cache_key}"
            
            # Tenta obter do cache
            redis_client = get_redis_client()
            if redis_client:
                try:
                    cached_data = redis_client.get(full_key)
                    if cached_data:
                        logger.debug(f"Cache hit para {full_key}")
                        return json.loads(cached_data)
                except RedisError as e:
                    logger.warning(f"Erro ao acessar cache: {e}")
            
            # Se não tem cache, executa função
            result = await func(*args, **kwargs)
            
            # Armazena no cache (assíncrono para não bloquear resposta)
            if redis_client and result:
                try:
                    redis_client.setex(
                        full_key,
                        cache_config.ttl,
                        json.dumps(result, default=str)
                    )
                except RedisError as e:
                    logger.warning(f"Erro ao armazenar em cache: {e}")
            
            return result
            
        return wrapper
    return decorator

def _build_cache_key(func_name: str, kwargs: dict) -> str:
    """Constrói chave de cache única baseada nos parâmetros"""
    # Remove parâmetros que não devem afetar cache
    filtered_kwargs = {
        k: v for k, v in kwargs.items() 
        if k not in ['correlation_id', 'current_user']
    }
    
    # Cria hash dos parâmetros
    key_str = f"{func_name}:{json.dumps(filtered_kwargs, sort_keys=True, default=str)}"
    return hashlib.md5(key_str.encode()).hexdigest()

def resilient_external_call(
    retry_config: RetryConfig = None,
    circuit_config: CircuitBreakerConfig = None,
    timeout: float = 10.0
):
    """
    Decorator para chamadas externas com resiliência
    Implementa retry + circuit breaker + timeout
    """
    if retry_config is None:
        retry_config = RetryConfig()
    if circuit_config is None:
        circuit_config = CircuitBreakerConfig()
    
    def decorator(func):
        # Aplica circuit breaker
        @circuit(
            failure_threshold=circuit_config.failure_threshold,
            recovery_timeout=circuit_config.recovery_timeout,
            expected_exception=circuit_config.expected_exception
        )
        # Aplica retry com backoff exponencial
        @retry(
            stop=stop_after_attempt(retry_config.max_attempts),
            wait=wait_exponential(
                min=retry_config.min_wait,
                max=retry_config.max_wait
            ),
            retry=retry_if_exception_type(retry_config.retry_on)
        )
        @wraps(func)
        def wrapper(*args, **kwargs):
            # Configura timeout para requests
            if 'timeout' not in kwargs:
                kwargs['timeout'] = timeout
            
            return func(*args, **kwargs)
            
        return wrapper
    return decorator

# Exemplo de implementação em endpoints reais
# src/api/users.py
"""
Endpoints de usuários refatorados para performance
"""

from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify
from flask_jwt_extended import jwt_required, get_jwt_identity
import os

users_bp = Blueprint('users', __name__)

@users_bp.route('/api/v2/users/<int:user_id>', methods=['GET'])
@jwt_required()
@performance_monitor("GET /api/v2/users/{user_id}")
@cached_endpoint(
    cache_config=CacheConfig(ttl=60, key_prefix="user_profile"),
    key_builder=lambda user_id, **kwargs: f"user:{user_id}"
)
async def get_user_profile(user_id: int):
    """
    Obtém perfil de usuário com cache estratégico
    ---
    tags:
      - Users
    parameters:
      - name: user_id
        in: path
        required: true
        schema:
          type: integer
    responses:
      200:
        description: Perfil do usuário
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/UserProfile'
      404:
        description: Usuário não encontrado
      429:
        description: Rate limit excedido
    """
    from src.services.user_service import UserService
    
    # Valida autorização
    current_user_id = get_jwt_identity()
    if current_user_id != user_id:
        return jsonify({"error": "Não autorizado"}), 403
    
    # Obtém dados com fallback para cache
    try:
        user_service = UserService()
        profile = await user_service.get_profile(user_id)
        
        if not profile:
            return jsonify({"error": "Usuário não encontrado"}), 404
            
        return jsonify(profile), 200
        
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Erro ao obter perfil: {e}")
        return jsonify({"error": "Erro interno do servidor"}), 500

@users_bp.route('/api/v2/users/search', methods=['GET'])
@jwt_required()
@performance_monitor("GET /api/v2/users/search")
async def search_users():
    """
    Busca usuários com paginação e cache
    ---
    tags:
      - Users
    parameters:
      - name: q
        in: query
        required: false
        schema:
          type: string
      - name: page
        in: query
        required: false
        schema:
          type: integer
          default: 1
      - name: limit
        in: query
        required: false
        schema:
          type: integer
          default: 20
          maximum: 100
    responses:
      200:
        description: Lista de usuários
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              type: object
              properties:
                data:
                  type: array
                  items:
                    $ref: '#/components/schemas/User'
                pagination:
                  $ref: '#/components/schemas/Pagination'
    """
    from src.services.user_service import UserService
    
    try:
        # Parâmetros com valores default
        query = request.args.get('q', '')
        page = int(request.args.get('page', 1))
        limit = min(int(request.args.get('limit', 20)), 100)  # Max 100
        
        # Cache específico para busca
        cache_key = f"search:{hashlib.md5(f'{query}:{page}:{limit}'.encode()).hexdigest()}"
        
        redis_client = get_redis_client()
        if redis_client:
            cached = redis_client.get(f"user_search:{cache_key}")
            if cached:
                return jsonify(json.loads(cached)), 200
        
        # Executa busca
        user_service = UserService()
        results, total = await user_service.search_users(
            query=query,
            page=page,
            limit=limit
        )
        
        response = {
            "data": results,
            "pagination": {
                "page": page,
                "limit": limit,
                "total": total,
                "pages": (total + limit - 1) // limit
            }
        }
        
        # Armazena em cache (TTL menor para buscas)
        if redis_client and results:
            redis_client.setex(
                f"user_search:{cache_key}",
                30,  # 30 segundos
                json.dumps(response, default=str)
            )
        
        return jsonify(response), 200
        
    except ValueError as e:
        return jsonify({"error": "Parâmetros inválidos"}), 400
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Erro na busca: {e}")
        return jsonify({"error": "Erro interno"}), 500

# src/services/user_service.py
"""
Service layer com chamadas externas resilientes
"""

import aiohttp
from tenacity import AsyncRetrying, stop_after_attempt, wait_exponential

class UserService:
    """Service para operações com usuários"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.external_api_url = os.getenv('EXTERNAL_USER_API', 'https://api.example.com')
        self.session_timeout = aiohttp.ClientTimeout(total=5.0)
    
    @resilient_external_call(
        retry_config=RetryConfig(max_attempts=2, min_wait=0.5, max_wait=2.0),
        circuit_config=CircuitBreakerConfig(failure_threshold=3, recovery_timeout=60),
        timeout=3.0
    )
    async def _call_external_api(self, endpoint: str, params: dict = None):
        """
        Chamada resiliente para API externa
        """
        url = f"{self.external_api_url}/{endpoint}"
        
        async with aiohttp.ClientSession(timeout=self.session_timeout) as session:
            async with session.get(url, params=params) as response:
                response.raise_for_status()
                return await response.json()
    
    async def get_profile(self, user_id: int) -> Optional[dict]:
        """
        Obtém perfil do usuário com fallback para dados locais
        """
        try:
            # Tenta API externa primeiro
            data = await self._call_external_api(f"users/{user_id}")
            return self._transform_profile_data(data)
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.warning(f"API externa falhou, usando fallback: {e}")
            # Fallback para banco local
            return await self._get_local_profile(user_id)
    
    async def search_users(self, query: str, page: int, limit: int) -> Tuple[list, int]:
        """
        Busca usuários com estratégia de cache e fallback
        """
        from src.database import db
        from src.models.user import User
        
        try:
            # Tenta busca otimizada com índice
            search_query = f"%{query}%"
            
            # Query com paginação otimizada
            users_query = User.query.filter(
                User.is_active == True,
                User.name.ilike(search_query)
            ).order_by(User.created_at.desc())
            
            # Count total (pode ser caro, considerar cache)
            total = users_query.count()
            
            # Paginação
            users = users_query.offset((page - 1) * limit).limit(limit).all()
            
            # Transforma para dict
            results = [user.to_dict() for user in users]
            
            return results, total
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro na busca local: {e}")
            return [], 0
    
    async def _get_local_profile(self, user_id: int) -> Optional[dict]:
        """Fallback para obter perfil do banco local"""
        from src.database import db
        from src.models.user import User
        
        try:
            user = User.query.get(user_id)
            if user:
                return user.to_dict()
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Erro ao obter perfil local: {e}")
        
        return None
    
    def _transform_profile_data(self, data: dict) -> dict:
        """Transforma dados da API externa para formato interno"""
        return {
            "id": data.get("id"),
            "name": data.get("name"),
            "email": data.get("email"),
            "avatar": data.get("avatar_url"),
            "created_at": data.get("created_at")
        }

from flask import Blueprint, request, jsonify

async def get_products():
    """

    tags:
      - Products
    parameters:
      - name: category
        in: query
        required: false
        schema:
          type: string
      - name: min_price

      - name: max_price
        in: query

          type: number

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core Architecture
# Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11 com Observabilidade
# Tech Lead: Arquitetura de Sistema e Padrões Técnicos

"""
ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11
Data: 2024-01-15
Status: Aceita
Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra + Especialista Backend

CONTEXTO:
A V10 do DIYAPP atingiu limites de escalabilidade devido à arquitetura monolítica.
Precisamos evoluir para microsserviços mantendo 100% de autonomia da squad.
O sistema deve suportar 10x crescimento de usuários com zero downtime.

DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços baseada em domínios (DDD) com:
- 6 serviços independentes com banco de dados próprio
- Comunicação via eventos (Kafka) para consistência eventual
- API Gateway para roteamento e rate limiting
- Service Mesh (Istio) para comunicação service-to-service
- Observabilidade completa com OpenTelemetry

OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- Opção A: Monólito modularizado - Prós: Simples, baixa latência. Contras: Escala vertical limitada
- Opção B: Microsserviços completos - Prós: Escala independente, resiliência. Contras: Complexidade operacional
- Opção C: Serverless (Lambda) - Prós: Escala automática, custo variável. Contras: Vendor lock-in, cold starts

Opção escolhida: B - Justificativa: Alinhamento com crescimento projetado, autonomia por squad

CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
Positivas: Escala horizontal ilimitada, deploy independente, resiliência por serviço
Negativas: Complexidade distribuída, necessidade de observabilidade robusta
Riscos: Latência em chamadas cross-service, consistência de dados distribuídos

REVISÃO: 2024-04-15 (3 meses para avaliar métricas de performance)
"""

# ============================================================================
# ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO V11
# ============================================================================

"""
diyapp-v11/
├── .github/
│   ├── workflows/
│   │   ├── ci.yml          # Pipeline CI/CD
│   │   └── security-scan.yml
│   └── PULL_REQUEST_TEMPLATE.md
├── docs/
│   ├── architecture/
│   │   ├── ADR-001-microsservices.md
│   │   ├── ADR-002-observability.md
│   │   └── service-mesh.md
│   └── api/
│       └── openapi/
├── infrastructure/
│   ├── terraform/          # IaC para todos os ambientes
│   ├── kubernetes/
│   │   ├── base/
│   │   ├── overlays/
│   │   └── helm-charts/
│   └── monitoring/
│       ├── prometheus/
│       └── grafana/
├── libs/                   # Bibliotecas compartilhadas
│   ├── common/
│   ├── telemetry/
│   └── messaging/
└── services/              # Microsserviços
    ├── api-gateway/
    ├── auth-service/
    ├── user-service/
    ├── project-service/
    ├── billing-service/
    ├── notification-service/
    └── analytics-service/
"""

# ============================================================================
# ENGINEERING STANDARDS - V11
# ============================================================================

# diyapp-v11/docs/engineering-standards.md
engineering_standards = """
# Engineering Standards - DIYAPP V11

## 1. Padrões de Código

### 1.1 Linguagens Principais
- Backend: Python 3.11+ (FastAPI), TypeScript/Node.js 18+ (NestJS)
- Frontend: React 18+ com TypeScript
- Mobile: React Native 0.72+

### 1.2 Guia de Estilo
```python
# Python - FastAPI
from typing import Optional, List
from pydantic import BaseModel, Field
from datetime import datetime

class UserCreate(BaseModel):
    """Schema para criação de usuário"""
    email: str = Field(..., min_length=5, max_length=255)
    name: str = Field(..., min_length=2, max_length=100)
    is_active: bool = Field(default=True)
    
    class Config:
        schema_extra = {
            "example": {
                "email": "user@example.com",
                "name": "John Doe",
                "is_active": True
            }
        }

# TypeScript - NestJS
export class CreateUserDto {
  @IsEmail()
  @MaxLength(255)
  email: string;

  @IsString()
  @MinLength(2)
  @MaxLength(100)
  name: string;

  @IsBoolean()
  @IsOptional()
  isActive?: boolean = true;
}
```

### 1.3 Convenções de Nomenclatura
- Services: `kebab-case` (user-service, auth-service)
- Classes: `PascalCase` (UserService, AuthenticationHandler)
- Métodos/Funções: `camelCase` (getUserById, validateToken)
- Variáveis: `camelCase` (userCount, isAuthenticated)
- Constantes: `SCREAMING_SNAKE_CASE` (MAX_RETRY_COUNT, API_TIMEOUT_MS)
- Arquivos: `kebab-case` (user-controller.ts, auth-middleware.py)

## 2. Padrões de API

### 2.1 RESTful Design
```
GET    /v1/users          # Listar usuários
GET    /v1/users/{id}     # Buscar usuário específico
POST   /v1/users          # Criar usuário
PUT    /v1/users/{id}     # Atualizar usuário completo
PATCH  /v1/users/{id}     # Atualizar parcialmente
DELETE /v1/users/{id}     # Remover usuário
```

### 2.2 Versionamento
- URL Path Versioning: `/v1/`, `/v2/`
- Header Versioning: `Accept: application/vnd.diyapp.v1+json`
- Sempre manter backward compatibility por 6 meses

### 2.3 Response Format
```json
{
  "data": {
    "id": "123",
    "type": "user",
    "attributes": {
      "email": "user@example.com",
      "name": "John Doe"
    }
  },
  "meta": {
    "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
    "version": "v1"
  },
  "links": {
    "self": "/v1/users/123"
  }
}
```

## 3. Padrões de Banco de Dados

### 3.1 Por Serviço
- Cada serviço tem seu próprio banco de dados
- Nenhum acesso direto entre bancos de serviços diferentes
- Comunicação via eventos para consistência

### 3.2 Migrações
- Usar Alembic (Python) ou TypeORM migrations (TypeScript)
- Todas as migrações devem ser reversíveis
- Testar migração/rollback em staging antes de produção

## 4. Padrões de Mensageria

### 3.1 Event Schema
```json
{
  "event_id": "evt_123456789",
  "event_type": "user.created",
  "event_version": "1.0",
  "timestamp": "2024-01-15T10:30:00Z",
  "producer": "user-service",
  "data": {
    "user_id": "usr_123",
    "email": "user@example.com"
  },
  "metadata": {
    "correlation_id": "corr_987654321",
    "trace_id": "trace_123456789"
  }
}
```

## 5. Observabilidade

### 5.1 Logs Estruturados
```python
# Python - usando structlog
import structlog

logger = structlog.get_logger()

def create_user(user_data: dict):
    logger.info(
        "user.creation.started",
        user_email=user_data["email"],
        source_ip=request.client.host,
        correlation_id=get_correlation_id()
    )
    
    try:
        user = User.create(**user_data)
        logger.info(
            "user.creation.success",
            user_id=user.id,
            duration_ms=get_elapsed_time()
        )
        return user
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(
            "user.creation.failed",
            error=str(e),
            stack_trace=traceback.format_exc()
        )
        raise
```

### 5.2 Métricas
- Latência por endpoint (p50, p95, p99)
- Taxa de erro por serviço
- Throughput (requests/segundo)
- Uso de recursos (CPU, memória, disco)

### 5.3 Tracing
- Usar OpenTelemetry para tracing distribuído
- Propagação de trace_id entre serviços
- Sampling rate: 100% em dev, 10% em produção
"""

# ============================================================================
# IMPLEMENTAÇÃO: MÓDULO DE OBSERVABILIDADE
# ============================================================================

# diyapp-v11/libs/telemetry/__init__.py
"""
Módulo de Telemetria Centralizado - OpenTelemetry
"""

import os
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
import logging

from opentelemetry import trace
from opentelemetry.sdk.trace import TracerProvider
from opentelemetry.sdk.trace.export import BatchSpanProcessor
from opentelemetry.sdk.resources import Resource
from opentelemetry.exporter.otlp.proto.grpc.trace_exporter import OTLPSpanExporter
from opentelemetry.instrumentation.fastapi import FastAPIInstrumentor
from opentelemetry.instrumentation.requests import RequestsInstrumentor
from opentelemetry.instrumentation.sqlalchemy import SQLAlchemyInstrumentor

import structlog
from structlog.processors import JSONRenderer, TimeStamper
from structlog.stdlib import BoundLogger, get_logger

# Configuração do recurso OpenTelemetry
resource = Resource.create({
    "service.name": os.getenv("OTEL_SERVICE_NAME", "unknown-service"),
    "service.version": os.getenv("APP_VERSION", "1.0.0"),
    "deployment.environment": os.getenv("ENVIRONMENT", "development"),
    "squad.name": "diyapp-v11-core"
})

class TelemetryConfig:
    """Configuração centralizada de telemetria"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.otel_endpoint = os.getenv("OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT", "http://localhost:4317")
        self.enable_tracing = os.getenv("ENABLE_TRACING", "true").lower() == "true"
        self.enable_metrics = os.getenv("ENABLE_METRICS", "true").lower() == "true"
        self.sampling_rate = float(os.getenv("TRACE_SAMPLING_RATE", "0.1"))
        
    def is_production(self) -> bool:
        return os.getenv("ENVIRONMENT", "development") == "production"

class TelemetryManager:
    """Gerenciador central de observabilidade"""
    
    _instance = None
    
    def __new__(cls):
        if cls._instance is None:
            cls._instance = super().__new__(cls)
            cls._instance._initialized = False
        return cls._instance
    
    def __init__(self):
        if self._initialized:
            return
            
        self.config = TelemetryConfig()
        self.tracer_provider = None
        self.meter_provider = None
        self._initialized = True
        
    def setup_tracing(self, service_name: str):
        """Configura tracing distribuído com OpenTelemetry"""
        if not self.config.enable_tracing:
            return
            
        # Configurar provedor de traces
        self.tracer_provider = TracerProvider(
            resource=resource,
            sampler=self._get_sampler()
        )
        
        # Configurar exportador OTLP
        otlp_exporter = OTLPSpanExporter(
            endpoint=self.config.otel_endpoint,
            insecure=not self.config.is_production()
        )
        
        # Adicionar processador de spans
        span_processor = BatchSpanProcessor(otlp_exporter)
        self.tracer_provider.add_span_processor(span_processor)
        
        # Configurar como provedor global
        trace.set_tracer_provider(self.tracer_provider)
        
        # Instrumentar bibliotecas
        FastAPIInstrumentor().instrument(tracer_provider=self.tracer_provider)
        RequestsInstrumentor().instrument()
        
        return self.tracer_provider
    
    def setup_logging(self):
        """Configura logging estruturado com structlog"""
        # Configurar structlog
        structlog.configure(
            processors=[
                structlog.stdlib.filter_by_level,
                structlog.stdlib.add_logger_name,
                structlog.stdlib.add_log_level,
                structlog.stdlib.PositionalArgumentsFormatter(),
                TimeStamper(fmt="iso"),
                structlog.processors.StackInfoRenderer(),
                structlog.processors.format_exc_info,
                structlog.processors.UnicodeDecoder(),
                JSONRenderer()
            ],
            context_class=dict,
            logger_factory=structlog.stdlib.LoggerFactory(),
            wrapper_class=structlog.stdlib.BoundLogger,
            cache_logger_on_first_use=True,
        )
        
        # Configurar logging padrão
        logging.basicConfig(
            format="%(message)s",
            level=logging.INFO,
            handlers=[logging.StreamHandler()]
        )
        
        return get_logger()
    
    def _get_sampler(self):
        """Retorna sampler baseado na taxa configurada"""
        from opentelemetry.sdk.trace.sampling import TraceIdRatioBased
        
        if self.config.is_production():
            return TraceIdRatioBased(self.config.sampling_rate)
        return TraceIdRatioBased(1.0)  # 100% sampling em dev
    
    def get_tracer(self, name: str):
        """Retorna tracer para o serviço"""
        if self.tracer_provider:
            return self.tracer_provider.get_tracer(name)
        return trace.get_tracer(name)
    
    @asynccontextmanager
    async def instrument_fastapi(self, app):
        """Context manager para instrumentar FastAPI"""
        if self.config.enable_tracing:
            FastAPIInstrumentor().instrument_app(app)
        
        yield
        
        if self.config.enable_tracing:
            FastAPIInstrumentor().uninstrument_app(app)

# ============================================================================
# IMPLEMENTAÇÃO: SERVICE TEMPLATE
# ============================================================================

# diyapp-v11/services/template-service/src/main.py
"""
Template de Serviço V11 - Padrão para todos os microsserviços
"""

from fastapi import FastAPI, Depends, HTTPException, Request
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.middleware.trustedhost import TrustedHostMiddleware
import uvicorn
from typing import List, Optional

from libs.telemetry import TelemetryManager, TelemetryConfig
from libs.messaging import EventProducer, EventConsumer
import structlog

# Configuração
config = TelemetryConfig()
telemetry = TelemetryManager()
logger = telemetry.setup_logging()

app = FastAPI(
    title="Template Service V11",
    description="Microsserviço template para DIYAPP V11",
    version="1.0.0",
    docs_url="/docs" if not config.is_production() else None,
    redoc_url="/redoc" if not config.is_production() else None,
)

# Middlewares
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=os.getenv("ALLOWED_ORIGINS", "*").split(","),
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

app.add_middleware(
    TrustedHostMiddleware,
    allowed_hosts=os.getenv("ALLOWED_HOSTS", "*").split(",")
)

# Dependências
async def get_logger(request: Request) -> structlog.BoundLogger:
    """Injeta logger com contexto de requisição"""
    correlation_id = request.headers.get("X-Correlation-ID", "unknown")
    return logger.bind(correlation_id=correlation_id)

async def get_tracer():
    """Injeta tracer OpenTelemetry"""
    return telemetry.get_tracer("template-service")

# Health Check
@app.get("/health")
async def health_check(logger: structlog.BoundLogger = Depends(get_logger)):
    """Endpoint de health check com telemetria"""
    logger.info("health.check.requested")
    
    return {
        "status": "healthy",
        "service": "template-service",
        "version": "1.0.0",
        "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat()
    }

# Metrics Endpoint
@app.get("/metrics")
async def metrics():
    """Endpoint para Prometheus metrics"""
    # Em produção, usar prometheus-fastapi-instrumentator
    from prometheus_client import generate_latest, CONTENT_TYPE_LATEST
    
    return Response(
        content=generate_latest(),
        media_type=CONTENT_TYPE_LATEST
    )

# Event Handlers
class TemplateEventHandler:
    """Handler para eventos do serviço"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.producer = EventProducer()
        self.consumer = EventConsumer(
            group_id="template-service-group",
            topics=["user.created", "user.updated"]
        )
    
    async def handle_user_created(self, event: dict):
        """Processa evento de usuário criado"""
        with telemetry.get_tracer("template-service").start_as_current_span(
            "handle_user_created"
        ) as span:
            span.set_attribute("user.id", event["data"]["user_id"])
            
            logger.info(
                "event.user.created.received",
                user_id=event["data"]["user_id"],
                event_id=event["event_id"]
            )
            
            # Lógica de negócio aqui
            # ...
            
            logger.info("event.user.created.process

## 1. Design Tokens (design-tokens.js)

```javascript
// design-tokens.js
class DesignTokens {
  static colors = {
    // Primary Palette
    primary: {
      50: '#f0f9ff',
      100: '#e0f2fe',
      200: '#bae6fd',
      300: '#7dd3fc',
      400: '#38bdf8',
      500: '#0ea5e9',
      600: '#0284c7',
      700: '#0369a1',
      800: '#075985',
      900: '#0c4a6e',
    },
    
    // Secondary Palette
    secondary: {
      50: '#fdf4ff',
      100: '#fae8ff',
      200: '#f5d0fe',
      300: '#f0abfc',
      400: '#e879f9',
      500: '#d946ef',
      600: '#c026d3',
      700: '#a21caf',
      800: '#86198f',
      900: '#701a75',
    },
    
    // Neutral Palette
    neutral: {
      0: '#ffffff',
      50: '#f8fafc',
      100: '#f1f5f9',
      200: '#e2e8f0',
      300: '#cbd5e1',
      400: '#94a3b8',
      500: '#64748b',
      600: '#475569',
      700: '#334155',
      800: '#1e293b',
      900: '#0f172a',
      950: '#020617',
    },
    
    // Semantic Colors
    semantic: {
      success: {
        50: '#f0fdf4',
        500: '#10b981',
        700: '#047857',
      },
      warning: {
        50: '#fffbeb',
        500: '#f59e0b',
        700: '#b45309',
      },
      error: {
        50: '#fef2f2',
        500: '#ef4444',
        700: '#b91c1c',
      },
      info: {
        50: '#eff6ff',
        500: '#3b82f6',
        700: '#1d4ed8',
      },
    },
  };

  static typography = {
    fontFamily: {
      sans: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
      mono: "'JetBrains Mono', 'Courier New', monospace",
    },
    
    fontSize: {
      xs: '0.75rem',    // 12px
      sm: '0.875rem',   // 14px
      base: '1rem',     // 16px
      lg: '1.125rem',   // 18px
      xl: '1.25rem',    // 20px
      '2xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
      '3xl': '1.875rem', // 30px
      '4xl': '2.25rem',  // 36px
      '5xl': '3rem',     // 48px
    },
    
    fontWeight: {
      normal: '400',
      medium: '500',
      semibold: '600',
      bold: '700',
    },
    
    lineHeight: {
      tight: '1.25',
      normal: '1.5',
      relaxed: '1.75',
    },
  };

  static spacing = {
    0: '0',
    1: '0.25rem',   // 4px
    2: '0.5rem',    // 8px
    3: '0.75rem',   // 12px
    4: '1rem',      // 16px
    5: '1.25rem',   // 20px
    6: '1.5rem',    // 24px
    8: '2rem',      // 32px
    10: '2.5rem',   // 40px
    12: '3rem',     // 48px
    16: '4rem',     // 64px
    20: '5rem',     // 80px
  };

  static borderRadius = {
    none: '0',
    sm: '0.125rem',   // 2px
    base: '0.25rem',  // 4px
    md: '0.375rem',   // 6px
    lg: '0.5rem',     // 8px
    xl: '0.75rem',    // 12px
    '2xl': '1rem',    // 16px
    '3xl': '1.5rem',  // 24px
    full: '9999px',
  };

  static shadows = {
    sm: '0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
    base: '0 1px 3px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 1px 2px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 2px 4px -2px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 4px 6px -4px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    xl: '0 20px 25px -5px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1), 0 8px 10px -6px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1)',
    '2xl': '0 25px 50px -12px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.25)',
    inner: 'inset 0 2px 4px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05)',
  };

  static zIndex = {
    hide: -1,
    base: 0,
    docked: 10,
    dropdown: 1000,
    sticky: 1100,
    banner: 1200,
    overlay: 1300,
    modal: 1400,
    popover: 1500,
    toast: 1700,
    tooltip: 1800,
  };

  static breakpoints = {
    sm: '640px',
    md: '768px',
    lg: '1024px',
    xl: '1280px',
    '2xl': '1536px',
  };

  static transitions = {
    duration: {
      fast: '150ms',
      normal: '300ms',
      slow: '500ms',
    },
    easing: {
      linear: 'linear',
      ease: 'ease',
      'ease-in': 'ease-in',
      'ease-out': 'ease-out',
      'ease-in-out': 'ease-in-out',
    },
  };

  // WCAG AA Compliant color combinations
  static accessibility = {
    textContrast: {
      primary: {
        onPrimary50: DesignTokens.colors.neutral[900],
        onPrimary500: DesignTokens.colors.neutral[0],
        onPrimary900: DesignTokens.colors.neutral[0],
      },
      neutral: {
        onNeutral0: DesignTokens.colors.neutral[900],
        onNeutral100: DesignTokens.colors.neutral[900],
        onNeutral500: DesignTokens.colors.neutral[0],
        onNeutral900: DesignTokens.colors.neutral[0],
      },
    },
  };

  static getTokenValue(path) {
    const parts = path.split('.');
    let value = this;
    
    for (const part of parts) {
      if (value[part] === undefined) {
        console.warn(`Token not found: ${path}`);
        return null;
      }
      value = value[part];
    }
    
    return value;
  }

  static applyToCSS() {
    const root = document.documentElement;
    
    // Apply color tokens
    Object.entries(this.colors).forEach(([category, shades]) => {
      Object.entries(shades).forEach(([shade, value]) => {
        root.style.setProperty(`--color-${category}-${shade}`, value);
      });
    });
    
    // Apply typography tokens
    Object.entries(this.typography.fontSize).forEach(([size, value]) => {
      root.style.setProperty(`--font-size-${size}`, value);
    });
    
    // Apply spacing tokens
    Object.entries(this.spacing).forEach(([size, value]) => {
      root.style.setProperty(`--spacing-${size}`, value);
    });
    
    // Apply other tokens
    root.style.setProperty('--font-family-sans', this.typography.fontFamily.sans);
    root.style.setProperty('--font-family-mono', this.typography.fontFamily.mono);
  }
}

// Export for use in components
if (typeof module !== 'undefined' && module.exports) {
  module.exports = DesignTokens;
}
```

## 2. Componente Button (components/Button.js)

```javascript
// components/Button.js
class Button extends HTMLElement {
  static observedAttributes = ['variant', 'size', 'state', 'loading', 'disabled'];
  
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.attachShadow({ mode: 'open' });
    this.render();
  }
  
  connectedCallback() {
    this.setupEventListeners();
  }
  
  attributeChangedCallback(name, oldValue, newValue) {
    if (oldValue !== newValue) {
      this.render();
      this.setupEventListeners();
    }
  }
  
  get variant() {
    return this.getAttribute('variant') || 'primary';
  }
  
  get size() {
    return this.getAttribute('size') || 'medium';
  }
  
  get state() {
    return this.getAttribute('state') || 'default';
  }
  
  get loading() {
    return this.hasAttribute('loading');
  }
  
  get disabled() {
    return this.hasAttribute('disabled');
  }
  
  get styles() {
    const variants = {
      primary: `
        background-color: var(--color-primary-600);
        color: var(--color-neutral-0);
        border: 1px solid var(--color-primary-600);
      `,
      secondary: `
        background-color: var(--color-secondary-600);
        color: var(--color-neutral-0);
        border: 1px solid var(--color-secondary-600);
      `,
      outline: `
        background-color: transparent;
        color: var(--color-primary-600);
        border: 1px solid var(--color-primary-600);
      `,
      ghost: `
        background-color: transparent;
        color: var(--color-neutral-700);
        border: 1px solid transparent;
      `,
      danger: `
        background-color: var(--color-semantic-error-500);
        color: var(--color-neutral-0);
        border: 1px solid var(--color-semantic-error-500);
      `,
    };
    
    const sizes = {
      small: `
        padding: var(--spacing-2) var(--spacing-3);
        font-size: var(--font-size-sm);
        height: 32px;
      `,
      medium: `
        padding: var(--spacing-2) var(--spacing-4);
        font-size: var(--font-size-base);
        height: 40px;
      `,
      large: `
        padding: var(--spacing-3) var(--spacing-6);
        font-size: var(--font-size-lg);
        height: 48px;
      `,
    };
    
    const states = {
      default: `
        &:hover:not(:disabled):not([loading]) {
          transform: translateY(-1px);
          box-shadow: var(--shadow-md);
        }
        &:active:not(:disabled):not([loading]) {
          transform: translateY(0);
        }
      `,
      disabled: `
        opacity: 0.5;
        cursor: not-allowed;
      `,
      loading: `
        cursor: wait;
        position: relative;
        color: transparent;
      `,
    };
    
    return `
      ${variants[this.variant] || variants.primary}
      ${sizes[this.size] || sizes.medium}
      ${states[this.disabled ? 'disabled' : this.loading ? 'loading' : this.state]}
    `;
  }
  
  render() {
    const loadingSpinner = this.loading ? `
      <div class="loading-spinner">
        <svg width="20" height="20" viewBox="0 0 20 20" fill="none">
          <circle cx="10" cy="10" r="8" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-opacity="0.3"/>
          <path d="M10 2a8 8 0 0 1 8 8" stroke="currentColor" stroke-width="2" stroke-linecap="round"/>
        </svg>
      </div>
    ` : '';
    
    this.shadowRoot.innerHTML = `
      <style>
        :host {
          display: inline-block;
        }
        
        button {
          all: unset;
          display: inline-flex;
          align-items: center;
          justify-content: center;
          gap: var(--spacing-2);
          border-radius: var(--border-radius-md);
          font-family: var(--font-family-sans);
          font-weight: var(--font-weight-medium);
          line-height: var(--line-height-normal);
          cursor: pointer;
          transition: all var(--transition-duration-normal) var(--transition-ease-out);
          user-select: none;
          ${this.styles}
        }
        
        button:focus-visible {
          outline: 2px solid var(--color-primary-500);
          outline-offset: 2px;
        }
        
        .loading-spinner {
          position: absolute;
          top: 50%;
          left: 50%;
          transform: translate(-50%, -50%);
          animation: spin 1s linear infinite;
        }
        
        .loading-spinner svg {
          color: currentColor;
        }
        
        @keyframes spin {
          from { transform: translate(-50%, -50%) rotate(0deg); }
          to { transform: translate(-50%, -50%) rotate(360deg); }
        }
        
        .icon {
          display: inline-flex;
          align-items: center;
          justify-content: center;
        }
        
        .icon:only-child {
          margin: 0;
        }
        
        ::slotted(svg) {
          width: 1.25em;
          height: 1.25em;
        }
      </style>
      
      <button 
        part="button"
        ?disabled="${this.disabled || this.loading}"
        aria-busy="${this.loading}"
        aria-disabled="${this.disabled}"
      >
        <slot name="prefix"></slot>
        <slot></slot>
        <slot name="suffix"></slot>
        ${loadingSpinner}
      </button>
    `;
  }
  
  setupEventListeners() {
    const button = this.shadowRoot.querySelector('button');
    if (button) {
      button.addEventListener('click', (e) => {
        if (this.disabled || this.loading) {
          e.preventDefault();
          e.stopPropagation();
        }
      });
    }
  }
}

customElements.define('ds-button', Button);
```

## 3. Componente Card (components/Card.js)

```javascript
// components/Card.js
class Card extends HTMLElement {
  static observedAttributes = ['variant', 'elevation', 'interactive'];
  
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.attachShadow({ mode: 'open' });
    this.render();
  }
  
  attributeChangedCallback() {
    this.render();
  }
  
  get variant() {
    return this.getAttribute('variant') || 'default';
  }
  
  get elevation() {
    return this.getAttribute('elevation') || 'base';
  }
  
  get interactive() {
    return this.hasAttribute('interactive');
  }
  
  get styles() {
    const elevations = {
      none: 'box-shadow: none;',
      base: `box-shadow: ${DesignTokens.shadows.base};`,
      md: `box-shadow: ${DesignTokens.shadows.md};`,
      lg: `box-shadow: ${DesignTokens.shadows.lg};`,
    };
    
    const variants = {
      default: `
        background-color: var(--color-neutral-0);
        border: 1px solid var(--color-neutral-200);
      `,
      elevated: `
        background-color: var(--color-neutral-0);
        border: none;
      `,
      subtle: `
        background-color: var(--color-neutral-50);
        border: 1px solid var(--color-neutral-100);
      `,
    };
    
    const interactiveStyle = this.interactive ? `
      cursor: pointer;
      transition: all var(--transition-duration-normal) var(--transition-ease-out);
      
      &:hover {
        transform: translateY(-2px);
        box-shadow: var(--shadow-lg);
      }
      
      &:active {
        transform: translateY(0);
      }
    ` : '';
    
    return `
      ${variants[this.variant] || variants.default}
      ${elevations[this.elevation] || elevations.base}
      ${interactiveStyle}
    `;
  }
  
  render() {
    this.shadowRoot.innerHTML = `
      <style>
        :host {
          display: block;
        }
        
        .card {
          border-radius: var(--border-radius-lg);
          padding

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]

```typescript
// src/App.tsx
import { Suspense } from 'react'
import { Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import Layout from '@components/Layout/Layout'
import LoadingSpinner from '@components/Feedback/LoadingSpinner'
import ErrorBoundary from '@components/Feedback/ErrorBoundary'

// Lazy load pages for code splitting
const Dashboard = React.lazy(() => import('@pages/Dashboard/Dashboard'))
const Projects = React.lazy(() => import('@pages/Projects/Projects'))
const ProjectDetail = React.lazy(() => import('@pages/Projects/ProjectDetail'))
const Settings = React.lazy(() => import('@pages/Settings/Settings'))
const NotFound = React.lazy(() => import('@pages/NotFound/NotFound'))

function App() {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <Layout>
        <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner fullScreen />}>
          <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
            <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path="/projects" element={<Projects />} />
            <Route path="/projects/:id" element={<ProjectDetail />} />
            <Route path="/settings" element={<Settings />} />
            <Route path="*" element={<NotFound />} />
          </Routes>
        </Suspense>
      </Layout>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  )
}

export default App
```

// src/components/Layout/Sidebar.tsx
import React from 'react'
import { NavLink } from 'react-router-dom'
import { 
  LayoutDashboard, 
  FolderKanban, 
  Settings, 
  FileText,
  Users,
  Calendar,
  BarChart3
} from 'lucide-react'
import { useSidebar } from '@hooks/useSidebar'
import clsx from 'clsx'

const navItems = [
  { path: '/dashboard', icon: LayoutDashboard, label: 'Dashboard' },
  { path: '/projects', icon: FolderKanban, label: 'Projects' },
  { path: '/documents', icon: FileText, label: 'Documents' },
  { path: '/team', icon: Users, label: 'Team' },
  { path: '/calendar', icon: Calendar, label: 'Calendar' },
  { path: '/analytics', icon: BarChart3, label: 'Analytics' },
  { path: '/settings', icon: Settings, label: 'Settings' },
]

const Sidebar: React.FC = () => {
  const { isCollapsed } = useSidebar()

  return (
    <aside
      className={clsx(
        'fixed top-16 bottom-0 left-0 bg-white border-r border-gray-200 transition-all duration-300 ease-in-out z-40',
        isCollapsed ? 'w-20' : 'w-64'
      )}
    >
      <nav className="p-4">
        <ul className="space-y-2">
          {navItems.map((item) => (
            <li key={item.path}>
              <NavLink
                to={item.path}
                className={({ isActive }) =>
                  clsx(
                    'flex items-center rounded-lg px-3 py-2.5 text-sm font-medium transition-colors',
                    isActive
                      ? 'bg-blue-50 text-blue-700'
                      : 'text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-100 hover:text-gray-900',
                    isCollapsed ? 'justify-center' : 'space-x-3'
                  )
                }
                end
              >
                <item.icon className="w-5 h-5 flex-shrink-0" />
                {!isCollapsed && <span>{item.label}</span>}
              </NavLink>
            </li>
          ))}
        </ul>
      </nav>
    </aside>
  )
}

export default Sidebar

```typescript
// src/components/UI/Button.tsx
import React from 'react'
import clsx from 'clsx'

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'ghost' | 'danger'
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'

interface ButtonProps extends React.ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant
  size?: ButtonSize
  loading?: boolean
  fullWidth?: boolean
}

const Button: React.FC<ButtonProps> = ({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  loading = false,
  fullWidth = false,
  className,
  disabled,
  ...props
}) => {
  const baseStyles = 'inline-flex items-center justify-center font-medium rounded-lg transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2 focus:ring-blue-500 disabled:opacity-50 disabled:cursor-not-allowed'
  
  const variants: Record<ButtonVariant, string> = {
    primary: 'bg-blue-600 text-white hover:bg-blue-700',
    secondary: 'bg-gray-200 text-gray-900 hover:bg-gray-300',
    ghost: 'bg-transparent text-gray-700 hover:bg-gray-100',
    danger: 'bg-red-600 text-white hover:bg-red-700'
  }
  
  const sizes: Record<ButtonSize, string> = {
    sm: 'px-3 py-1.5 text-sm',
    md: 'px-4 py-2 text-sm',
    lg: 'px-6 py-3 text-base'
  }

  return (
    <button
      className={clsx(
        baseStyles,
        variants[variant],
        sizes[size],
        fullWidth && 'w-full',
        className
      )}
      disabled={disabled || loading}
      aria-busy={loading}
      {...props}
    >
      {loading && (
        <svg className="animate-spin -ml-1 mr-2 h-4 w-4 text-current" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24">
          <circle className="opacity-25" cx="12" cy="12" r="10" stroke="currentColor" strokeWidth="4" />
          <path className="opacity-75" fill="currentColor" d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z" />
        </svg>
      )}
      {children}
    </button>
  )
}

export default Button
```

```typescript
// src/components/Feedback/LoadingSpinner.tsx
import React from 'react'
import clsx from 'clsx'

interface LoadingSpinnerProps {
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg'
  fullScreen?: boolean
  className?: string
}

const LoadingSpinner: React.FC<LoadingSpinnerProps> = ({
  size = 'md',
  fullScreen = false,
  className
}) => {
  const sizeClasses = {
    sm: 'w-4 h-4',
    md: 'w-8 h-8',
    lg: 'w-12 h-12'
  }

  const spinner = (
    <div className={clsx('flex items-center justify-center', className)}>
      <svg
        className={clsx('animate-spin text-blue-600', sizeClasses[size])}
        fill="none"
        viewBox="0 0 24 24"
        aria-label="Loading"
      >
        <circle
          className="opacity-25"
          cx="12"
          cy="12"
          r="10"
          stroke="currentColor"
          strokeWidth="4"
        />
        <path
          className="opacity-75"
          fill="currentColor"
          d="M4 12a8 8 0 018-8V0C5.373 0 0 5.373 0 12h4zm2 5.291A7.962 7.962 0 014 12H0c0 3.042 1.135 5.824 3 7.938l3-2.647z"
        />
      </svg>
    </div>
  )

  if (fullScreen) {
    return (
      <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-white bg-opacity-75 flex items-center justify-center z-50">
        {spinner}
      </div>
    )
  }

  return spinner
}

export default LoadingSpinner
```

```typescript
// src/components/Feedback/ErrorBoundary.tsx
import React, { Component, ErrorInfo, ReactNode } from 'react'
import Button from '@components/UI/Button'

interface Props {
  children: ReactNode
}

interface State {
  hasError: boolean
  error?: Error
}

class ErrorBoundary extends Component<Props, State> {
  public state: State = {
    hasError: false
  }

  public static getDerivedStateFromError(error: Error): State {
    return { hasError: true, error }
  }

  public componentDidCatch(error: Error, errorInfo: ErrorInfo) {
   

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```typescript
// src/server.ts - Ponto de entrada do servidor
import express from 'express';
import cors from 'cors';
import helmet from 'helmet';
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
import { config } from './config';
import { authRouter } from './routes/auth.routes';
import { usersRouter } from './routes/users.routes';
import { healthRouter } from './routes/health.routes';
import { errorHandler } from './middleware/error.middleware';
import { requestLogger } from './middleware/logger.middleware';
import { authenticateToken } from './middleware/auth.middleware';
import { connectDatabase, runMigrations } from './database';

class Server {
  private app: express.Application;
  private port: number;

  constructor() {
    this.app = express();
    this.port = config.server.port;

    this.initializeDatabase();
    this.initializeMiddlewares();
    this.initializeRoutes();
    this.initializeErrorHandling();
  }

  private async initializeDatabase(): Promise<void> {
    try {
      await connectDatabase();
      console.log('✅ Database connected successfully');
      
      await runMigrations();
      console.log('✅ Database migrations completed');
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('❌ Database initialization failed:', error);
      process.exit(1);
    }
  }

  private initializeMiddlewares(): void {
    // Security headers
    this.app.use(helmet());
    
    // CORS configuration
    this.app.use(cors({
      origin: config.server.corsOrigins,
      credentials: true,
    }));

    // Rate limiting for public endpoints
    const publicLimiter = rateLimit({
      windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
      max: 100, // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
      message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later',
      standardHeaders: true,
      legacyHeaders: false,
    });

    // Apply rate limiting to public routes
    this.app.use('/api/auth', publicLimiter);
    this.app.use('/api/health', publicLimiter);

    // Body parsing
    this.app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
    this.app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

    // Request logging with correlation ID
    this.app.use(requestLogger);
  }

  private initializeRoutes(): void {
    // Public routes
    this.app.use('/api/auth', authRouter);
    this.app.use('/api/health', healthRouter);

    // Protected routes (require authentication)
    this.app.use('/api/users', authenticateToken, usersRouter);

    // 404 handler for undefined routes
    this.app.use('*', (req: express.Request, res: express.Response) => {
      res.status(404).json({
        error: 'Not Found',
        message: `Route ${req.originalUrl} not found`,
        correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || 'unknown',
      });
    });
  }

  private initializeErrorHandling(): void {
    this.app.use(errorHandler);
  }

  public start(): void {
    this.app.listen(this.port, () => {
      console.log(`🚀 Server running on port ${this.port}`);
      console.log(`📊 Environment: ${config.environment}`);
      console.log(`🔗 Health check: http://localhost:${this.port}/api/health`);
    });
  }
}

// Start server
const server = new Server();
server.start();
```

```typescript
// src/config/index.ts - Configurações centralizadas
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import { z } from 'zod';

dotenv.config();

const configSchema = z.object({
  environment: z.enum(['development', 'staging', 'production']).default('development'),
  
  server: z.object({
    port: z.number().min(1).max(65535).default(3000),
    corsOrigins: z.array(z.string()).default(['http://localhost:3000']),
    jwtSecret: z.string().min(32),
    jwtExpiresIn: z.string().default('24h'),
    bcryptRounds: z.number().min(10).max(14).default(12),
  }),

  database: z.object({
    host: z.string(),
    port: z.number().default(5432),
    name: z.string(),
    user: z.string(),
    password: z.string(),
    ssl: z.boolean().default(false),
    pool: z.object({
      max: z.number().default(20),
      min: z.number().default(5),
      idleTimeout: z.number().default(30000),
    }),
  }),

  rateLimit: z.object({
    windowMs: z.number().default(900000), // 15 minutes
    maxRequests: z.number().default(100),
  }),
});

const rawConfig = {
  environment: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  
  server: {
    port: parseInt(process.env.PORT || '3000'),
    corsOrigins: (process.env.CORS_ORIGINS || 'http://localhost:3000').split(','),
    jwtSecret: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-super-secret-jwt-key-min-32-chars-long',
    jwtExpiresIn: process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h',
    bcryptRounds: parseInt(process.env.BCRYPT_ROUNDS || '12'),
  },

  database: {
    host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
    port: parseInt(process.env.DB_PORT || '5432'),
    name: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp',
    user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
    password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'postgres',
    ssl: process.env.DB_SSL === 'true',
    pool: {
      max: parseInt(process.env.DB_POOL_MAX || '20'),
      min: parseInt(process.env.DB_POOL_MIN || '5'),
      idleTimeout: parseInt(process.env.DB_POOL_IDLE_TIMEOUT || '30000'),
    },
  },

  rateLimit: {
    windowMs: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS || '900000'),
    maxRequests: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX || '100'),
  },
};

export const config = configSchema.parse(rawConfig);
```

```typescript
// src/database/index.ts - Conexão e migrações do PostgreSQL
import { Pool, PoolConfig } from 'pg';
import { config } from '../config';
import fs from 'fs/promises';
import path from 'path';

class Database {
  private pool: Pool;

  constructor() {
    const poolConfig: PoolConfig = {
      host: config.database.host,
      port: config.database.port,
      database: config.database.name,
      user: config.database.user,
      password: config.database.password,
      ssl: config.database.ssl ? { rejectUnauthorized: false } : false,
      max: config.database.pool.max,
      min: config.database.pool.min,
      idleTimeoutMillis: config.database.pool.idleTimeout,
    };

    this.pool = new Pool(poolConfig);

    // Log connection events
    this.pool.on('connect', () => {
      console.log('🔌 New database connection established');
    });

    this.pool.on('error', (err) => {
      console.error('❌ Unexpected database pool error:', err);
    });
  }

  async query(text: string, params?: any[]): Promise<any> {
    const start = Date.now();
    try {
      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      // Log slow queries
      if (duration > 1000) {
        console.warn(`🐌 Slow query detected: ${text} took ${duration}ms`);
      }
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      console.error('❌ Database query error:', {
        query: text,
        params: this.maskSensitiveData(params),
        error: error instanceof Error ? error.message : 'Unknown error',
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  private maskSensitiveData(params?: any[]): any[] {
    if (!params) return [];
    
    return params.map(param => {
      if (typeof param === 'string') {
        // Mask emails
        if (param.includes('@')) {
          const [local, domain] = param.split('@');
          return `${local.charAt(0)}***@${domain}`;
        }
        // Mask tokens (JWT-like strings)
        if (param.length > 32 && param.includes('.')) {
          return '***MASKED_TOKEN***';
        }
      }
      return param;
    });
  }

  async close(): Promise<void> {
    await this.pool.end();
    console.log('🔌 Database connections closed');
  }

  async runMigrations(): Promise<void> {
    const client = await this.pool.connect();
    
    try {
      await client.query('BEGIN');
      
      // Create migrations table if not exists
      await client.query(`
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS migrations (
          id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
          name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
          executed_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
        )
      `);

      // Read migration files
      const migrationsDir = path.join(__dirname, 'migrations');
      const files = await fs.readdir(migrationsDir);
      const sqlFiles = files.filter(f => f.endsWith('.sql')).sort();

      for (const file of sqlFiles) {
        // Check if migration already executed
        const result = await client.query(
          'SELECT id FROM migrations WHERE name = $1',
          [file]
        );

        if (result.rows.length === 0) {
          console.log(`🔄 Running migration: ${file}`);
          
          const sql = await fs.readFile(
            path.join(migrationsDir, file),
            'utf8'
          );
          
          await client.query(sql);
          await client.query(
            'INSERT INTO migrations (name) VALUES ($1)',
            [file]
          );
          
          console.log(`✅ Migration completed: ${file}`);
        }
      }

      await client.query('COMMIT');
    } catch (error) {
      await client.query('ROLLBACK');
      console.error('❌ Migration failed:', error);
      throw error;
    } finally {
      client.release();
    }
  }
}

// Singleton instance
export const db = new Database();

// Export convenience functions
export const connectDatabase = async (): Promise<void> => {
  // Test connection
  await db.query('SELECT NOW()');
};

export const runMigrations = async (): Promise<void> => {
  await db.runMigrations();
};
```

-- src/database/migrations/001_initial_schema.sql
-- Migration inicial com rollback script

-- Users table
CREATE TABLE users (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  email VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  username VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
  password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
  full_name VARCHAR(255),
  avatar_url TEXT,
  is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
  is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
  last_login_at TIMESTAMP,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  updated_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- User sessions table
CREATE TABLE user_sessions (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  refresh_token VARCHAR(512) NOT NULL,
  user_agent TEXT,
  ip_address INET,
  expires_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
  revoked_at TIMESTAMP,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  
  CONSTRAINT refresh_token_unique UNIQUE(refresh_token)
);

-- Audit logs table
CREATE TABLE audit_logs (
  id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT gen_random_uuid(),
  user_id UUID REFERENCES users(id) ON DELETE SET NULL,
  action VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
  resource_type VARCHAR(100),
  resource_id VARCHAR(255),
  details JSONB,
  ip_address INET,
  user_agent TEXT,
  created_at TIMESTAMP DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP
);

-- Indexes for performance
CREATE INDEX idx_users_email ON users(email);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_username ON users(username);
CREATE INDEX idx_users_created_at ON users(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_sessions_user_id ON user_sessions(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_user_sessions_expires_at ON user_sessions(expires_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_user_id ON audit_logs(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_created_at ON audit_logs(created_at);
CREATE INDEX idx_audit_logs_action ON audit_logs(action);

-- Function to update updated_at timestamp
CREATE OR REPLACE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column()
RETURNS TRIGGER AS $$
BEGIN
    NEW.updated_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
    RETURN NEW;
END;
$$ language 'plpgsql';

-- Trigger for users table
CREATE TRIGGER update_users_updated_at 
    BEFORE UPDATE ON users 
    FOR EACH ROW 
    EXECUTE FUNCTION update_updated_at_column();

-- DROP TABLE IF EXISTS users CASCADE;

```typescript
// src/middleware/auth.middleware.ts - Middleware de autenticação JWT
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import { config } from '../config';
import { db } from '../database';

interface JwtPayload {
  userId: string;
  email: string;
  type: 'access' | 'refresh';
}

export const authenticateToken = async (
  req: Request,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
): Promise<void> => {
  const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];
  const token = authHeader && authHeader.split(' ')[1]; // Bearer TOKEN

  if (!token) {
    res.status(401).json({
      error: 'Unauthorized',
      message: 'Access token required',
      correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string,
    });
    return;
  }

  try {
    // Verify JWT token
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, config.server.jwtSecret) as JwtPayload;
    
    // Check token type
    if (decoded.type !== 'access') {
      res.status(403).json({
        error: 'Forbidden',
        message: 'Invalid token type',
        correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string,
      });
      return;
    }

    // Verify user exists and is active
    const userResult = await db.query(
      'SELECT id, email, is_active FROM users WHERE id = $1',
      [decoded.userId]
    );

    if (userResult.rows.length === 0) {
      res.status(403).json({
        error: 'Forbidden',
        message: 'User not found',
        correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string,
      });
      return;
    }

    const user = userResult.rows[0];
    
    if (!user.is_active) {
      res.status(403).json({
        error: 'Forbidden',
        message: 'User account is deactivated',
        correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string,
      });
      return;
    }

    // Attach user to request
    req.user = {
      id: user.id,
      email: user.email,
    };

    next();
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof jwt.TokenExpiredError) {
      res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Unauthorized',
        message: 'Token expired',
        correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string,
      });
    } else if (error instanceof jwt.JsonWebTokenError) {
      res.status(403).json({
        error: 'Forbidden',
        message: 'Invalid token',
        correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string,
      });
    } else {
      console.error('❌ Authentication error:', error);
      res.status(500).json({
        error: 'Internal Server Error',
        message: 'Authentication failed',
        correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string,
      });
    }
  }
};

export const generateTokens = async (
  userId: string,
  email: string
): Promise<{ accessToken: string; refreshToken: string }> => {
  const accessToken = jwt.sign(
    { userId, email, type: 'access' },
    config.server.jwtSecret,
    { expiresIn: config.server.jwtExpiresIn }
  );

  const refreshToken = jwt.sign(
    { userId, email, type: 'refresh' },
    config.server.jwtSecret,
    { expiresIn: '7d' } // Refresh tokens last longer
  );

  return { accessToken, refreshToken };
};
```

```typescript
// src/routes/auth.routes.ts - Rotas de autenticação

  email: z.string().email(),

});

const refreshTokenSchema = z.object({
  refreshToken: z.string(),
});

      res.status(409).json({
        error: 'Conflict',
        message: 'User with this email or username already exists',
        correlationId: req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string,
      });
      return;
    }

    // Hash password
    const passwordHash = await bcrypt.hash(
      validated

## 5. dbt/models/staging/stg_events.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging'
    )
}}

WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        user_id,
        event_type,
        TIMESTAMP_MICROS(CAST(event_timestamp AS INT64)) AS event_timestamp,
        JSON_EXTRACT_SCALAR(properties, '$.page_url') AS page_url,
        JSON_EXTRACT_SCALAR(properties, '$.element_id') AS element_id,
        JSON_EXTRACT_SCALAR(properties, '$.feature_name') AS feature_name,
        session_id,
        TIMESTAMP_MICROS(CAST(ingested_at AS INT64)) AS ingested_at,
        DATE(TIMESTAMP_MICROS(CAST(event_timestamp AS INT64))) AS event_date
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
      AND user_id IS NOT NULL
      AND event_type IS NOT NULL
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    user_id,
    event_type,
    event_timestamp,
    event_date,
    page_url,
    element_id,
    feature_name,
    session_id,
    ingested_at,
    -- Add derived columns
    CASE 
        WHEN event_type IN ('page_view', 'click') THEN 'engagement'
        WHEN event_type IN ('submit', 'api_call') THEN 'conversion'
        WHEN event_type = 'error' THEN 'error'
        ELSE 'other'
    END AS event_category
FROM raw_events
```

## 6. dbt/models/marts/product/daily_active_users.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='product_marts',
        tags=['product', 'marts', 'kpi'],
        post_hook=[
            "GRANT SELECT ON {{ this }} TO 'product_manager'",
            "{{ create_alert('daily_active_users', 'product') }}"
        ]
    )
}}

WITH daily_users AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS date,
        user_id,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS sessions_per_user,
        COUNT(*) AS events_per_user
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }}
    WHERE event_date >= DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 30 DAY)
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

daily_metrics AS (
    SELECT
        date,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS daily_active_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN sessions_per_user >= 3 THEN user_id END) AS engaged_users,
        AVG(sessions_per_user) AS avg_sessions_per_user,
        AVG(events_per_user) AS avg_events_per_user,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) - LAG(COUNT(DISTINCT user_id), 1) OVER (ORDER BY date) AS dau_change,
        SAFE_DIVIDE(
            COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) - LAG(COUNT(DISTINCT user_id), 7) OVER (ORDER BY date),
            LAG(COUNT(DISTINCT user_id), 7) OVER (ORDER BY date)
        ) * 100 AS wow_growth_pct
    FROM daily_users
    GROUP BY 1
)

SELECT
    date,
    daily_active_users,
    engaged_users,
    avg_sessions_per_user,
    avg_events_per_user,
    dau_change,
    wow_growth_pct,
    CASE 
        WHEN wow_growth_pct < -10 THEN 'ALERT: Significant DAU drop'
        WHEN wow_growth_pct > 20 THEN 'ALERT: Significant DAU spike'
        ELSE 'Normal'
    END AS dau_health_status,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS calculated_at
FROM daily_metrics
WHERE date >= DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 30 DAY)
ORDER BY date DESC
```

## 7. dbt/models/marts/ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='ai_marts',
        tags=['ai', 'marts', 'cost'],
        post_hook=[
            "GRANT SELECT ON {{ this }} TO 'ai_ops'",
            "GRANT SELECT ON {{ this }} TO 'llm_specialist'",
            "{{ create_alert('llm_cost_by_feature', 'ai') }}"
        ]
    )
}}

WITH hourly_costs AS (
    SELECT
        TIMESTAMP_TRUNC(timestamp, HOUR) AS hour,
        feature_name,
        model_name,
        provider,
        SUM(input_tokens) AS total_input_tokens,
        SUM(output_tokens) AS total_output_tokens,
        SUM(cost_usd) AS total_cost_usd,
        AVG(latency_ms) AS avg_latency_ms,
        COUNT(*) AS total_calls,
        SUM(CASE WHEN success THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS successful_calls,
        SAFE_DIVIDE(
            SUM(CASE WHEN success THEN 1 ELSE 0 END),
            COUNT(*)
        ) * 100 AS success_rate_pct
    FROM {{ ref('stg_llm_calls') }}
    WHERE timestamp >= TIMESTAMP_SUB(CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(), INTERVAL 7 DAY)
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

feature_daily_rollup AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(hour) AS date,
        feature_name,
        provider,
        SUM(total_input_tokens) AS daily_input_tokens,
        SUM(total_output_tokens) AS daily_output_tokens,
        SUM(total_cost_usd) AS daily_cost_usd,
        AVG(avg_latency_ms) AS avg_daily_latency_ms,
        SUM(total_calls) AS daily_calls,
        AVG(success_rate_pct) AS avg_success_rate,
        -- Cost efficiency metrics
        SAFE_DIVIDE(SUM(total_cost_usd), SUM(total_input_tokens + total_output_tokens)) AS cost_per_token,
        SAFE_DIVIDE(SUM(total_cost_usd), SUM(total_calls)) AS cost_per_call
    FROM hourly_costs
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3
),

anomaly_detection AS (
    SELECT
        *,
        AVG(daily_cost_usd) OVER (
            PARTITION BY feature_name, provider 
            ORDER BY date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 7 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING


### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Arquitetura de Microsserviços

## 1. ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microsserviços V11

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

**CONTEXTO:**
A V10 do DIYAPP evoluiu para uma arquitetura monolítica que está limitando:
- Deploy independente por squad
- Escalabilidade horizontal específica por componente
- Isolamento de falhas
- Velocidade de desenvolvimento paralelo
- Experimentação com diferentes stacks tecnológicas

**DECISÃO:**
Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com os seguintes princípios:
1. Cada microsserviço é responsável por um domínio de negócio específico
2. Comunicação via API REST para síncrono e eventos para assíncrono
3. Cada microsserviço possui seu próprio banco de dados
4. Observabilidade unificada com OpenTelemetry
5. Autonomia completa por squad para deploy e operação

**OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:**
- **Opção A:** Monólito modularizado - Prós: Simplicidade operacional, debugging fácil. Contras: Acoplamento alto, deploy único, escala limitada.
- **Opção B:** Microsserviços completos - Prós: Autonomia por squad, escalabilidade granular, isolamento de falhas. Contras: Complexidade operacional, latência de rede, consistência eventual.
- **Opção C:** Arquitetura hexagonal - Prós: Testabilidade, desacoplamento. Contras: Overhead de abstração, curva de aprendizado.

**Opção escolhida: B** - Justificativa: Alinha com estratégia de squads autônomas, permite evolução independente e escala com crescimento do produto.

**CONSEQUÊNCIAS:**
**Positivas:**
- Deploy independente por microsserviço
- Escalabilidade granular
- Isolamento de falhas
- Autonomia tecnológica por squad
- Melhor paralelismo de desenvolvimento

**Negativas:**
- Complexidade de operação aumentada
- Necessidade de orquestração (Kubernetes)
- Latência de rede entre serviços
- Consistência eventual em alguns casos
- Monitoramento distribuído necessário

**Riscos:**
1. **Cascata de falhas:** Mitigar com circuit breakers e timeouts
2. **Debugging distribuído:** Mitigar com OpenTelemetry e correlation IDs
3. **Deploy descoordenado:** Mitigar com contrato de API versionado e testes de integração

**REVISÃO:** 2024-04-15

## 2. Engineering Standards - V11

```yaml
# engineering-standards-v11.yaml
version: "1.0.0"
last_updated: "2024-01-15"

# 1. Estrutura de Projeto
project_structure:
  base_pattern: "domain-driven"
  required_directories:
    - "src/"
