## 3. Implementação de Observabilidade com OpenTelemetry

```typescript
// src/infrastructure/observability/telemetry.ts
import { NodeSDK } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-node';
import { getNodeAutoInstrumentations } from '@opentelemetry/auto-instrumentations-node';
import { OTLPTraceExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-trace-otlp-grpc';
import { OTLPMetricExporter } from '@opentelemetry/exporter-metrics-otlp-grpc';
import { Resource } from '@opentelemetry/resources';
import { SemanticResourceAttributes } from '@opentelemetry/semantic-conventions';
import { PeriodicExportingMetricReader } from '@opentelemetry/sdk-metrics';
import { WinstonInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-winston';
import { HttpInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-http';
import { ExpressInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-express';
import { PgInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-pg';
import { RedisInstrumentation } from '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-redis';

export class TelemetryService {
  private sdk: NodeSDK | null = null;
  
  constructor(
    private serviceName: string,
    private serviceVersion: string,
    private environment: string
  ) {}

  async start(): Promise<void> {
    const resource = new Resource({
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_NAME]: this.serviceName,
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.SERVICE_VERSION]: this.serviceVersion,
      [SemanticResourceAttributes.DEPLOYMENT_ENVIRONMENT]: this.environment,
    });

    const traceExporter = new OTLPTraceExporter({
      url: process.env.OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4317',
    });

    const metricReader = new PeriodicExportingMetricReader({
      exporter: new OTLPMetricExporter({
        url: process.env.OTEL_EXPORTER_OTLP_ENDPOINT || 'http://localhost:4317',
      }),
      exportIntervalMillis: 60000, // 1 minute
    });

    this.sdk = new NodeSDK({
      resource,
      traceExporter,
      metricReader,
      instrumentations: [
        getNodeAutoInstrumentations({
          '@opentelemetry/instrumentation-fs': { enabled: false },
        }),
        new HttpInstrumentation(),
        new ExpressInstrumentation(),
        new PgInstrumentation(),
        new RedisInstrumentation(),
        new WinstonInstrumentation(),
      ],
    });

    await this.sdk.start();
    console.log(`Telemetry started for ${this.serviceName}`);
  }

  async shutdown(): Promise<void> {
    if (this.sdk) {
      await this.sdk.shutdown();
      console.log('Telemetry shutdown complete');
    }
  }
}

// src/infrastructure/observability/logger.ts
import winston from 'winston';
import { AsyncLocalStorage } from 'async_hooks';

interface LogContext {
  correlationId: string;
  userId?: string;
  service: string;
  version: string;
  [key: string]: any;
}

class LoggerStorage {
  private static asyncLocalStorage = new AsyncLocalStorage<LogContext>();

  static run(context: LogContext, callback: () => void): void {
    this.asyncLocalStorage.run(context, callback);
  }

  static getContext(): LogContext | undefined {
    return this.asyncLocalStorage.getStore();
  }
}

export class StructuredLogger {
  private logger: winston.Logger;
  
  constructor(serviceName: string, serviceVersion: string) {
    const format = winston.format.combine(
      winston.format.timestamp(),
      winston.format.errors({ stack: true }),
      winston.format.json()
    );

    this.logger = winston.createLogger({
      level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
      defaultMeta: {
        service: serviceName,
        version: serviceVersion,
        environment: process.env.APP_ENV || 'development',
      },
      format,
      transports: [
        new winston.transports.Console(),
        new winston.transports.File({
          filename: 'logs/error.log',
          level: 'error',
        }),
        new winston.transports.File({
          filename: 'logs/combined.log',
        }),
      ],
    });
  }

  private enrichMessage(message: string, meta?: any): any {
    const context = LoggerStorage.getContext();
    const baseLog: any = {
      message,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      ...meta,
    };

    if (context) {
      baseLog.correlation_id = context.correlationId;
      if (context.userId) {
        baseLog.user_id = context.userId;
      }
      baseLog.service = context.service;
      baseLog.version = context.version;
    }

    return baseLog;
  }

  error(message: string, error?: Error, meta?: any): void {
    const logData = this.enrichMessage(message, meta);
    if (error) {
      logData.error = {
        name: error.name,
        message: error.message,
        stack: error.stack,
      };
    }
    this.logger.error(logData);
  }

  warn(message: string, meta?: any): void {
    this.logger.warn(this.enrichMessage(message, meta));
  }

  info(message: string, meta?: any): void {
    this.logger.info(this.enrichMessage(message, meta));
  }

  debug(message: string, meta?: any): void {
    this.logger.debug(this.enrichMessage(message, meta));
  }

  static createContext(context: LogContext): void {
    LoggerStorage.run(context, () => {});
  }
}

// src/infrastructure/observability/metrics.ts
import { metrics, Counter, Histogram, ObservableGauge } from '@opentelemetry/api';

export class ApplicationMetrics {
  private meter = metrics.getMeter('diyapp');
  
  // HTTP Metrics
  public httpRequestsTotal: Counter;
  public httpRequestDuration: Histogram;
  public httpRequestSize: Histogram;
  public httpResponseSize: Histogram;
  
  // Business Metrics
  public activeUsers: ObservableGauge;
  public queueSize: ObservableGauge;
  public cacheHitRatio: ObservableGauge;
  
  // Database Metrics
  public dbQueriesTotal: Counter;
  public dbQueryDuration: Histogram;
  public dbConnections: ObservableGauge;
  
  // External Services
  public externalCallsTotal: Counter;
  public externalCallDuration: Histogram;
  
  constructor(serviceName: string) {
    // HTTP Metrics
    this.httpRequestsTotal = this.meter.createCounter('http_requests_total', {
      description: 'Total HTTP requests',
      unit: '1',
    });
    
    this.httpRequestDuration = this.meter.createHistogram('http_request_duration_seconds', {
      description: 'HTTP request duration in seconds',
      unit: 's',
    });
    
    this.httpRequestSize = this.meter.createHistogram('http_request_size_bytes', {
      description: 'HTTP request size in bytes',
      unit: 'By',
    });
    
    this.httpResponseSize = this.meter.createHistogram('http_response_size_bytes', {
      description: 'HTTP response size in bytes',
      unit: 'By',
    });
    
    // Business Metrics
    this.activeUsers = this.meter.createObservableGauge('active_users', {
      description: 'Number of active users',
      unit: '1',
    });
    
    this.queueSize = this.meter.createObservableGauge('queue_size', {
      description: 'Current queue size',
      unit: '1',
    });
    
    this.cacheHitRatio = this.meter.createObservableGauge('cache_hit_ratio', {
      description: 'Cache hit ratio',
      unit: '1',
    });
    
    // Database Metrics
    this.dbQueriesTotal = this.meter.createCounter('db_queries_total', {
      description: 'Total database queries',
      unit: '1',
    });
    
    this.dbQueryDuration = this.meter.createHistogram('db_query_duration_seconds', {
      description: 'Database query duration in seconds',
      unit: 's',
    });
    
    this.dbConnections = this.meter.createObservableGauge('db_connections', {
      description: 'Active database connections',
      unit: '1',
    });
    
    // External Services
    this.externalCallsTotal = this.meter.createCounter('external_calls_total', {
      description: 'Total external service calls',
      unit: '1',
    });
    
    this.externalCallDuration = this.meter.createHistogram('external_call_duration_seconds', {
      description: 'External service call duration in seconds',
      unit: 's',
    });
  }
  
  recordHttpRequest(method: string, route: string, statusCode: number, duration: number): void {
    this.httpRequestsTotal.add(1, {
      method,
      route,
      status_code: statusCode.toString(),
      service: process.env.APP_NAME,
    });
    
    this.httpRequestDuration.record(duration, {
      method,
      route,
      status_code: statusCode.toString(),
    });
  }
}
```

## 4. Middleware de Observabilidade para Express

```typescript
// src/api/middleware/observability.middleware.ts
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { randomUUID } from 'crypto';
import { StructuredLogger } from '../../infrastructure/observability/logger';
import { ApplicationMetrics } from '../../infrastructure/observability/metrics';

export function observabilityMiddleware(
  logger: StructuredLogger,
  metrics: ApplicationMetrics
) {
  return (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): void => {
    const startTime = process.hrtime();
    const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] as string || randomUUID();
    
    // Create logging context
    StructuredLogger.createContext({
      correlationId,
      userId: (req as any).user?.id,
      service: process.env.APP_NAME || 'unknown',
      version: process.env.APP_VERSION || '0.0.0',
    });
    
    // Add correlation ID to response

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Design Atômico

Vou criar um sistema de design atômico completo com tokens de design, componentes reutilizáveis e protótipos de alta fidelidade para fluxos premium, seguindo os princípios de UX baseado em evidências.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-design-system/
├── index.html
├── style.css
├── design-tokens.js
├── components/
│   ├── atoms/
│   ├── molecules/
│   └── organisms/
├── prototypes/
│   └── premium-flows/
└── design-system-docs.html
```

## 1. Design Tokens (design-tokens.js)

```javascript
// design-tokens.js
// Sistema de tokens de design baseado em evidências e acessibilidade

const DesignTokens = {
  // Escala de espaçamento (base 4px)
  spacing: {
    xs: '4px',
    sm: '8px',
    md: '16px',
    lg: '24px',
    xl: '32px',
    '2xl': '48px',
    '3xl': '64px',
    '4xl': '96px'

  // Tipografia - WCAG AA compliant
  typography: {
    fontFamily: {
      primary: "'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, 'Segoe UI', Roboto, sans-serif",
      mono: "'Roboto Mono', 'Courier New', monospace"
    },

      xs: '12px',
      sm: '14px',

      lg: '18px',

      '2xl': '24px',
      '3xl': '30px',
      '4xl': '36px',
      '5xl': '48px'

      bold: '700'

      primary: '#111827',
      secondary: '#374151',
      tertiary: '#6b7280',
      inverse: '#ffffff',
      disabled: '#9ca3af'
    },

    // Borders
    border: {
      light: '#e5e7eb',
      base: '#d1d5db',
      strong: '#9ca3af'
    }
  },

  // Elevation (sombras)
  elevation: {
    none: 'none',
    xs: '0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
    sm: '0 1px 3px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 1px 2px 0 rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
    md: '0 4px 6px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 2px 4px -1px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.06)',
    lg: '0 10px 15px -3px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 4px 6px -2px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)',
    xl: '0 20px 25px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.1), 0 10px 10px -5px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.04)'
  },

  // Border radius
  borderRadius: {
    none: '0',
    sm: '4px',
    md: '8px',
    lg: '12px',
    xl: '16px',
    full: '9999px'
  },

  // Transições e animações
  transitions: {
    duration: {
      fast: '150ms',
      normal: '250ms',
      slow: '350ms'
    },
    easing: {
      easeInOut: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      easeOut: 'cubic-bezier(0, 0, 0.2, 1)',
      easeIn: 'cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 1, 1)'
    }
  },

  // Breakpoints responsivos
  breakpoints: {
    sm: '640px',
    md: '768px',
    lg: '1024px',
    xl: '1280px',
    '2xl': '1536px'
  },

  // Z-index layers
  zIndex: {
    base: 0,
    dropdown: 1000,
    sticky: 1020,
    fixed: 1030,
    modalBackdrop: 1040,
    modal: 1050,
    popover: 1060,
    tooltip: 1070
  }
};

// Exportar tokens como CSS custom properties
function injectDesignTokens() {
  const root = document.documentElement;
  
  // Injetar todas as propriedades CSS
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.colors).forEach(([category, values]) => {
    Object.entries(values).forEach(([key, value]) => {
      if (typeof value === 'object') {
        Object.entries(value).forEach(([subKey, subValue]) => {
          root.style.setProperty(`--color-${category}-${key}-${subKey}`, subValue);
        });
      } else {
        root.style.setProperty(`--color-${category}-${key}`, value);
      }
    });
  });

  // Injetar espaçamento
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.spacing).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    root.style.setProperty(`--spacing-${key}`, value);
  });

  // Injetar tipografia
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.typography.fontSize).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    root.style.setProperty(`--font-size-${key}`, value);
  });

  // Injetar border radius
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.borderRadius).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    root.style.setProperty(`--radius-${key}`, value);
  });

  // Injetar elevação
  Object.entries(DesignTokens.elevation).forEach(([key, value]) => {
    root.style.setProperty(`--elevation-${key}`, value);
  });
}

// Inicializar tokens quando o DOM estiver pronto
if (document.readyState === 'loading') {
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', injectDesignTokens);
} else {
  injectDesignTokens();
}

export default DesignTokens;
```

        "path": "src/App.tsx",
        "content": `import { Routes, Route, Navigate } from 'react-router-dom'
import { Suspense, lazy } from 'react'
import Layout from './components/Layout/Layout'
import LoadingSpinner from './components/Feedback/LoadingSpinner'
import ErrorBoundary from './components/Error/ErrorBoundary'

// Lazy load pages for code splitting
const Dashboard = lazy(() => import('@pages/Dashboard'))
const Projects = lazy(() => import('@pages/Projects'))
const Tasks = lazy(() => import('@pages/Tasks'))
const Settings = lazy(() => import('@pages/Settings'))
const NotFound = lazy(() => import('@pages/NotFound'))

function App() {
  return (
    <ErrorBoundary>
      <Layout>
        <Suspense fallback={<LoadingSpinner fullScreen />}>
          <Routes>
            <Route path="/" element={<Navigate to="/dashboard" replace />} />
            <Route path="/dashboard" element={<Dashboard />} />
            <Route path="/projects" element={<Projects />} />
            <Route path="/tasks" element={<Tasks />} />
            <Route path="/settings" element={<Settings />} />
            <Route path="*" element={<NotFound />} />
          </Routes>
        </Suspense>
      </Layout>
    </ErrorBoundary>
  )
}

export default App`
      },
      {
        "path": "src/components/Layout/Layout.tsx",

// src/config/env.ts
import dotenv from 'dotenv';
import { z } from 'zod';

dotenv.config();

const envSchema = z.object({
  NODE_ENV: z.enum(['development', 'production', 'test']).default('development'),
  PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('3000'),
  
  // Database
  DATABASE_URL: z.string().url(),
  DB_HOST: z.string().default('localhost'),
  DB_PORT: z.string().transform(Number).default('5432'),
  DB_NAME: z.string().default('diyapp_v11'),
  DB_USER: z.string().default('postgres'),
  DB_PASSWORD: z.string().default(''),
  
  // JWT
  JWT_SECRET: z.string().min(32),
  JWT_EXPIRES_IN: z.string().default('24h'),
  JWT_REFRESH_SECRET: z.string().min(32),
  JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN: z.string().default('7d'),
  
  // Security
  BCRYPT_SALT_ROUNDS: z.string().transform(Number).default('12'),
  RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS: z.string().transform(Number).default('900000'),
  RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS: z.string().transform(Number).default('100'),
  
  // Logging
  LOG_LEVEL: z.enum(['error', 'warn', 'info', 'http', 'verbose', 'debug', 'silly']).default('info'),
  LOG_DIR: z.string().default('logs'),
});

export type EnvConfig = z.infer<typeof envSchema>;

const env = envSchema.safeParse(process.env);

if (!env.success) {
  console.error('❌ Invalid environment variables:', env.error.format());
  process.exit(1);
}

export const config = env.data;
```

```typescript
// src/config/database.ts
import { Pool, PoolConfig } from 'pg';
import { config } from './env';
import logger from '../utils/logger';

class Database {
  private static instance: Database;
  private pool: Pool;
  private isConnected = false;

  private constructor() {
    const poolConfig: PoolConfig = {
      host: config.DB_HOST,
      port: config.DB_PORT,
      database: config.DB_NAME,
      user: config.DB_USER,
      password: config.DB_PASSWORD,
      max: 20,
      idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
      connectionTimeoutMillis: 5000,
    };

    // Use DATABASE_URL if provided (for production)
    if (config.DATABASE_URL && config.DATABASE_URL !== '') {
      poolConfig.connectionString = config.DATABASE_URL;
      poolConfig.ssl = { rejectUnauthorized: false };
    }

    this.pool = new Pool(poolConfig);

    this.pool.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Unexpected database error', { error: err.message });
      this.isConnected = false;
    });

    this.pool.on('connect', () => {
      if (!this.isConnected) {
        logger.info('Database connection established');
        this.isConnected = true;
      }
    });
  }

  public static getInstance(): Database {
    if (!Database.instance) {
      Database.instance = new Database();
    }
    return Database.instance;
  }

  public getPool(): Pool {
    return this.pool;
  }

  public async testConnection(): Promise<boolean> {
    try {
      const client = await this.pool.connect();
      await client.query('SELECT NOW()');
      client.release();
      this.isConnected = true;
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Database connection test failed', { error: (error as Error).message });
      this.isConnected = false;
      return false;
    }
  }

  public async query<T = any>(text: string, params?: any[]): Promise<{ rows: T[]; rowCount: number }> {
    const start = Date.now();
    try {
      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      if (duration > 100) {
        logger.warn('Slow query detected', {
          query: text,
          duration,
          params: this.maskSensitiveData(params),
        });
      }
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Database query error', {
        query: text,
        params: this.maskSensitiveData(params),
        error: (error as Error).message,
      });
      throw error;
    }
  }

  private maskSensitiveData(params?: any[]): any[] {
    if (!params) return [];
    
    return params.map(param => {
      if (typeof param === 'string') {
        // Mask emails
        if (param.includes('@')) {
          const [local, domain] = param.split('@');
          const maskedLocal = local.length > 2 
            ? local[0] + '*'.repeat(local.length - 2) + local[local.length - 1]
            : '**';
          return `${maskedLocal}@${domain}`;
        }
        
        // Mask tokens (JWT-like)
        if (param.length > 32 && param.split('.').length === 3) {
          return `${param.substring(0, 10)}...`;
        }
      }
      return param;
    });
  }

  public async close(): Promise<void> {
    await this.pool.end();
    this.isConnected = false;
    logger.info('Database connection closed');
  }
}

export const db = Database.getInstance();
```

```typescript
// src/utils/logger.ts
import winston from 'winston';
import DailyRotateFile from 'winston-daily-rotate-file';
import { config } from '../config/env';

const { combine, timestamp, json, errors, colorize, printf } = winston.format;

// Custom format for console output
const consoleFormat = printf(({ level, message, timestamp, correlationId, userId, endpoint, durationMs, status, error }) => {
  const base = `${timestamp} [${level}] ${message}`;
  const meta = [];
  
  if (correlationId) meta.push(`correlationId=${correlationId}`);
  if (userId) meta.push(`userId=${userId}`);
  if (endpoint) meta.push(`endpoint=${endpoint}`);
  if (durationMs) meta.push(`durationMs=${durationMs}`);
  if (status) meta.push(`status=${status}`);
  if (error) meta.push(`error=${error}`);
  
  return meta.length > 0 ? `${base} ${meta.join(' ')}` : base;
});

const transports: winston.transport[] = [
  // File transport for all logs
  new DailyRotateFile({
    filename: `${config.LOG_DIR}/application-%DATE%.log`,
    datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
    zippedArchive: true,
    maxSize: '20m',
    maxFiles: '30d',
    format: combine(
      timestamp(),
      errors({ stack: true }),
      json()
    ),
  }),
  
  // Error-only file transport
  new DailyRotateFile({
    filename: `${config.LOG_DIR}/error-%DATE%.log`,
    datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
    zippedArchive: true,
    maxSize: '20m',
    maxFiles: '30d',
    level: 'error',
    format: combine(
      timestamp(),
      errors({ stack: true }),
      json()
    ),
  }),
];

// Add console transport in non-production environments
if (config.NODE_ENV !== 'production') {
  transports.push(
    new winston.transports.Console({
      format: combine(
        colorize(),
        timestamp(),
        consoleFormat
      ),
    })
  );
}

const logger = winston.createLogger({
  level: config.LOG_LEVEL,
  defaultMeta: { service: 'diyapp-v11-core' },
  transports,
  exceptionHandlers: [
    new DailyRotateFile({
      filename: `${config.LOG_DIR}/exceptions-%DATE%.log`,
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      zippedArchive: true,
      maxSize: '20m',
      maxFiles: '30d',
    }),
  ],
  rejectionHandlers: [
    new DailyRotateFile({
      filename: `${config.LOG_DIR}/rejections-%DATE%.log`,
      datePattern: 'YYYY-MM-DD',
      zippedArchive: true,
      maxSize: '20m',
      maxFiles: '30d',
    }),
  ],
});

export default logger;
```

```typescript
// src/middleware/auth.ts
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import jwt from 'jsonwebtoken';
import { config } from '../config/env';
import logger from '../utils/logger';
import { ApiError } from '../utils/errors';

export interface AuthRequest extends Request {
  user?: {
    id: string;
    email: string;
    role: string;
  };
}

export const authenticate = async (
  req: AuthRequest,
  res: Response,
  next: NextFunction
): Promise<void> => {
  try {
    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
    
    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
      throw new ApiError(401, 'Authentication required');
    }

    const token = authHeader.substring(7);
    
    // Verify token
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, config.JWT_SECRET) as {
      userId: string;
      email: string;
      role: string;
      iat: number;
      exp: number;
    };

    // Check if token is expired (should be caught by verify, but double-check)
    const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    if (decoded.exp < now) {
      throw new ApiError(401, 'Token expired');
    }

    // Attach user to request
    req.user = {
      id: decoded.userId,
      email: decoded.email,
      role: decoded.role,
    };

    // Log authentication success (masked email)
    logger.info('Authentication successful', {
      correlationId: req.correlationId,
      userId: req.user.id,
      endpoint: req.originalUrl,
      method: req.method,
    });

    next();
  } catch (error) {
    if (error instanceof jwt.JsonWebTokenError) {
      logger.warn('JWT validation failed', {
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        error: error.message,
        endpoint: req.originalUrl,
      });
      next(new ApiError(401, 'Invalid token'));
    } else if (error instanceof jwt.TokenExpiredError) {
      logger.warn('JWT expired', {
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        endpoint: req.originalUrl,
      });
      next(new ApiError(401, 'Token expired'));
    } else {
      next(error);
    }
  }
};

export const authorize = (...roles: string[]) => {
  return (req: AuthRequest, res: Response, next: NextFunction): void => {
    if (!req.user) {
      throw new ApiError(401, 'Authentication required');
    }

    if (!roles.includes(req.user.role)) {
      logger.warn('Authorization failed', {
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        userId: req.user.id,
        userRole: req.user.role,
        requiredRoles: roles,
        endpoint: req.originalUrl,
      });
      throw new ApiError(403, 'Insufficient permissions');
    }

    next();
  };
};

export const generateTokens = (userId: string, email: string, role: string) => {
  const accessToken = jwt.sign(
    { userId, email, role },
    config.JWT_SECRET,
    { expiresIn: config.JWT_EXPIRES_IN }
  );

  const refreshToken = jwt.sign(
    { userId, email, role, type: 'refresh' },
    config.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET,
    { expiresIn: config.JWT_REFRESH_EXPIRES_IN }
  );

  return { accessToken, refreshToken };
};
```

```typescript
// src/middleware/validation.ts
import { Request, Response, NextFunction } from 'express';
import { validationResult, ValidationChain } from 'express-validator';
import { ApiError } from '../utils/errors';

export const validate = (validations: ValidationChain[]) => {
  return async (req: Request, res: Response, next: NextFunction): Promise<void> => {
    await Promise.all(validations.map(validation => validation.run(req)));

    const errors = validationResult(req);
    if (errors.isEmpty()) {
      return next();
    }

    const formattedErrors = errors.array().map(err => ({
      field: err.type === 'field' ? err.path : 'unknown',
      message: err.msg,
    }));

    throw new ApiError(400, 'Validation failed', formattedErrors);
  };
};
```

```typescript
// src/middleware/rateLimit.ts
import rateLimit from 'express-rate-limit';
import { config } from '../config/env';
import logger from '../utils/logger';
import { ApiError } from '../utils/errors';

export const apiRateLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: config.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS,
  max: config.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS,
  message: 'Too many requests from this IP, please try again later.',
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false,
  skipSuccessfulRequests: false,
  handler: (req, res, next, options) => {
    logger.warn('Rate limit exceeded', {
      correlationId: req.correlationId,
      ip: req.ip,
      endpoint: req.originalUrl,
      maxRequests: config.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS,
      windowMs: config.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS,
    });
    
    throw new ApiError(429, options.message);
  },
});

## 1. Configuração do Ambiente (docker-compose.yml)

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # PostgreSQL para metadata do Airflow
  postgres:
    image: postgres:13
    environment:
      POSTGRES_USER: airflow
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: airflow
      POSTGRES_DB: airflow
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U airflow"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Airflow Webserver
  airflow-webserver:
    build:
      context: ./airflow/docker
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    restart: always
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor
      AIRFLOW__CORE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow:airflow@postgres/airflow
      AIRFLOW__CORE__FERNET_KEY: ${AIRFLOW_FERNET_KEY}
      AIRFLOW__CORE__LOAD_EXAMPLES: 'false'
    volumes:
      - ./airflow/dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./airflow/logs:/opt/airflow/logs
      - ./airflow/plugins:/opt/airflow/plugins
      - ./ingestion:/opt/airflow/ingestion
      - ./monitoring:/opt/airflow/monitoring
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    command: webserver
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "curl", "--fail", "http://localhost:8080/health"]
      interval: 30s
      timeout: 10s
      retries: 5

  # Airflow Scheduler
  airflow-scheduler:
    build:
      context: ./airflow/docker
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    restart: always
    depends_on:
      - airflow-webserver
    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: LocalExecutor
      AIRFLOW__CORE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow:airflow@postgres/airflow
      AIRFLOW__CORE__FERNET_KEY: ${AIRFLOW_FERNET_KEY}
    volumes:
      - ./airflow/dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./airflow/logs:/opt/airflow/logs
      - ./airflow/plugins:/opt/airflow/plugins
      - ./ingestion:/opt/airflow/ingestion
      - ./monitoring:/opt/airflow/monitoring
    command: scheduler

  # dbt para transformações
  dbt:
    image: fishtownanalytics/dbt:1.0.0
    volumes:
      - ./dbt:/usr/app
      - ./dbt/profiles.yml:/root/.dbt/profiles.yml
    environment:
      DBT_PROJECT_DIR: /usr/app
    depends_on:
      - postgres
    command: tail -f /dev/null

  # Dashboard web
  dashboard:
    build:
      context: ./dashboard
      dockerfile: Dockerfile
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    volumes:
      - ./dashboard:/app
    depends_on:
      - postgres

volumes:
  postgres_data:
```

## 3. Modelos dbt - Camada Staging

### dbt/models/staging/schema.yml
```yaml
version: 2

sources:
  - name: raw
    schema: raw
    tables:
      - name: events
        description: "Raw events from product"
        loaded_at_field: ingested_at
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 24, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 48, period: hour}
      - name: llm_calls
        description: "Raw LLM calls from gateway"
        loaded_at_field: call_timestamp
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 1, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 2, period: hour}
      - name: users
        description: "Raw user data"
        loaded_at_field: updated_at
        freshness:
          warn_after: {count: 24, period: hour}
          error_after: {count: 48, period: hour}

models:
  - name: stg_events
    description: "Cleaned and standardized events"
    columns:
      - name: event_id
        description: "Unique event identifier"
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: user_id
        description: "User identifier"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: event_type
        description: "Type of event"
        tests:
          - not_null
          - accepted_values:
              values: ['page_view', 'button_click', 'form_submit', 'feature_used', 'error']
      - name: event_timestamp
        description: "Timestamp when event occurred"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: feature_name
        description: "Name of feature if applicable"
      - name: properties
        description: "JSON properties of the event"
      - name: session_id
        description: "Session identifier"
      - name: ingested_at
        description: "Timestamp when data was ingested"
        tests:
          - not_null

  - name: stg_llm_calls
    description: "Cleaned and standardized LLM calls"
    columns:
      - name: call_id
        description: "Unique LLM call identifier"
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: request_id
        description: "Request identifier"
      - name: model_name
        description: "LLM model used"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: provider
        description: "Provider (OpenAI, Anthropic, etc)"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: feature_name
        description: "Feature that triggered the call"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: input_tokens
        description: "Number of input tokens"
        tests:
          - not_null
          - relationships:
              to: ref('stg_events')
              field: feature_name
      - name: output_tokens
        description: "Number of output tokens"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: total_tokens
        description: "Total tokens consumed"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: cost_usd
        description: "Cost in USD"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: latency_ms
        description: "Response latency in milliseconds"
      - name: call_timestamp
        description: "Timestamp when call was made"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: success
        description: "Whether call was successful"
        tests:
          - not_null
```

### dbt/models/staging/stg_events.sql
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging'
    )
}}

WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        user_id,
        event_type,
        TIMESTAMP(event_timestamp) AS event_timestamp,
        feature_name,
        JSON_PARSE(properties) AS properties,
        session_id,
        TIMESTAMP(ingested_at) AS ingested_at
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
),

cleaned_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        COALESCE(user_id, 'anonymous') AS user_id,
        LOWER(event_type) AS event_type,
        event_timestamp,
        CASE 
            WHEN feature_name IS NULL AND event_type = 'feature_used' 
            THEN 'unknown_feature'
            ELSE feature_name
        END AS feature_name,
        properties,
        session_id,
        ingested_at,
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS event_date
    FROM raw_events
)

SELECT * FROM cleaned_events
```

### dbt/models/staging/stg_llm_calls.sql
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging'
    )
}}

WITH raw_calls AS (
    SELECT
        call_id,
        request_id,
        model_name,
        provider,
        feature_name,
        CAST(input_tokens AS INTEGER) AS input_tokens,
        CAST(output_tokens AS INTEGER) AS output_tokens,
        CAST(total_tokens AS INTEGER) AS total_tokens,
        CAST(cost_usd AS DECIMAL(10,6)) AS cost_usd,
        CAST(latency_ms AS INTEGER) AS latency_ms,
        TIMESTAMP(call_timestamp) AS call_timestamp,
        CAST(success AS BOOLEAN) AS success
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'llm_calls') }}
    WHERE call_timestamp IS NOT NULL
),

validated_calls AS (
    SELECT
        call_id,
        request_id,
        model_name,
        provider,
        feature_name,
        input_tokens,
        output_tokens,
        total_tokens,
        cost_usd,
        latency_ms,
        call_timestamp,
        success,
        DATE(call_timestamp) AS call_date,
        -- Data quality checks
        CASE 
            WHEN total_tokens != (input_tokens + output_tokens) 
            THEN TRUE 
            ELSE FALSE 
        END AS token_mismatch_flag,
        CASE 
            WHEN cost_usd < 0 OR cost_usd > 1000 
            THEN TRUE 
            ELSE FALSE 
        END AS cost_outlier_flag
    FROM raw_calls
)

SELECT * FROM validated_calls
```

## 4. Modelos dbt - Camada Marts

### dbt/models/marts/product/daily_active_users.sql
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='product_marts',
        tags=['daily', 'product', 'kpi']
    )
}}

WITH daily_users AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS activity_date,
        user_id,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS daily_sessions,
        COUNT(*) AS daily_events,
        COUNT(DISTINCT feature_name) AS features_used
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }}
    WHERE user_id != 'anonymous'
    GROUP BY 1, 2
),

daily_aggregates AS (
    SELECT
        activity_date,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS active_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT CASE WHEN daily_sessions >= 3 THEN user_id END) AS engaged_users,
        SUM(daily_events) AS total_events,
        AVG(daily_events) AS avg_events_per_user,
        AVG(features_used) AS avg_features_per_user
    FROM daily_users
    GROUP BY 1
),

rolling_metrics AS (
    SELECT
        activity_date,
        active_users,
        engaged_users,
        total_events,
        avg_events_per_user,
        avg_features_per_user,
        AVG(active_users) OVER (
            ORDER BY activity_date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW
        ) AS weekly_avg_active_users,
        AVG(engaged_users) OVER (
            ORDER BY activity_date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW
        ) AS weekly_avg_engaged_users
    FROM daily_aggregates
)

SELECT 
    activity_date,
    active_users,
    engaged_users,
    total_events,
    avg_events_per_user,
    avg_features_per_user,
    weekly_avg_active_users,
    weekly_avg_engaged_users,
    -- Growth metrics
    active_users - LAG(active_users, 1) OVER (ORDER BY activity_date) AS daily_active_users_growth,
    ROUND(
        (active_users - LAG(active_users, 1) OVER (ORDER BY activity_DATE)) * 100.0 / 
        NULLIF(LAG(active_users, 1) OVER (ORDER BY activity_date), 0), 
        2
    ) AS daily_active_users_growth_pct,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS calculated_at
FROM rolling_metrics
ORDER BY activity_date DESC
```

### dbt/models/marts/ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql
```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='ai_marts',
        tags=['hourly', 'ai', 'cost']
    )
}}

WITH hourly_costs AS (
    SELECT
        DATE_TRUNC('hour', call_timestamp) AS hour_start,
        feature_name,
        model_name,
        provider,
        COUNT(*) AS total_calls,
        SUM(CASE WHEN success THEN 1 ELSE 0 END) AS successful_calls,
        SUM(input_tokens) AS total_input_tokens,
        SUM(output_tokens) AS total_output_tokens,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS total_tokens,
        SUM(cost_usd) AS total_cost_usd,
        AVG(latency_ms) AS avg_latency_ms,
        PERCENTILE_CONT(0.5) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY latency_ms) AS p50_latency_ms,
        PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY latency_ms) AS p95_latency_ms
    FROM {{ ref('stg_llm_calls') }}
    WHERE call_timestamp >= DATEADD('hour', -24, CURRENT_TIMESTAMP())
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

feature_daily AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(hour_start) AS cost_date,
        feature_name,
        model_name,
        provider,
        SUM(total_calls) AS daily_calls,
        SUM(successful_calls) AS daily_successful_calls,
        SUM(total_input_tokens) AS daily_input_tokens,
        SUM(total_output_tokens) AS daily_output_tokens,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS daily_tokens,
        SUM(total_cost_usd) AS daily_cost_usd,
        AVG(avg_latency_ms) AS daily_avg_latency,
        SUM(total_cost_usd) * 30 AS estimated_monthly_cost
    FROM hourly_costs
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

cost_anomalies AS (
    SELECT
        *,
        AVG(daily_cost_usd) OVER (
            PARTITION BY feature_name, model_name 
            ORDER BY cost_date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 7 PRECEDING AND 1 PRECEDING
        ) AS avg_7day_cost,
        STDDEV(daily_cost_usd) OVER (
            PARTITION BY feature_name, model_name 
            ORDER BY cost_date 
            ROWS BETWEEN 7 PRECEDING AND 1 PR

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Infraestrutura como Código

Vou configurar uma infraestrutura completa e autônoma para o DIYAPP V11, focando em estabilidade e observabilidade. A arquitetura será baseada em Kubernetes com monitoramento SRE-ready.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-infra/
├── terraform/
│   ├── modules/
│   │   ├── vpc/
│   │   ├── eks/
│   │   ├── rds/
│   │   └── monitoring/
│   ├── environments/
│   │   ├── dev/
│   │   ├── staging/
│   │   └── prod/
│   └── providers.tf
├── kubernetes/
│   ├── base/
│   ├── overlays/
│   ├── manifests/
│   └── helm/
├── github-actions/
│   ├── ci-cd-pipeline.yml
│   ├── security-scan.yml
│   └── chaos-testing.yml
├── monitoring/
│   ├── prometheus/
│   ├── grafana/
│   ├── alerts/
│   └── dashboards/
├── scripts/
├── docs/
└── index.html
```

## 1. Terraform - Infraestrutura como Código

### `terraform/providers.tf`
```hcl
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  
  required_providers {
    aws = {
      source  = "hashicorp/aws"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
    kubectl = {
      source  = "gavinbunney/kubectl"
      version = "~> 1.14"
    }
  }

  backend "s3" {
    bucket         = "diyapp-terraform-state"
    key            = "v11/terraform.tfstate"
    region         = "us-east-1"
    encrypt        = true
    dynamodb_table = "diyapp-terraform-locks"
  }
}

provider "aws" {
  region = var.aws_region
  default_tags {
    tags = {
      Project     = "DIYAPP-V11"
      Environment = var.environment
      ManagedBy   = "Terraform"
      Squad       = "Autonomous-SRE"
    }
  }
}

provider "kubernetes" {
  host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
  cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
  token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
}

provider "helm" {
  kubernetes {
    host                   = module.eks.cluster_endpoint
    cluster_ca_certificate = base64decode(module.eks.cluster_certificate_authority_data)
    token                  = data.aws_eks_cluster_auth.this.token
  }
}
```

### `terraform/modules/vpc/main.tf`
```hcl
module "vpc" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/vpc/aws"
  version = "5.1.2"

  name = "diyapp-v11-${var.environment}"
  cidr = var.vpc_cidr

  azs             = var.availability_zones
  private_subnets = var.private_subnet_cidrs
  public_subnets  = var.public_subnet_cidrs

  enable_nat_gateway     = true
  single_nat_gateway     = var.environment == "dev" ? true : false
  one_nat_gateway_per_az = var.environment == "prod" ? true : false

  enable_dns_hostnames = true
  enable_dns_support   = true

  # EKS requirements
  private_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/role/internal-elb" = "1"
    "kubernetes.io/cluster/diyapp-v11-${var.environment}" = "shared"
  }

  public_subnet_tags = {
    "kubernetes.io/role/elb" = "1"
    "kubernetes.io/cluster/diyapp-v11-${var.environment}" = "shared"
  }

  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_vpc_endpoint" "s3" {
  vpc_id       = module.vpc.vpc_id
  service_name = "com.amazonaws.${var.aws_region}.s3"
  vpc_endpoint_type = "Gateway"

  route_table_ids = module.vpc.private_route_table_ids

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "diyapp-v11-s3-endpoint-${var.environment}"
  })
}

resource "aws_security_group" "vpc_endpoints" {
  name        = "diyapp-v11-vpc-endpoints-${var.environment}"
  description = "Security group for VPC endpoints"
  vpc_id      = module.vpc.vpc_id

  ingress {
    description = "HTTPS from VPC"
    from_port   = 443
    to_port     = 443
    protocol    = "tcp"
    cidr_blocks = [module.vpc.vpc_cidr_block]
  }

  egress {
    from_port   = 0
    to_port     = 0
    protocol    = "-1"
    cidr_blocks = ["0.0.0.0/0"]
  }

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "diyapp-v11-vpc-endpoints-${var.environment}"
  })
}
```

### `terraform/modules/eks/main.tf`
```hcl
module "eks" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/eks/aws"
  version = "19.16.0"

  cluster_name    = "diyapp-v11-${var.environment}"
  cluster_version = "1.28"

  vpc_id     = var.vpc_id
  subnet_ids = var.private_subnet_ids

  cluster_endpoint_public_access  = true
  cluster_endpoint_private_access = true

  # EKS Managed Node Group
  eks_managed_node_groups = {
    main = {
      name           = "main-${var.environment}"
      instance_types = var.node_instance_types
      min_size       = var.min_size
      max_size       = var.max_size
      desired_size   = var.desired_size

      # SLOs: 99.9% availability
      capacity_type  = var.environment == "prod" ? "ON_DEMAND" : "SPOT"

      # Node labels for SRE observability
      labels = {
        Environment = var.environment
        NodeType    = "main"
        ManagedBy   = "terraform"
      }

      # Taints for critical workloads
      taints = var.environment == "prod" ? [
        {
          key    = "critical"
          value  = "true"
          effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
        }
      ] : []

      update_config = {
        max_unavailable_percentage = 33
      }

      # Enable detailed monitoring for SLO tracking
      enable_monitoring = true

      tags = merge(var.tags, {
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/enabled"             = "true"
        "k8s.io/cluster-autoscaler/diyapp-v11-${var.environment}" = "owned"
      })
    }

    # GPU nodes for AI workloads
    gpu = var.enable_gpu_nodes ? {
      name           = "gpu-${var.environment}"
      instance_types = ["g4dn.xlarge", "g5.xlarge"]
      min_size       = 1
      max_size       = 3
      desired_size   = 1

      labels = {
        Environment = var.environment
        NodeType    = "gpu"
        GPU         = "true"
      }

      taints = [
        {
          key    = "nvidia.com/gpu"
          value  = "present"
          effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
        }
      ]
    } : null
  }

  # Cluster Autoscaler for error budget management
  cluster_autoscaler = {
    enabled           = true
    suspend           = false
    balance_similar_node_groups = true
    expander          = "priority"
  }

  # Fargate profiles for serverless workloads
  fargate_profiles = {
    monitoring = {
      name = "monitoring"
      selectors = [
        {
          namespace = "monitoring"
          labels = {
            workload = "monitoring"
          }
        }
      ]
    }
  }

  # CloudWatch logging for SRE observability
  cloudwatch_log_group_retention_in_days = var.environment == "prod" ? 365 : 30
  enable_cluster_creator_admin_permissions = true

  tags = var.tags
}

# IAM roles for service accounts (IRSA)
module "iam_assumable_role_admin" {
  source  = "terraform-aws-modules/iam/aws//modules/iam-assumable-role-with-oidc"
  version = "5.33.0"

  create_role = true
  role_name   = "diyapp-v11-${var.environment}-cluster-admin"

  provider_url = module.eks.oidc_provider
  role_policy_arns = [
    "arn:aws:iam::aws:policy/AdministratorAccess"
  ]

  oidc_fully_qualified_subjects = [
    "system:serviceaccount:kube-system:cluster-autoscaler",
    "system:serviceaccount:monitoring:prometheus"
  ]
}

# Cluster Autoscaler IAM policy
resource "aws_iam_policy" "cluster_autoscaler" {
  name        = "diyapp-v11-cluster-autoscaler-${var.environment}"
  description = "Policy for Kubernetes Cluster Autoscaler"

  policy = jsonencode({
    Version = "2012-10-17"
    Statement = [
      {
        Effect = "Allow"
        Action = [
          "autoscaling:DescribeAutoScalingGroups",
          "autoscaling:DescribeAutoScalingInstances",
          "autoscaling:DescribeLaunchConfigurations",
          "autoscaling:DescribeTags",
          "autoscaling:SetDesiredCapacity",
          "autoscaling:TerminateInstanceInAutoScalingGroup",
          "ec2:DescribeLaunchTemplateVersions"
        ]
        Resource = "*"
      }
    ]
  })

  tags = var.tags
}
```

### `terraform/modules/monitoring/main.tf`
```hcl
# S3 bucket for ALB logs (for SLO tracking)
resource "aws_s3_bucket" "alb_logs" {
  bucket = "diyapp-v11-alb-logs-${var.environment}-${random_id.this.hex}"

  tags = merge(var.tags, {
    Name = "diyapp-v11-alb-logs-${var.environment}"
  })
}

resource "aws_s3_bucket_lifecycle_configuration" "alb_logs" {
  bucket = aws_s3_bucket.alb_logs.id

  rule {
    id     = "log_lifecycle"
    status = "Enabled"

    transition {
      days          = 30
      storage_class = "STANDARD_IA"
    }

    transition {
      days          = 90
      storage_class = "GLACIER"
    }

    expiration {
      days = 365
    }
  }
}

# CloudWatch alarms for SLOs
resource "aws_cloudwatch_metric_alarm" "api_latency_p95" {
  alarm_name          = "diyapp-v11-api-latency-p95-${var.environment}"
  comparison_operator = "GreaterThanThreshold"
  evaluation_periods  = "2"
  metric_name         = "TargetResponseTime"
  namespace           = "AWS/ApplicationELB"
  period              = "300"
  statistic           = "p95"
  threshold           = "0.3" # 300ms SLO
  alarm_description   = "API latency P95 exceeds 300ms SLO"
  treat_missing_data  = "breaching"

  dimensions = {
    LoadBalancer = aws_lb.this.arn_suffix
  }

  alarm_actions = [aws_sns_topic.sre_alerts.arn]

  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_cloudwatch_metric_alarm" "error_rate_5xx" {
  alarm_name          = "diyapp-v11-error-rate-5xx-${var.environment}"
  comparison_operator = "GreaterThanThreshold"
  evaluation_periods  = "1"
  metric_name         = "HTTPCode_Target_5XX_Count"
  namespace           = "AWS/ApplicationELB"
  period              = "300"
  statistic           = "Sum"
  threshold           = "10" # Alert if >10 5xx errors in 5 minutes
  alarm_description   = "5xx error rate exceeds threshold"
  treat_missing_data  = "notBreaching"

  dimensions = {
    LoadBalancer = aws_lb.this.arn_suffix
  }

  alarm_actions = [aws_sns_topic.sre_alerts.arn]

  tags = var.tags
}

# SNS topic for SRE alerts
resource "aws_sns_topic" "sre_alerts" {
  name = "diyapp-v11-sre-alerts-${var.environment}"

  tags = var.tags
}

resource "aws_sns_topic_subscription" "sre_pagerduty" {
  topic_arn = aws_sns_topic.sre_alerts.arn
  protocol  = "https"
  endpoint  = var.pagerduty_endpoint
}

resource "aws_sns_topic_subscription" "sre_slack" {
  topic_arn = aws_sns_topic.sre_alerts.arn
  protocol  = "https"
  endpoint  = var.slack_webhook_url
}

# Prometheus workspace for SLO tracking
resource "aws_prometheus_workspace" "this" {
  alias = "diyapp-v11-${var.environment}"

  tags = var.tags
}

# Grafana workspace
resource "aws_grafana_workspace" "this" {
  name                     = "diyapp-v11-${var.environment}"
  account_access_type      = "CURRENT_ACCOUNT"
  authentication_providers = ["AWS_SSO"]
  permission_type         = "SERVICE_MANAGED"
  data_sources            = ["PROMETHEUS", "CLOUDWATCH"]

  tags = var.tags
}

# Random ID for unique resource names
resource "random_id" "this" {
  byte_length = 8
}

### `terraform/environments/prod/main.tf`
```hcl
module "vpc" {
  source = "../../modules/vpc"

  environment          = "prod"

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
```python
#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""
DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core
Security Specialist Implementation
WAF + Vault + Snyk + RBAC Integration
"""

import os
import json
import yaml
import hashlib
import logging
from datetime import datetime
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
from dataclasses import dataclass, asdict
from enum import Enum
import subprocess
import sys

# ============================================================================
# 1. CONFIGURAÇÃO DE LOGGING
# ============================================================================

logging.basicConfig(
    level=logging.INFO,
    format='%(asctime)s - %(name)s - %(levelname)s - [SECURITY] %(message)s',
    handlers=[
        logging.FileHandler('security_audit.log'),
        logging.StreamHandler()
    ]
)
logger = logging.getLogger('security_specialist')

# ============================================================================
# 2. MODELOS DE DADOS
# ============================================================================

class Severity(Enum):
    CRITICAL = "CRITICAL"
    HIGH = "HIGH"
    MEDIUM = "MEDIUM"
    LOW = "LOW"

class VulnerabilityStatus(Enum):
    OPEN = "OPEN"
    IN_PROGRESS = "IN_PROGRESS"
    RESOLVED = "RESOLVED"
    MITIGATED = "MITIGATED"

@dataclass
class Vulnerability:
    id: str
    cve_id: Optional[str]
    title: str
    description: str
    severity: Severity
    cvss_score: float
    component: str
    detected_at: str
    sla_deadline: str
    status: VulnerabilityStatus
    assigned_to: Optional[str]
    fix_pr: Optional[str]
    
    def is_critical(self) -> bool:
        return self.cvss_score >= 9.0
    
    def is_high(self) -> bool:
        return 7.0 <= self.cvss_score < 9.0
    
    def sla_violated(self) -> bool:
        from datetime import datetime
        now = datetime.now()
        deadline = datetime.fromisoformat(self.sla_deadline)
        return now > deadline and self.status != VulnerabilityStatus.RESOLVED

@dataclass
class RBACPolicy:
    name: str
    description: str
    permissions: List[str]
    resources: List[str]
    conditions: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    
    def to_dict(self) -> Dict:
        return asdict(self)

@dataclass
class WAFRule:
    id: str
    name: str
    description: str
    pattern: str
    action: str  # BLOCK, ALLOW, LOG, CHALLENGE
    severity: Severity
    enabled: bool = True
    
    def match(self, request_data: Dict) -> bool:
        """Check if request matches WAF rule pattern"""
        # Simplified pattern matching - in production use regex or specialized WAF engine
        request_str = json.dumps(request_data).lower()
        pattern_lower = self.pattern.lower()
        
        if "sql" in pattern_lower and any(keyword in request_str for keyword in 
                                          ["' or '1'='1", "union select", "drop table", "--"]):
            return True
            
        if "xss" in pattern_lower and any(keyword in request_str for keyword in
                                          ["<script>", "javascript:", "onload=", "onerror="]):
            return True
            
        if "path_traversal" in pattern_lower and any(keyword in request_str for keyword in
                                                     ["../", "..\\", "/etc/passwd"]):
            return True
            
        return False

# ============================================================================
# 3. WEB APPLICATION FIREWALL (WAF)
# ============================================================================

class DIYAppWAF:
    """Lightweight WAF implementation for DIYAPP"""
    
    def __init__(self):
        self.rules: List[WAFRule] = []
        self._load_default_rules()
        self.blocked_ips: Dict[str, datetime] = {}
        self.request_log: List[Dict] = []
        
    def _load_default_rules(self):
        """Load OWASP Top 10 protection rules"""
        default_rules = [
            WAFRule(
                id="SQLI-001",
                name="SQL Injection Detection",
                description="Detects common SQL injection patterns",
                pattern="sql_injection",
                action="BLOCK",
                severity=Severity.CRITICAL
            ),
            WAFRule(
                id="XSS-001",
                name="Cross-Site Scripting Detection",
                description="Detects XSS attempts in inputs",
                pattern="xss",
                action="BLOCK",
                severity=Severity.HIGH
            ),
            WAFRule(
                id="PT-001",
                name="Path Traversal Detection",
                description="Detects directory traversal attempts",
                pattern="path_traversal",
                action="BLOCK",
                severity=Severity.HIGH
            ),
            WAFRule(
                id="RCE-001",
                name="Remote Code Execution Detection",
                description="Detects RCE patterns in inputs",
                pattern="rce",
                action="BLOCK",
                severity=Severity.CRITICAL
            ),
            WAFRule(
                id="LFI-001",
                name="Local File Inclusion Detection",
                description="Detects LFI attempts",
                pattern="lfi",
                action="BLOCK",
                severity=Severity.HIGH
            )
        ]
        self.rules.extend(default_rules)
        
    def inspect_request(self, request_data: Dict, client_ip: str) -> Dict:
        """
        Inspect incoming HTTP request
        Returns: {"allowed": bool, "rule_matched": Optional[str], "action": str}
        """
        # Check if IP is blocked
        if client_ip in self.blocked_ips:
            block_time = self.blocked_ips[client_ip]
            if (datetime.now() - block_time).total_seconds() < 3600:  # 1 hour block
                return {
                    "allowed": False,
                    "rule_matched": "IP_BLOCKED",
                    "action": "BLOCK",
                    "severity": Severity.HIGH.value
                }
            else:
                del self.blocked_ips[client_ip]
        
        # Apply WAF rules
        for rule in self.rules:
            if rule.enabled and rule.match(request_data):
                logger.warning(f"WAF Rule triggered: {rule.id} - {rule.name} from IP: {client_ip}")
                
                # Log the request
                self.request_log.append({
                    "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
                    "client_ip": client_ip,
                    "rule_id": rule.id,
                    "request_data": request_data,
                    "action": rule.action
                })
                
                # Apply action
                if rule.action == "BLOCK":
                    self.blocked_ips[client_ip] = datetime.now()
                    
                return {
                    "allowed": rule.action != "BLOCK",
                    "rule_matched": rule.id,
                    "action": rule.action,
                    "severity": rule.severity.value
                }
        
        return {"allowed": True, "rule_matched": None, "action": "ALLOW"}
    
    def add_custom_rule(self, rule: WAFRule):
        """Add custom WAF rule"""
        self.rules.append(rule)
        logger.info(f"Added custom WAF rule: {rule.id} - {rule.name}")
    
    def get_metrics(self) -> Dict:
        """Get WAF metrics"""
        blocked_count = sum(1 for log in self.request_log if log["action"] == "BLOCK")
        return {
            "total_requests_checked": len(self.request_log),
            "blocked_requests": blocked_count,
            "active_rules": len([r for r in self.rules if r.enabled]),
            "blocked_ips": len(self.blocked_ips)
        }

# ============================================================================
# 4. SECRET MANAGEMENT (HashiCorp Vault Integration)
# ============================================================================

class SecretManager:
    """Secret management with HashiCorp Vault integration"""
    
    def __init__(self, vault_addr: str = None, token: str = None):
        self.vault_addr = vault_addr or os.getenv("VAULT_ADDR", "http://localhost:8200")
        self.token = token or os.getenv("VAULT_TOKEN")
        self.local_secrets: Dict[str, str] = {}
        self.secret_rotation_log: List[Dict] = []
        
        # For development/testing without real Vault
        if not self.token:
            logger.warning("VAULT_TOKEN not set. Using local secret storage for development.")
            self._init_local_secrets()
    
    def _init_local_secrets(self):
        """Initialize local secrets for development"""
        self.local_secrets = {
            "database/password": self._generate_secret(),
            "api/keys/openai": self._generate_secret(),
            "api/keys/twilio": self._generate_secret(),
            "jwt/secret": self._generate_secret(32),
            "encryption/master_key": self._generate_secret(64)
        }
    
    def _generate_secret(self, length: int = 24) -> str:
        """Generate random secret"""
        import secrets
        import string
        alphabet = string.ascii_letters + string.digits + "!@#$%^&*"
        return ''.join(secrets.choice(alphabet) for _ in range(length))
    
    def get_secret(self, path: str) -> Optional[str]:
        """Get secret from Vault or local storage"""
        try:
            if self.token:
                # Real Vault integration
                import hvac
                client = hvac.Client(url=self.vault_addr, token=self.token)
                secret = client.secrets.kv.v2.read_secret_version(path=path)
                return secret['data']['data']['value']
            else:
                # Local development mode
                return self.local_secrets.get(path)
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to get secret from {path}: {e}")
            return None
    
    def set_secret(self, path: str, value: str, rotate: bool = False):
        """Set secret in Vault or local storage"""
        try:
            if self.token:
                import hvac
                client = hvac.Client(url=self.vault_addr, token=self.token)
                client.secrets.kv.v2.create_or_update_secret(
                    path=path,
                    secret={'value': value}
                )
            else:
                self.local_secrets[path] = value
            
            if rotate:
                self.secret_rotation_log.append({
                    "timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
                    "path": path,
                    "action": "ROTATED",
                    "rotated_by": os.getenv("USER", "system")
                })
                logger.info(f"Secret rotated: {path}")
            else:
                logger.info(f"Secret set: {path}")
                
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Failed to set secret {path}: {e}")
    
    def rotate_secret(self, path: str) -> str:
        """Rotate secret and return new value"""
        new_secret = self._generate_secret()
        self.set_secret(path, new_secret, rotate=True)
        return new_secret
    
    def list_secrets(self) -> List[str]:
        """List all secret paths"""
        if self.token:
            import hvac
            client = hvac.Client(url=self.vault_addr, token=self.token)
            return client.secrets.kv.v2.list_secrets(path="")['data']['keys']
        else:
            return list(self.local_secrets.keys())
    
    def audit_secrets(self) -> Dict:
        """Audit secret usage and rotation"""
        return {
            "total_secrets": len(self.list_secrets()),
            "rotations_last_30d": len([r for r in self.secret_rotation_log 
                                      if (datetime.now() - datetime.fromisoformat(r["timestamp"])).days <= 30]),
            "old_secrets": self._find_old_secrets()
        }
    
    def _find_old_secrets(self) -> List[str]:
        """Find secrets that haven't been rotated in 90 days"""
        old_paths = []
        for path in self.list_secrets():
            rotations = [r for r in self.secret_rotation_log if r["path"] == path]
            if rotations:
                last_rotation = max(datetime.fromisoformat(r["timestamp"]) for r in rotations)
                if (datetime.now() - last_rotation).days > 90:
                    old_paths.append(path)
        return old_paths

# ============================================================================
# 5. DEPENDENCY SCANNING (Snyk Integration)
# ============================================================================

class DependencyScanner:
    """Snyk integration for dependency vulnerability scanning"""
    
    def __init__(self, snyk_token: str = None):
        self.snyk_token = snyk_token or os.getenv("SNYK_TOKEN")
        self.vulnerabilities: List[Vulnerability] = []
        self.scan_results: Dict[str, Any] = {}
        
    def scan_dependencies(self, package_file: str = "package.json") -> List[Vulnerability]:
        """Scan dependencies for vulnerabilities"""
        vulnerabilities = []
        
        try:
            if self.snyk_token:
                # Real Snyk API integration
                vulnerabilities.extend(self._scan_with_snyk_api(package_file))
            else:
                # Local simulation for development
                vulnerabilities.extend(self._simulate_scan(package_file))
            
            # Store results
            self.vulnerabilities = vulnerabilities
            self._update_scan_results(vulnerabilities)
            
            # Check SLA violations
            self._check_sla_violations()
            
            return vulnerabilities
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Dependency scan failed: {e}")
            return []
    
    def _scan_with_snyk_api(self, package_file: str) -> List[Vulnerability]:
        """Scan using Snyk API"""
        import requests
        
        with open(package_file, 'r') as f:
            package_data = json.load(f)
        
        # This is a simplified version - real implementation would use Snyk's API properly
        headers = {
            "Authorization": f"token {self.snyk_token}",
            "Content-Type": "application/json"
        }
        
        # In production, you would make actual API calls to Snyk
        # For now, return simulated results
        return self._simulate_scan(package_file)
    
    def _simulate_scan(self, package_file: str) -> List[Vulnerability]:
        """Simulate dependency scan for development"""
        from datetime import datetime, timedelta
        
        simulated_vulns = [
            Vulnerability(
                id="VULN-001",

                cvss_score=7.4,
                component="lodash@4.17.15",

                sla_deadline=(datetime.now() + timedelta(hours=72)).isoformat(),
                status=VulnerabilityStatus.OPEN,
                assigned_to=None,
                fix_pr=None
            ),
            Vulnerability(
                id="VULN-002",
                cve_id="CVE-2022-12346",
                title="Command Injection in express",
                description="Express before 4.17.3 allows command injection via unsanitized input",
                severity=Severity.CRITICAL,
                cvss_score=9.8,
                component="express@4.16.0",
                detected_at=datetime.now().isoformat(),
                sla_deadline=(datetime.now() + timedelta(hours=24)).isoformat(),
                status=VulnerabilityStatus.OPEN,
                assigned_to=None,
                fix_pr=None
            ),
            Vulnerability(

                severity=Severity.MEDIUM,
                cvss_score=5.3,

                fix_pr=None
            )
        ]
        
        return simulated_vulns
    
    def _update_scan_results(self, vulnerabilities: List[Vulnerability]):
        """Update scan results with statistics"""
        critical = [v for v in vulnerabilities if v.is_critical()]
        high = [v for v in vulnerabilities if v.is_high()]
        
        self.scan_results = {
            "scan_timestamp": datetime.now().isoformat(),
            "total_vulnerabilities": len(vulnerabilities),
            "critical_count": len(critical),
            "high_count": len(high),
            "medium_count": len([v for v in vulnerabilities if v.severity == Severity.MEDIUM]),
            "low_count": len([v for v in vulnerabilities if v.severity == Severity.LOW]),
            "sla_violations": len([v for v in vulnerabilities if v.sla_violated()])
        }
    
    def _check_sla_violations(self):
        """Check for SLA violations and alert"""
        for vuln in self.vulnerabilities:
            if vuln.sla_violated():
                logger.critical(
                    f"SLA VIOLATION: {vuln.id} - {vuln.title} "
                    f"(CVSS: {vuln.cvss_score}) is past SLA deadline!"
                )
                # In production, this would trigger alerts (Slack, PagerDuty, etc.)
    
    def generate_report(self) -> Dict:
        """Generate vulnerability report"""
        return {
            "summary": self.scan_results,
            "vulnerabilities": [asdict(v) for v in self.vulnerabilities],
            "recommendations": self._generate_recommendations()
        }

            recs.append("IMMEDIATE ACTION REQUIRED: Critical vulnerabilities detected. Patch within 24 hours.")
        
        if self.scan_results["sla_violations"] > 0:
            recs.append(f"URGENT: {self.scan_results['sla
