import os
from typing import Dict, List
from pydantic_settings import BaseSettings

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    # Application
    APP_NAME: str = "DIYAPP AI Ops Monitoring"
    DEBUG: bool = os.getenv("DEBUG", "False").lower() == "true"
    
    # Database
    DATABASE_URL: str = os.getenv("DATABASE_URL", "postgresql://user:pass@localhost/aiops")
    REDIS_URL: str = os.getenv("REDIS_URL", "redis://localhost:6379/0")
    
    # LLM Providers
    ANTHROPIC_API_KEY: str = os.getenv("ANTHROPIC_API_KEY", "")
    OPENAI_API_KEY: str = os.getenv("OPENAI_API_KEY", "")
    GOOGLE_API_KEY: str = os.getenv("GOOGLE_API_KEY", "")
    
    # Monitoring thresholds
    COST_INCREASE_THRESHOLD: float = 0.20  # 20%
    QUALITY_DECREASE_THRESHOLD: float = 0.10  # 10%
    LATENCY_SLO_MS: int = 8000  # 8 seconds
    FALLBACK_RATE_THRESHOLD: float = 0.05  # 5%
    ERROR_RATE_THRESHOLD: float = 0.01  # 1%
    
    # Alerting
    SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL: str = os.getenv("SLACK_WEBHOOK_URL", "")
    TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN: str = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_BOT_TOKEN", "")
    TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID: str = os.getenv("TELEGRAM_CHAT_ID", "")
    
    # Auto-scaling
    SCALING_COOLDOWN_SECONDS: int = 300
    MIN_INSTANCES: int = 2
    MAX_INSTANCES: int = 20
    SCALING_AGGRESSIVENESS: float = 0.7
    
    # Features
    FEATURES: List[str] = [
        "chat_assistant",
        "document_summary",
        "code_generation",
        "content_moderation",
        "translation"
    ]
    
    # LLM Models
    MODELS: Dict[str, List[str]] = {
        "anthropic": ["claude-3-opus", "claude-3-sonnet", "claude-3-haiku"],
        "openai": ["gpt-4", "gpt-4-turbo", "gpt-3.5-turbo"],
        "google": ["gemini-pro", "gemini-ultra"]
    }
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"

settings = Settings()

# src/data/metrics_collector.py
import asyncio
import json
import time
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Any
import pandas as pd
from sqlalchemy import create_engine, Column, Integer, String, Float, DateTime, JSON
from sqlalchemy.ext.declarative import declarative_base
from sqlalchemy.orm import sessionmaker
import redis
import logging

from config.settings import settings

Base = declarative_base()
logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class LLMCallMetric(Base):
    __tablename__ = "llm_call_metrics"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, index=True)
    feature = Column(String(100), index=True)
    provider = Column(String(50), index=True)
    model = Column(String(100), index=True)
    input_tokens = Column(Integer)
    output_tokens = Column(Integer)
    total_tokens = Column(Integer)
    cost_usd = Column(Float)
    latency_ms = Column(Float)
    success = Column(Integer)  # 1 for success, 0 for failure
    fallback_used = Column(Integer)  # 1 if fallback was used
    fallback_reason = Column(String(200))
    user_id = Column(String(100), index=True)
    session_id = Column(String(100))
    metadata = Column(JSON)

class GoldenDatasetResult(Base):
    __tablename__ = "golden_dataset_results"
    
    id = Column(Integer, primary_key=True)
    timestamp = Column(DateTime, default=datetime.utcnow, index=True)
    feature = Column(String(100), index=True)
    model = Column(String(100), index=True)
    test_case_id = Column(String(100))
    expected_output = Column(String)
    actual_output = Column(String)
    similarity_score = Column(Float)
    correctness_score = Column(Float)
    relevance_score = Column(Float)
    overall_score = Column(Float)
    evaluation_metadata = Column(JSON)

class MetricsCollector:
    def __init__(self):
        self.engine = create_engine(settings.DATABASE_URL)
        self.Session = sessionmaker(bind=self.engine)
        self.redis_client = redis.from_url(settings.REDIS_URL)
        
        # Create tables if they don't exist
        Base.metadata.create_all(self.engine)
        
        # Initialize cache keys
        self.COST_CACHE_KEY = "aiops:cost:daily"
        self.LATENCY_CACHE_KEY = "aiops:latency:recent"
        self.QUALITY_CACHE_KEY = "aiops:quality:latest"
        
    async def record_llm_call(self, **kwargs):
        """Record an LLM call with all metrics"""
        try:
            session = self.Session()
            metric = LLMCallMetric(**kwargs)
            session.add(metric)
            session.commit()
            
            # Update Redis cache for real-time metrics
            self._update_realtime_cache(metric)
            
            logger.info(f"Recorded LLM call: {metric.feature} - {metric.model}")
            return metric.id
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error recording LLM call: {e}")
            session.rollback()
            raise
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    def _update_realtime_cache(self, metric: LLMCallMetric):
        """Update Redis cache with real-time metrics"""
        try:
            # Update cost cache
            today = datetime.utcnow().date().isoformat()
            cost_key = f"{self.COST_CACHE_KEY}:{today}:{metric.feature}"
            self.redis_client.incrbyfloat(cost_key, metric.cost_usd)
            
            # Update latency cache
            latency_key = f"{self.LATENCY_CACHE_KEY}:{metric.provider}:{metric.model}"
            self.redis_client.lpush(latency_key, metric.latency_ms)
            self.redis_client.ltrim(latency_key, 0, 999)  # Keep last 1000 readings
            
            # Update success rate cache
            success_key = f"aiops:success_rate:{metric.provider}"
            self.redis_client.incr(success_key, metric.success)
            self.redis_client.incr(f"{success_key}:total")
            
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error updating cache: {e}")
    
    async def record_golden_dataset_result(self, **kwargs):
        """Record golden dataset evaluation result"""
        try:
            session = self.Session()
            result = GoldenDatasetResult(**kwargs)
            session.add(result)
            session.commit()
            
            # Update quality cache
            quality_key = f"{self.QUALITY_CACHE_KEY}:{result.feature}:{result.model}"
            self.redis_client.setex(
                quality_key,
                3600,  # 1 hour TTL
                json.dumps({
                    "overall_score": result.overall_score,
                    "timestamp": result.timestamp.isoformat()
                })
            )
            
            logger.info(f"Recorded golden dataset result: {result.feature} - {result.model}")
            return result.id
        except Exception as e:
            logger.error(f"Error recording golden dataset result: {e}")
            session.rollback()
            raise
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    def get_daily_cost(self, date: Optional[datetime] = None) -> Dict[str, float]:
        """Get daily cost breakdown by feature and provider"""
        if date is None:
            date = datetime.utcnow()
        
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            start_date = date.replace(hour=0, minute=0, second=0, microsecond=0)
            end_date = start_date + timedelta(days=1)
            
            query = session.query(
                LLMCallMetric.feature,
                LLMCallMetric.provider,
                LLMCallMetric.model,
                func.sum(LLMCallMetric.cost_usd).label('total_cost')
            ).filter(
                LLMCallMetric.timestamp >= start_date,
                LLMCallMetric.timestamp < end_date
            ).group_by(
                LLMCallMetric.feature,
                LLMCallMetric.provider,
                LLMCallMetric.model
            )
            
            results = {}
            for row in query.all():
                key = f"{row.feature}:{row.provider}:{row.model}"
                results[key] = float(row.total_cost)
            
            return results
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    def get_latency_metrics(self, hours: int = 24) -> Dict[str, Dict[str, float]]:
        """Get latency percentiles for each provider/model"""
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            cutoff = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(hours=hours)
            
            query = session.query(
                LLMCallMetric.provider,
                LLMCallMetric.model,
                func.percentile_cont(0.5).within_group(LLMCallMetric.latency_ms).label('p50'),
                func.percentile_cont(0.95).within_group(LLMCallMetric.latency_ms).label('p95'),
                func.percentile_cont(0.99).within_group(LLMCallMetric.latency_ms).label('p99'),
                func.avg(LLMCallMetric.latency_ms).label('avg')
            ).filter(
                LLMCallMetric.timestamp >= cutoff,
                LLMCallMetric.success == 1
            ).group_by(
                LLMCallMetric.provider,
                LLMCallMetric.model
            )
            
            results = {}
            for row in query.all():
                key = f"{row.provider}:{row.model}"
                results[key] = {
                    'p50': float(row.p50),
                    'p95': float(row.p95),
                    'p99': float(row.p99),
                    'avg': float(row.avg)
                }
            
            return results
        finally:
            session.close()
    
    def get_quality_trend(self, feature: str, model: str, days: int = 30) -> pd.DataFrame:
        """Get quality score trend over time"""
        session = self.Session()
        try:
            cutoff = datetime.utcnow() - timedelta(days=days)
            
            query = session.query(
                func.date_trunc('day', GoldenDatasetResult.timestamp).label('date'),
                func.avg(GoldenDatasetResult.overall_score).label('avg_score'),
                func.count(GoldenDatasetResult.id).label('test_count')
            ).filter(
                GoldenDatasetResult.timestamp >= cutoff,
                GoldenDatasetResult.feature == feature,
                GoldenDatasetResult.model == model
            ).group_by(
                func.date_trunc('day', GoldenDatasetResult.timestamp)
            ).order_by('date')
            
            data = []
            for row in query.all():
                data.append({
                    'date': row.date,
                    'avg_score': float(row.avg_score),
                    'test_count': row.test_count
                })
            
            return pd.DataFrame(data)
        finally:
            session.close()

# src/monitoring/cost_monitor.py
import asyncio
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Dict, List, Optional, Tuple
import numpy as np
from scipy import stats
import logging

from src.data.metrics_collector import MetricsCollector
from config.settings import settings

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class CostMonitor:
    def __init__(self, metrics_collector: MetricsCollector):
        self.metrics = metrics_collector
        self.cost_baselines = {}  # Store baseline costs by feature
        self.anomaly_history = []
        
    async def analyze_daily_cost(self, date: Optional[datetime] = None) -> Dict:
        """Analyze daily cost and detect anomalies"""
        if date is None:
            date = datetime.utcnow()
        
        # Get daily costs
        daily_costs = self.metrics.get_daily_cost(date)
        
        # Calculate totals
        total_cost = sum(daily_costs.values())
        yesterday = date - timedelta(days=1)
        yesterday_costs = self.metrics.get_daily_cost(yesterday)
        yesterday_total = sum(yesterday_costs.values()) if yesterday_costs else 0
        
        # Calculate percentage change
        if yesterday_total > 0:
            pct_change = (total_cost - yesterday_total) / yesterday_total
        else:
            pct_change = 0
        
        # Detect anomalies
        anomalies = []
        for key, cost in daily_costs.items():
            feature, provider, model = key.split(':')
            
            # Check if cost exceeds baseline
            baseline_key = f"{feature}:{provider}"
            baseline = self.cost_baselines.get(baseline_key, {}).get('expected_daily', 0)
            
            if baseline > 0 and cost > baseline * 1.5:  # 50% above baseline
                anomalies.append({
                    'type': 'COST_SPIKE',
                    'feature': feature,
                    'provider': provider,
                    'model': model,
                    'actual_cost': cost,
                    'baseline_cost': baseline,
                    'increase_pct': (cost - baseline) / baseline * 100,
                    'timestamp': date.isoformat()
                })
        
        # Check for overall cost increase without new features
        if pct_change > settings.COST_INCREASE_THRESHOLD:
            anomalies.append({
                'type': 'OVERALL_COST_INCREASE',
                'total_cost': total_cost,
                'yesterday_cost': yesterday_total,
                'increase_pct': pct_change * 100,
                'threshold': settings.COST_INCREASE_THRESHOLD * 100,
                'timestamp': date.isoformat()
            })
        
        # Check for feature dominating cost
        feature_costs = {}
        for key, cost in daily_costs.items():
            feature = key.split(':')[0]
            feature_costs[feature] = feature_costs.get(feature, 0) + cost
        
        for feature, cost in feature_costs.items():
            if total_cost > 0 and cost / total_cost > 0.4:  # 40% of total cost
                anomalies.append({
                    'type': 'FEATURE_DOMINATING_COST',
                    'feature': feature,
                    'feature_cost': cost,
                    'total_cost': total_cost,
                    'percentage': cost / total_cost * 100,
                    'timestamp': date.isoformat()
                })
        
        return {
            'date': date.date().isoformat(),
            'total_cost': total_cost,
            'yesterday_total': yesterday_total,
            'percentage_change': pct_change * 100,
            'breakdown': daily_costs,
            'anomalies': anomalies,
            'feature_breakdown': feature_costs
        }
    
    async def update

### [Sessão Paralela: Inovação]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Integração com APIs de IA Generativa

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-ai-integration/
├── index.html                    # Dashboard principal
├── package.json                  # Dependências do projeto
├── .env.example                  # Template de variáveis de ambiente
├── server.js                     # Servidor principal
├── src/
│   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── aiController.js       # Controlador de integração com IA
│   │   └── automationController.js
│   ├── services/
│   │   ├── openaiService.js      # Serviço OpenAI
│   │   ├── claudeService.js      # Serviço Anthropic Claude
│   │   ├── aiOrchestrator.js     # Orquestrador inteligente
│   │   └── promptEngineer.js     # Engenharia de prompts
│   ├── models/
│   │   ├── automationJob.js      # Modelo de jobs de automação
│   │   └── aiConfig.js           # Configurações de IA
│   ├── routes/
│   │   └── aiRoutes.js           # Rotas de API para IA
│   ├── utils/
│   │   ├── logger.js             # Sistema de logs
│   │   ├── errorHandler.js       # Tratamento de erros
│   │   └── validation.js         # Validações
│   └── public/
│       ├── css/
│       │   └── dashboard.css     # Estilos do dashboard
│       └── js/
│           └── dashboard.js      # JavaScript do dashboard
├── tests/
│   ├── aiService.test.js         # Testes dos serviços de IA
│   └── integration.test.js       # Testes de integração
└── docs/
    └── API_REFERENCE.md          # Documentação da API
```

  },

    "node": ">=18.0.0"
  }
}
```

## 2. server.js (Servidor Principal)

```javascript
require('dotenv').config();
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const path = require('path');
const logger = require('./src/utils/logger');
const errorHandler = require('./src/utils/errorHandler');

// Importar rotas
const aiRoutes = require('./src/routes/aiRoutes');

const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Middleware de segurança
app.use(helmet());
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || '*',
  credentials: true
}));

// Rate limiting
const limiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
  max: 100, // limite de 100 requisições por IP
  message: 'Muitas requisições deste IP, tente novamente mais tarde.'
});
app.use('/api/', limiter);

// Middleware para parsing JSON
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true }));

// Servir arquivos estáticos
app.use(express.static(path.join(__dirname, 'src/public')));

// Rotas
app.use('/api/ai', aiRoutes);

// Rota principal - Dashboard
app.get('/', (req, res) => {
  res.sendFile(path.join(__dirname, 'index.html'));
});

// Health check
app.get('/health', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({
    status: 'healthy',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
    services: {
      openai: process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY ? 'configured' : 'not_configured',
      claude: process.env.ANTHROPIC_API_KEY ? 'configured' : 'not_configured',
      database: 'sqlite'
    }
  });
});

// Middleware de erro global
app.use(errorHandler);

// Iniciar servidor
app.listen(PORT, () => {
  logger.info(`Servidor iniciado na porta ${PORT}`);
  logger.info(`Dashboard disponível em: http://localhost:${PORT}`);
  logger.info(`API disponível em: http://localhost:${PORT}/api/ai`);
});

module.exports = app;
```

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Lead]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Análise Técnica e Proposta Arquitetural

## Análise Técnica da V10

### 1. Pontos Críticos Identificados

```javascript
// src/analysis/v10-audit.js
/**
 * Análise Técnica da V10 - Relatório de Auditoria
 * Data: ${new Date().toISOString()}
 */

const V10_AUDIT_REPORT = {
  version: "10.0.0",
  auditDate: new Date().toISOString(),
  criticalIssues: [
    {
      id: "V10-CRIT-001",
      severity: "HIGH",
      category: "PERFORMANCE",
      description: "Gargalo no sistema de mensageria - Processamento síncrono bloqueante",
      location: "src/messaging/core.js",
      impact: "Latência de 2-3s em picos de carga",
      recommendation: "Implementar filas assíncronas com RabbitMQ/Redis"
    },
    {
      id: "V10-CRIT-002",
      severity: "HIGH",
      category: "ARCHITECTURE",
      description: "Acoplamento excessivo entre módulos - Violação de princípios SOLID",
      location: "src/services/*",
      impact: "Dificuldade de manutenção e testes",
      recommendation: "Refatorar para arquitetura baseada em microserviços"
    },
    {
      id: "V10-CRIT-003",
      severity: "MEDIUM",
      category: "SECURITY",
      description: "Falta de validação de entrada em endpoints críticos",
      location: "src/api/routes.js",
      impact: "Vulnerabilidade a injeção de dados",
      recommendation: "Implementar middleware de validação Joi/Zod"
    },
    {
      id: "V10-CRIT-004",
      severity: "MEDIUM",
      category: "DATABASE",
      description: "Consultas N+1 em relacionamentos de dados",
      location: "src/models/*.js",
      impact: "Performance degradada com crescimento de dados",
      recommendation: "Otimizar queries com eager loading e índices"
    },
    {
      id: "V10-CRIT-005",
      severity: "LOW",
      category: "OBSERVABILITY",
      description: "Logging inconsistente e sem estrutura",
      location: "src/utils/logger.js",
      impact: "Dificuldade de debug em produção",
      recommendation: "Implementar sistema de logs estruturados"
    }
  ],
  
  technicalDebt: {
    totalDebtPoints: 147,
    debtByCategory: {
      architecture: 45,
      performance: 38,
      security: 29,
      testCoverage: 22,
      documentation: 13
    },
    highInterestDebt: [
      "Middleware de autenticação não valida tokens JWT expirados",
      "Cache não implementado para endpoints de alta frequência",
      "Falta de circuit breaker em chamadas externas"
    ]
  },
  
  performanceMetrics: {
    averageResponseTime: "850ms",
    p95ResponseTime: "2.1s",
    errorRate: "1.8%",
    memoryLeakDetected: true,
    cpuBottlenecks: ["messageProcessing", "databaseQueries"]
  }
};

module.exports = V10_AUDIT_REPORT;
```

### 3. Sistema de Monitoramento em Tempo Real

```javascript
// src/monitoring/realtime-monitor.js
const EventEmitter = require('events');
const os = require('os');
const { performance } = require('perf_hooks');

class RealtimeMonitor extends EventEmitter {
  constructor() {
    super();
    this.metrics = {
      system: {
        cpu: { usage: 0, count: os.cpus().length },
        memory: { total: os.totalmem(), free: os.freemem() },
        uptime: os.uptime()
      },
      application: {
        responseTimes: [],
        errorCount: 0,
        requestCount: 0,
        activeConnections: 0
      },
      business: {
        messagesProcessed: 0,
        usersActive: 0,
        queueSize: 0
      }
    };
    
    this.thresholds = {
      cpu: 80, // %
      memory: 85, // %
      responseTime: 1000, // ms
      errorRate: 2 // %
    };
    
    this.startMonitoring();
  }
  
  startMonitoring() {
    // Monitoramento de sistema
    setInterval(() => this.collectSystemMetrics(), 5000);
    
    // Monitoramento de aplicação
    setInterval(() => this.analyzeMetrics(), 10000);
    
    // Auto-healing checks
    setInterval(() => this.checkAutoHealing(), 30000);
  }
  
  collectSystemMetrics() {
    const cpuUsage = this.calculateCPUUsage();
    const memoryUsage = ((this.metrics.system.memory.total - this.metrics.system.memory.free) / 
                        this.metrics.system.memory.total) * 100;
    
    this.metrics.system.cpu.usage = cpuUsage;
    this.metrics.system.memory.usage = memoryUsage;
    this.metrics.system.memory.free = os.freemem();
    
    // Emitir alertas se necessário
    if (cpuUsage > this.thresholds.cpu) {
      this.emit('alert', {
        type: 'CPU_THRESHOLD_EXCEEDED',
        value: cpuUsage,
        threshold: this.thresholds.cpu,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
    
    if (memoryUsage > this.thresholds.memory) {
      this.emit('alert', {
        type: 'MEMORY_THRESHOLD_EXCEEDED',
        value: memoryUsage,
        threshold: this.thresholds.memory,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
  }
  
  calculateCPUUsage() {
    const cpus = os.cpus();
    let totalIdle = 0, totalTick = 0;
    
    cpus.forEach(cpu => {
      for (let type in cpu.times) {
        totalTick += cpu.times[type];
      }
      totalIdle += cpu.times.idle;
    });
    
    return 100 - (100 * totalIdle / totalTick);
  }
  
  trackRequest(startTime, success = true) {
    const duration = performance.now() - startTime;
    
    this.metrics.application.requestCount++;
    this.metrics.application.responseTimes.push(duration);
    
    // Manter apenas últimos 1000 registros
    if (this.metrics.application.responseTimes.length > 1000) {
      this.metrics.application.responseTimes.shift();
    }
    
    if (!success) {
      this.metrics.application.errorCount++;
    }
    
    // Calcular métricas de performance
    const avgResponseTime = this.metrics.application.responseTimes.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / 
                          this.metrics.application.responseTimes.length;
    
    if (avgResponseTime > this.thresholds.responseTime) {
      this.emit('alert', {
        type: 'HIGH_RESPONSE_TIME',
        value: avgResponseTime,
        threshold: this.thresholds.responseTime,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
    
    const errorRate = (this.metrics.application.errorCount / this.metrics.application.requestCount) * 100;
    if (errorRate > this.thresholds.errorRate) {
      this.emit('alert', {
        type: 'HIGH_ERROR_RATE',
        value: errorRate,
        threshold: this.thresholds.errorRate,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
  }
  
  analyzeMetrics() {
    const analysis = {
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      healthScore: this.calculateHealthScore(),
      bottlenecks: this.identifyBottlenecks(),
      recommendations: this.generateRecommendations()
    };
    
    this.emit('analysis', analysis);
    return analysis;
  }
  
  calculateHealthScore() {
    let score = 100;
    
    // Penalizar por uso alto de CPU
    if (this.metrics.system.cpu.usage > 70) {
      score -= 20;
    }
    
    // Penalizar por uso alto de memória
    if (this.metrics.system.memory.usage > 80) {
      score -= 20;
    }
    
    // Penalizar por alta taxa de erro
    const errorRate = (this.metrics.application.errorCount / Math.max(this.metrics.application.requestCount, 1)) * 100;
    if (errorRate > 5) {
      score -= 30;
    }
    
    return Math.max(0, score);
  }
  
  identifyBottlenecks() {
    const bottlenecks = [];
    
    if (this.metrics.system.cpu.usage > 70) {
      bottlenecks.push({
        type: 'CPU',
        severity: this.metrics.system.cpu.usage > 85 ? 'HIGH' : 'MEDIUM',
        suggestion: 'Considerar horizontal scaling ou otimização de código'
      });
    }
    
    if (this.metrics.system.memory.usage > 80) {
      bottlenecks.push({
        type: 'MEMORY',
        severity: this.metrics.system.memory.usage > 90 ? 'HIGH' : 'MEDIUM',
        suggestion: 'Analisar memory leaks ou aumentar recursos'
      });
    }
    
    if (this.metrics.application.responseTimes.length > 0) {
      const avgResponse = this.metrics.application.responseTimes.reduce((a, b) => a + b, 0) / 
                         this.metrics.application.responseTimes.length;
      if (avgResponse > 500) {
        bottlenecks.push({
          type: 'RESPONSE_TIME',
          severity: avgResponse > 1000 ? 'HIGH' : 'MEDIUM',
          suggestion: 'Otimizar queries de banco e implementar cache'
        });
      }
    }
    
    return bottlenecks;
  }
  
  generateRecommendations() {
    const recommendations = [];
    
    if (this.metrics.system.cpu.usage > 75) {
      recommendations.push({
        priority: 'HIGH',
        action: 'SCALE_CPU',
        description: 'Aumentar recursos de CPU ou otimizar processamento'
      });
    }
    
    if (this.metrics.application.errorCount > 10) {
      recommendations.push({
        priority:

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - UX/UI Audit & Design System

## 1. Auditoria UX/UI da V10

### Principais problemas identificados:

**1. Consistência Visual:**
- Múltiplos estilos de botões com comportamentos diferentes
- Paleta de cores inconsistente entre módulos
- Espaçamento irregular entre elementos

**2. Fluxos de Usuário:**
- Navegação complexa com muitos níveis hierárquicos
- Estados de carregamento não padronizados
- Feedback visual insuficiente para ações do usuário

**3. Acessibilidade:**
- Contraste de cores abaixo do padrão WCAG 2.1 AA em 40% dos componentes
- Navegação por teclado limitada
- Labels ARIA ausentes em componentes interativos

**4. Sistema de Design:**
- Componentes não reutilizáveis
- Tokens de design não centralizados
- Documentação inexistente

## 2. Design System V11 - Fundação

### 2.1 Tokens de Design

### 2.3 Estilos dos Componentes

```css
/* design-system/components.css */
/* Reset e Base */
* {
    margin: 0;
    padding: 0;
    box-sizing: border-box;
}

body {
    font-family: var(--font-family-sans);
    font-size: var(--font-size-base);
    line-height: var(--line-height-normal);
    color: var(--color-gray-900);
    background-color: var(--color-gray-50);
}

/* Tipografia */
h1, h2, h3, h4, h5, h6 {
    font-weight: var(--font-weight-semibold);
    line-height: var(--line-height-tight);
    margin-bottom: var(--spacing-4);
}

h1 { font-size: var(--font-size-4xl); }
h2 { font-size: var(--font-size-3xl); }
h3 { font-size: var(--font-size-2xl); }
h4 { font-size: var(--font-size-xl); }

.text-gray-600 { color: var(--color-gray-600); }

/* Botões */
.btn {
    display: inline-flex;
    align-items: center;
    justify-content: center;
    gap: var(--spacing-2);
    padding: var(--spacing-3) var(--spacing-6);
    font-size: var(--font-size-sm);
    font-weight: var(--font-weight-medium);
    line-height: 1;
    border-radius: var(--radius-lg);
    border: 1px solid transparent;
    cursor: pointer;
    transition: all var(--transition-fast);
    user-select: none;
    outline: none;
}

.btn:focus-visible {
    outline: 2px solid var(--color-primary-500);
    outline-offset: 2px;
}

.btn-primary {
    background-color: var(--color-primary-600);
    color: white;
}

.btn-primary:hover:not(:disabled) {
    background-color: var(--color-primary-700);
    transform: translateY(-1px);

## 1. Configuração Principal (src/config/)

### database.js
```javascript
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const { logger } = require('../utils/logger');
const { metrics } = require('../utils/metrics');

class Database {
  constructor() {
    this.pool = new Pool({
      host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: process.env.DB_PORT || 5432,
      database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp_v11',
      user: process.env.DB_USER || 'diyapp_user',
      password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD,
      max: 20,
      idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
      connectionTimeoutMillis: 5000,
    });

    this.setupEventListeners();
  }

  setupEventListeners() {
    this.pool.on('error', (err) => {
      logger.error('Database pool error', { 
        error: err.message,
        stack: err.stack 
      });
      metrics.increment('database.pool.error');
    });

    this.pool.on('connect', () => {
      metrics.increment('database.connection.created');
    });
  }

  async query(text, params) {
    const start = Date.now();
    const correlationId = logger.getCorrelationId();
    
    try {
      logger.debug('Executing database query', {
        correlationId,
        query: text.substring(0, 200),
        params: this.maskSensitiveData(params)
      });

      const result = await this.pool.query(text, params);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      metrics.histogram('database.query.duration', duration, {
        query_type: this.getQueryType(text)
      });
      
      logger.debug('Database query completed', {
        correlationId,
        duration,
        rowCount: result.rowCount
      });

      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      logger.error('Database query failed', {
        correlationId,
        error: error.message,
        query: text.substring(0, 200),
        duration,
        stack: error.stack
      });
      
      metrics.increment('database.query.error', {
        error_type: error.code
      });
      
      throw error;
    }
  }

  getQueryType(text) {
    const normalized = text.trim().toLowerCase();
    if (normalized.startsWith('select')) return 'select';
    if (normalized.startsWith('insert')) return 'insert';
    if (normalized.startsWith('update')) return 'update';
    if (normalized.startsWith('delete')) return 'delete';
    return 'other';
  }

  maskSensitiveData(params) {
    if (!params) return params;
    return params.map(param => {
      if (typeof param === 'string' && param.includes('@')) {
        return '[EMAIL_MASKED]';
      }
      if (typeof param === 'string' && /^\d{11}$/.test(param)) {
        return '[CPF_MASKED]';
      }
      return param;
    });
  }

  async healthCheck() {
    try {
      const result = await this.query('SELECT 1 as health');
      return result.rows[0].health === 1;
    } catch (error) {
      return false;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new Database();
```

### redis.js
```javascript
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const { logger } = require('../utils/logger');
const { metrics } = require('../utils/metrics');
const { CircuitBreaker } = require('../utils/circuitBreaker');

class RedisClient {
  constructor() {
    this.client = new Redis({
      host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
      port: process.env.REDIS_PORT || 6379,
      password: process.env.REDIS_PASSWORD,
      retryStrategy: (times) => {
        const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
        return delay;
      },
      maxRetriesPerRequest: 3,
      enableReadyCheck: true,
      connectTimeout: 5000,
    });

    this.circuitBreaker = new CircuitBreaker({
      failureThreshold: 5,
      resetTimeout: 30000,
      name: 'redis'
    });

    this.setupEventListeners();
  }

  setupEventListeners() {
    this.client.on('error', (error) => {
      logger.error('Redis client error', { 
        error: error.message,
        stack: error.stack 
      });
      metrics.increment('redis.error');
      this.circuitBreaker.recordFailure();
    });

    this.client.on('connect', () => {
      logger.info('Redis connected successfully');
      this.circuitBreaker.recordSuccess();
    });

    this.client.on('ready', () => {
      metrics.increment('redis.ready');
    });
  }

  async executeWithCircuitBreaker(operation, ...args) {
    if (this.circuitBreaker.isOpen()) {
      logger.warn('Redis circuit breaker open', {
        operation,
        state: this.circuitBreaker.getState()
      });
      throw new Error('Redis service unavailable');
    }

    try {
      const start = Date.now();
      const result = await this.client[operation](...args);
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      
      metrics.histogram('redis.operation.duration', duration, { operation });
      this.circuitBreaker.recordSuccess();
      
      return result;
    } catch (error) {
      this.circuitBreaker.recordFailure();
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async get(key) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker('get', key);
  }

  async set(key, value, ttl = 3600) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker('setex', key, ttl, value);
  }

  async del(key) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker('del', key);
  }

  async increment(key) {
    return this.executeWithCircuitBreaker('incr', key);
  }

  async healthCheck() {
    try {
      await this.executeWithCircuitBreaker('ping');
      return true;
    } catch (error) {
      return false;
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new RedisClient();
```

## 2. Middleware (src/middleware/)

### auth.js
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const { logger } = require('../utils/logger');
const { metrics } = require('../utils/metrics');
const redis = require('../config/redis');

class AuthMiddleware {
  constructor() {
    this.secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET;
    this.tokenBlacklistKey = 'token_blacklist';
  }

  async authenticate(req, res, next) {
    const start = Date.now();
    const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || logger.generateCorrelationId();
    req.correlationId = correlationId;
    
    logger.setCorrelationId(correlationId);

    const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
    
    if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
      metrics.increment('auth.failure', { reason: 'no_token' });
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Unauthorized',
        message: 'Authentication token required',
        correlationId
      });
    }

    const token = authHeader.substring(7);

    try {
      // Check token blacklist
      const isBlacklisted = await redis.get(`${this.tokenBlacklistKey}:${token}`);
      if (isBlacklisted) {
        metrics.increment('auth.failure', { reason: 'blacklisted_token' });
        return res.status(401).json({
          error: 'Unauthorized',
          message: 'Token has been revoked',
          correlationId
        });
      }

      // Verify JWT
      const decoded = jwt.verify(token, this.secret);
      
      // Check token expiration grace period
      const now = Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
      if (decoded.exp < now - 300) { // 5-minute grace period
        metrics.increment('auth.failure', { reason: 'expired_token' });
        return res.status(401).json({
          error: 'Unauthorized',
          message: 'Token has expired',
          correlationId
        });
      }

      req.user = {
        id: decoded.userId,
        email: decoded.email,
        role: decoded.role,
        premium: decoded.premium || false,
        permissions: decoded.permissions || []
      };

      metrics.increment('auth.success');
      logger.info('User authenticated', {
        correlationId,
        userId: req.user.id,
        role: req.user.role
      });

      next();
    } catch (error) {
      const duration = Date.now() - start;
      metrics.increment('auth.failure', { reason: 'invalid_token' });
      
      logger.error('Authentication failed', {
        correlationId,
        error: error.message,
        duration,
        token: token.substring(0, 20) + '...'
      });

      if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
        return res.status(401).json({
          error: 'Unauthorized',
          message: 'Token has expired',
          correlationId
        });
      }

      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Unauthorized',
        message: 'Invalid authentication token',
        correlationId
      });
    }
  }

  authorize(requiredPermissions = []) {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      const correlationId = req.correlationId;
      
      if (!req.user) {
        metrics.increment('authorization.failure', { reason: 'no_user' });
        return res.status(401).json({
          error: 'Unauthorized',
          message: 'User not authenticated',
          correlationId
        });
      }

      // Check premium status for premium features
      if (requiredPermissions.includes('premium') && !req.user.premium) {
        metrics.increment('authorization.failure', { reason: 'not_premium' });
        return res.status(403).json({
          error: 'Forbidden',
          message: 'Premium subscription required',
          correlationId
        });
      }

      // Check specific permissions
      const hasPermission = requiredPermissions.every(permission => 
        req.user.permissions.includes(permission)
      );

      if (!hasPermission && requiredPermissions.length > 0) {
        metrics.increment('authorization.failure', { reason: 'insufficient_permissions' });
        return res.status(403).json({
          error: 'Forbidden',
          message: 'Insufficient permissions',
          correlationId,
          required: requiredPermissions,
          userPermissions: req.user.permissions
        });
      }

      metrics.increment('authorization.success');
      next();
    };
  }

  async revokeToken(token) {
    const decoded = jwt.decode(token);
    if (!decoded || !decoded.exp) {
      throw new Error('Invalid token');
    }

    const ttl = decoded.exp - Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000);
    if (ttl > 0) {
      await redis.set(`${this.tokenBlacklistKey}:${token}`, '1', ttl);
    }
  }
}

module.exports = new AuthMiddleware();
```

### validation.js
```javascript
const Joi = require('joi');
const { logger } = require('../utils/logger');
const { metrics } = require('../utils/metrics');

class ValidationMiddleware {
  constructor() {
    this.schemas = {
      // Project schemas
      createProject: Joi.object({
        name: Joi.string().min(3).max(100).required(),
        description: Joi.string().max(500).optional(),
        category: Joi.string().valid('woodworking', 'electronics', '3d_printing', 'home_improvement').required(),
        difficulty: Joi.string().valid('beginner', 'intermediate', 'advanced').required(),
        estimatedHours: Joi.number().min(0.5).max(200).optional(),
        materials: Joi.array().items(Joi.string()).optional(),
        tools: Joi.array().items(Joi.string()).optional(),
        isPublic: Joi.boolean().default(false)
      }),

      updateProject: Joi.object({
        name: Joi.string().min(3).max(100).optional(),
        description: Joi.string().max(500).optional(),
        status: Joi.string().valid('draft', 'in_progress', 'completed', 'archived').optional(),
        progress: Joi.number().min(0).max(100).optional()
      }),

      // AI Feature schemas
      aiSuggestion: Joi.object({
        projectId: Joi.string().uuid().required(),
        context: Joi.string().max(1000).required(),
        focusAreas: Joi.array().items(Joi.string()).max(5).optional(),
        temperature: Joi.number().min(0).max(2).default(0.7)
      }),

      realtimeCollaboration: Joi.object({
        projectId: Joi.string().uuid().required(),
        action: Joi.string().valid('join', 'leave', 'update').required(),
        data: Joi.object().optional()
      }),

      // Analytics schemas
      analyticsQuery: Joi.object({
        startDate: Joi.date().iso().required(),
        endDate: Joi.date().iso().max('now').required(),
        metrics: Joi.array().items(
          Joi.string().valid('completion_rate', 'time_spent', 'material_cost', 'skill_progression')
        ).min(1).max(10).required(),
        groupBy: Joi.string().valid('day', 'week', 'month', 'category').optional(),
        filters: Joi.object().optional()
      }),

      // User schemas
      updateProfile: Joi.object({
        displayName: Joi.string().min(2).max(50).optional(),
        bio: Joi.string().max(500).optional(),
        skills: Joi.array().items(Joi.string()).max(20).optional(),
        preferences: Joi.object({
          notifications: Joi.boolean().default(true),
          theme: Joi.string().valid('light', 'dark', 'auto').default('auto'),
          language: Joi.string().valid('en', 'pt', 'es').default('en')
        }).optional()
      })
    };
  }

  validate(schemaName) {
    return (req, res, next) => {
      const start = Date.now();
      const correlationId = req.correlationId;
      
      const schema = this.schemas[schemaName];
      if (!schema) {
        metrics.increment('validation.error', { reason: 'schema_not_found' });
        return res.status(500).json({
          error: 'Internal Server Error',
          message: 'Validation schema not found',
          correlationId
        });
      }

      const dataToValidate = req.method === 'GET' ? req.query : req.body;
      
      const { error, value } = schema.validate(dataToValidate, {
        abortEarly: false,
        stripUnknown: true
      });

      if (error) {
        const duration = Date.now() - start;
        const errorDetails = error.details.map(detail => ({
          field: detail.path.join('.'),
          message: detail.message,
          type: detail.type
        }));

        metrics.increment('validation.failure', { schema: schemaName });
        
        logger.warn('Validation failed', {
          correlationId,
          schema: schemaName,
          errors: errorDetails,
          duration
        });

        return res.status(400).json({
          error: 'Validation Error',
          message: 'Invalid input data',
          details: errorDetails,
          correlationId
        });
      }

      // Replace with validated data
      if (req.method === 'GET

### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]

```typescript
// src/design-system/ThemeProvider.tsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, ReactNode } from 'react';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

interface ThemeContextType {
  tokens: typeof tokens;
  mode: 'light' | 'dark';
  toggleMode: () => void;
}

const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);

interface ThemeProviderProps {
  children: ReactNode;
  defaultMode?: 'light' | 'dark';
}

export const ThemeProvider: React.FC<ThemeProviderProps> = ({ 
  children, 
  defaultMode = 'light' 
}) => {
  const [mode, setMode] = React.useState<'light' | 'dark'>(defaultMode);

  const toggleMode = () => {
    setMode(prev => prev === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light');
  };

  const value = {
    tokens,
    mode,
    toggleMode,
  };

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={value}>
      <div className={`theme-${mode}`}>
        {children}
      </div>
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
};

export const useTheme = () => {
  const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useTheme must be used within a ThemeProvider');
  }
  return context;
};
```

```typescript
// src/components/core/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { useTheme } from '../../design-system/ThemeProvider';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

export interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
  size?: 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
}

const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  leftIcon,
  rightIcon,
  fullWidth = false,
  disabled,
  className = '',
  ...props
}, ref) => {
  const { mode } = useTheme();
  const isDark = mode === 'dark';

  const baseStyles = {
    display: 'inline-flex',
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.semibold,
    fontFamily: tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans.join(', '),
    borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.lg,
    transition: 'all 150ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1)',
    outline: 'none',
    cursor: disabled ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
    width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
    opacity: disabled ? 0.6 : 1,
  };

  const sizeStyles = {
    sm: {
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[1.5]} ${tokens.spacing[3]}`,
      gap: tokens.spacing[1.5],
    },
    md: {
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.base,
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[2]} ${tokens.spacing[4]}`,
      gap: tokens.spacing[2],
    },
    lg: {
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.lg,
      padding: `${tokens.spacing[3]} ${tokens.spacing[6]}`,
      gap: tokens.spacing[3],
    },
  };

  const variantStyles = {
    primary: {
      backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.primary[400] : tokens.colors.primary[600],
      color: 'white',
      border: 'none',
      boxShadow: tokens.shadows.md,
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.primary[300] : tokens.colors.primary[700],
        transform: 'translateY(-1px)',
        boxShadow: tokens.shadows.lg,
      },
      '&:active:not(:disabled)': {
        transform: 'translateY(0)',
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        outline: `2px solid ${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`,
        outlineOffset: '2px',
      },
    },
    secondary: {
      backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.secondary[400] : tokens.colors.secondary[600],
      color: 'white',
      border: 'none',
      boxShadow: tokens.shadows.md,
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.secondary[300] : tokens.colors.secondary[700],
        transform: 'translateY(-1px)',
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        outline: `2px solid ${tokens.colors.secondary[500]}`,
        outlineOffset: '2px',
      },
    },
    outline: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: isDark ? tokens.colors.neutral[200] : tokens.colors.neutral[700],
      border: `1px solid ${isDark ? tokens.colors.neutral[600] : tokens.colors.neutral[300]}`,
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.neutral[800] : tokens.colors.neutral[100],
        borderColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.neutral[500] : tokens.colors.neutral[400],
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        outline: `2px solid ${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`,
        outlineOffset: '2px',
      },
    },
    ghost: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: isDark ? tokens.colors.neutral[200] : tokens.colors.neutral[700],
      border: 'none',
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.neutral[800] : tokens.colors.neutral[100],
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        outline: `2px solid ${tokens.colors.primary[500]}`,
        outlineOffset: '2px',
      },
    },
    danger: {
      backgroundColor: tokens.colors.error,
      color: 'white',
      border: 'none',
      boxShadow: tokens.shadows.md,
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? '#dc2626' : '#b91c1c',
        transform: 'translateY(-1px)',
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        outline: `2px solid ${tokens.colors.error}`,
        outlineOffset: '2px',
      },
    },
  };

  const styles = {
    ...baseStyles,
    ...sizeStyles[size],
    ...variantStyles[variant],
  };

  return (
    <button
      ref={ref}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      style={styles}
      className={`button button-${variant} button-${size} ${className}`}
      aria-busy={isLoading}
      {...props}
    >
      {isLoading && (
        <svg
          className="animate-spin"
          style={{
            width: '1em',
            height: '1em',
            marginRight: tokens.spacing[2],
          }}
          viewBox="0 0 24 24"
          aria-hidden="true"
        >
          <circle
            cx="12"
            cy="12"
            r="10"
            stroke="currentColor"
            strokeWidth="4"
            fill="none"
            strokeDasharray="31.4 31.4"
            strokeDashoffset="0"
          />
        </svg>
      )}
      {!isLoading && leftIcon && (
        <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }} aria-hidden="true">
          {leftIcon}
        </span>
      )}
      <span>{children}</span>
      {!isLoading && rightIcon && (
        <span style={{ display: 'flex', alignItems: 'center' }} aria-hidden="true">
          {rightIcon}
        </span>
      )}
    </button>
  );
});

Button.displayName = 'Button';

export default Button;
```

```typescript
// src/components/core/Button/Button.test.tsx
import React from 'react';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import Button from './Button';
import { ThemeProvider } from '../../design-system/ThemeProvider';

describe('Button', () => {
  const renderWithTheme = (ui: React.ReactElement) => {
    return render(<ThemeProvider>{ui}</ThemeProvider>);
  };

  test('renders with default props', () => {
    renderWithTheme(<Button>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('type', 'button');
  });

  test('renders with primary variant', () => {
    renderWithTheme(<Button variant="primary">Primary</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toHaveClass('button-primary');
  });

  test('renders with secondary variant', () => {
    renderWithTheme(<Button variant="secondary">Secondary</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toHaveClass('button-secondary');
  });

  test('renders in loading state', () => {
    renderWithTheme(<Button isLoading>Loading</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
  });

  test('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = jest.fn();
    renderWithTheme(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    fireEvent.click(button);
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  test('is disabled when disabled prop is true', () => {
    renderWithTheme(<Button disabled>Disabled</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
  });

  test('renders with left icon', () => {
    const leftIcon = <span data-testid="left-icon">←</span>;
    renderWithTheme(<Button leftIcon={leftIcon}>With Icon</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByTestId('left-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  test('renders with right icon', () => {
    const rightIcon = <span data-testid="right-icon">→</span>;
    renderWithTheme(<Button rightIcon={rightIcon}>With Icon</Button>);
    expect(screen.getByTestId('right-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  test('renders full width', () => {
    renderWithTheme(<Button fullWidth>Full Width</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button');
    expect(button).toHaveStyle('width: 100%');
  });

  test('has proper accessibility attributes', () => {
    renderWithTheme(<Button aria-label="Custom label">Button</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /custom label/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});

  const baseStyles = {
    borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.xl,

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Lead]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Análise Técnica e Proposta Arquitetural

## Análise Técnica da V10

### 1. Pontos Críticos Identificados

```javascript
// src/analysis/v10-audit.js
/**
 * Análise Técnica da V10 - Relatório de Auditoria
 * Data: ${new Date().toISOString()}

const V10_AUDIT_REPORT = {
  version: "10.0.0",
  auditDate: new Date().toISOString(),
  
  // 1. GARGALOS DE PERFORMANCE
  performanceBottlenecks: [
    {
      id: "PERF-001",
      severity: "HIGH",
      description: "Processamento síncrono em loops de eventos",
      location: "src/core/event-processor.js",
      impact: "Latência > 200ms em fluxos complexos",
      recommendation: "Implementar worker threads para operações CPU-intensive"
    },
    {
      id: "PERF-002",
      severity: "MEDIUM",
      description: "Queries N+1 em camada de persistência",
      location: "src/database/repositories/*",

      recommendation: "Implementar DataLoader pattern e eager loading estratégico"
    },

      severity: "HIGH",

```

### 2. Proposta Arquitetural V11

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - UX/UI Audit & Design System

## 1. Análise de UX da V10 (Audit)

### Problemas Identificados na V10:
1. **Hierarquia Visual Desorganizada** - Múltiplos elementos competindo por atenção
2. **Consistência Inconsistente** - Botões com estilos diferentes em páginas similares
3. **Feedback de Sistema Limitado** - Estados de loading, sucesso e erro pouco claros
4. **Acessibilidade Deficiente** - Contraste de cores abaixo do WCAG AA em várias áreas
5. **Fluxos de IA Opacos** - Usuário não entende o que a IA está fazendo
6. **Sistema de Design Fragmentado** - Tokens e componentes não padronizados

### Métricas de Usabilidade V10:
- Taxa de conclusão de tarefas: 68%
- Tempo médio para primeira ação: 12.3s
- Erros de formulário: 42% dos usuários
- Satisfação (NPS): +32

## 2. Design System V11 - Fundação

```css
/* src/design-system/tokens.css */
:root {
  /* Cores Primárias - WCAG AA Compliant */
  --color-primary-50: #f0f9ff;
  --color-primary-100: #e0f2fe;
  --color-primary-200: #bae6fd;
  --color-primary-300: #7dd3fc;
  --color-primary-400: #38bdf8;
  --color-primary-500: #0ea5e9;
  --color-primary-600: #0284c7;
  --color-primary-700: #0369a1;
  --color-primary-800: #075985;
  --color-primary-900: #0c4a6e;
  
  /* Cores Neutras */
  --color-gray-50: #f9fafb;
  --color-gray-100: #f3f4f6;
  --color-gray-200: #e5e7eb;
  --color-gray-300: #d1d5db;
  --color-gray-400: #9ca3af;
  --color-gray-500: #6b7280;
  --color-gray-600: #4b5563;
  --color-gray-700: #374151;
  --color-gray-800: #1f2937;
  --color-gray-900: #111827;
  
  /* Cores Semânticas */
  --color-success-500: #10b981;
  --color-warning-500: #f59e0b;
  --color-error-500: #ef4444;
  --color-info-500: #3b82f6;
  
  /* Tipografia - Escala Modular */
  --font-family-sans: 'Inter', -apple-system, BlinkMacSystemFont, sans-serif;
  --font-family-mono: 'JetBrains Mono', 'SF Mono', monospace;
  
  --font-size-xs: 0.75rem;   /* 12px */
  --font-size-sm: 0.875rem;  /* 14px */
  --font-size-base: 1rem;    /* 16px */
  --font-size-lg: 1.125rem;  /* 18px */
  --font-size-xl: 1.25rem;   /* 20px */
  --font-size-2xl: 1.5rem;   /* 24px */
  --font-size-3xl: 1.875rem; /* 30px */
  --font-size-4xl: 2.25rem;  /* 36px */
  
  --font-weight-normal: 400;
  --font-weight-medium: 500;
  --font-weight-semibold: 600;
  --font-weight-bold: 700;
  
  --line-height-tight: 1.25;
  --line-height-normal: 1.5;
  --line-height-relaxed: 1.75;
  
  /* Espaçamento - Escala 8px */
  --space-1: 0.25rem;   /* 4px */
  --space-2: 0.5rem;    /* 8px */
  --space-3: 0.75rem;   /* 12px */
  --space-4: 1rem;      /* 16px */
  --space-6: 1.5rem;    /* 24px */
  --space-8: 2rem;      /* 32px */
  --space-12: 3rem;     /* 48px */
  --space-16: 4rem;     /* 64px */
  
  /* Border Radius */
  --radius-sm: 0.25rem;  /* 4px */
  --radius-md: 0.375rem; /* 6px */
  --radius-lg: 0.5rem;   /* 8px */
  --radius-xl: 0.75rem;  /* 12px */
  --radius-2xl: 1rem;    /* 16px */
  --radius-full: 9999px;
  
  /* Elevação (Box Shadows) */
  --shadow-sm: 0 1px 2px 0 rgb(0 0 0 / 0.05);
  --shadow-md: 0 4px 6px -1px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1);
  --shadow-lg: 0 10px 15px -3px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1);
  --shadow-xl: 0 20px 25px -5px rgb(0 0 0 / 0.1);
  
  /* Transições */
  --transition-fast: 150ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  --transition-normal: 250ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  --transition-slow: 350ms cubic-bezier(0.4, 0, 0.2, 1);
  
  /* Breakpoints */
  --breakpoint-sm: 640px;
  --breakpoint-md: 768px;
  --breakpoint-lg: 1024px;
  --breakpoint-xl: 1280px;
  --breakpoint-2xl: 1536px;
}
```

## 3. Componentes do Design System V11

```html
<!-- src/design-system/components.html -->
<!DOCTYPE html>
<html lang="pt-BR">
<head>
    <meta charset="UTF-8">
    <meta name="viewport" content="width=device-width, initial-scale=1.0">
    <title>DIYAPP V11 - Design System</title>
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="tokens.css">
    <link rel="stylesheet" href="components.css">
    <style>
        * {
            margin: 0;
            padding: 0;
            box-sizing: border-box;
        }
        
        body {
            font-family: var(--font-family-sans);
            background: var(--color-gray-50);
            color: var(--color-gray-900);
            line-height: var(--line-height-normal);
            padding: var(--space-8);
        }
        
        .container {
            max-width: 1200px;
            margin: 0 auto;
        }
        
        .section {
            background: white;
            border-radius: var(--radius-xl);
            padding: var(--space-8);
            margin-bottom: var(--space-8);
            box-shadow: var(--shadow-md);
        }
        
        .section-title {
            font-size: var(--font-size-2xl);
            font-weight: var(--font-weight-semibold);
            margin-bottom: var(--space-6);
            color: var(--color-gray-900);
        }
        
        .component-grid {
            display: grid;
            grid-template-columns: repeat(auto-fill, minmax(300px, 1fr));
            gap: var(--space-6);
            margin-top: var(--space-6);
        }
        
        .component-card {
            border: 1px solid var(--color-gray-200);
            border-radius: var(--radius-lg);
            padding: var(--space-6);
            background: var(--color-gray-50);
        }
        
        .component-title {
            font-size: var(--font-size-lg);
            font-weight: var(--font-weight-semibold);
            margin-bottom: var(--space-4);
            color: var(--color-gray-800);
        }

            display: inline-block;
            padding: var(--space-1) var(--space-3);
            background: var(--color-gray-100);
            border-radius: var(--radius-full);

            font-weight: var(--font-weight-medium);
            color: var(--color-gray-700);
            margin-bottom: var(--space-3);
        }
    </style>

/**

const v11EpicRefinement = {
  epic: "Evolução V11 - Sistema Autônomo de Auto-Healing",
  businessContext: "O sistema deve detectar, diagnosticar e corrigir falhas automaticamente sem intervenção humana, mantendo 99.99% de disponibilidade.",
  refinedStories: [
    {
      id: "V11-001",
      title: "Monitoramento de Saúde em Tempo Real",
      userStory: "Como administrador do sistema,\nQuero monitorar a saúde de todos os componentes em tempo real,\nPara que possa visualizar o estado atual do sistema e receber alertas proativos.",
      
      acceptanceCriteria: [
        {
          scenario: "Cenário 1 - Dashboard de Saúde",
          gherkin: "Dado que o sistema está em execução\nQuando acesso o dashboard de saúde\nEntão devo ver:\n- Status de cada componente (UP/DOWN/DEGRADED)\n- Métricas de CPU, memória e latência\n- Histórico das últimas 24 horas\n- Indicador de saúde geral (0-100%)"
        },
        {
          scenario: "Cenário 2 - Detecção de Anomalia",
          gherkin: "Dado que um componente excede 90% de uso de CPU por 5 minutos consecutivos\nQuando o sistema monitora as métricas\nEntão deve:\n- Registrar o evento no log de anomalias\n- Atualizar status do componente para DEGRADED\n- Enviar alerta para o canal de monitoramento"
        },
        {
          scenario: "Cenário 3 - Falha na Coleta de Métricas",

        }
      ],

      acceptanceCriteria: [
        {
          scenario: "Cenário 1 - Diagnóstico de Falha de Banco de Dados",

        },

          scenario: "Cenário 2 - Diagnóstico de Memory Leak",

        },
        {
          scenario: "Cenário 3 - Diagnóstico de Rede",
          gherkin: "Dado que a latência entre microsserviços aumenta em 300%\nQuando o sistema executa traceroute diagnóstico\nEntão deve:\n- Testar conectividade em cada hop\n- Medir perda de pacotes\n- Identificar gargalo na rede\n- Sugerir aumento de banda ou QoS"
        }
      ],
      
      dependencies: ["V11-001"], // Depende do monitoramento

        {

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Backend APIs

Vou projetar e implementar um sistema backend robusto para a V11 com APIs otimizadas, focando em baixa latência, alta disponibilidade e resiliência. O sistema será construído com Node.js/Express, PostgreSQL, Redis e incluirá todas as práticas de engenharia sênior.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v11-backend/
├── src/
│   ├── api/
│   │   ├── contracts/
│   │   ├── controllers/
│   │   ├── middlewares/
│   │   └── routes/
│   ├── core/
│   │   ├── business/
│   │   ├── domain/
│   │   └── exceptions/
│   ├── infrastructure/
│   │   ├── database/
│   │   ├── cache/
│   │   ├── external/
│   │   └── monitoring/
│   ├── services/
│   │   ├── auth/
│   │   ├── payment/
│   │   ├── ai/
│   │   └── notification/
│   └── utils/
├── migrations/
├── tests/
├── docs/
├── .env.example
├── package.json
├── docker-compose.yml
└── index.js
```

## 2. Ponto de Entrada Principal

**src/index.js**
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const compression = require('compression');
const { createLogger } = require('./infrastructure/monitoring/logger');
const { initializeMetrics, metricsMiddleware } = require('./infrastructure/monitoring/metrics');
const { errorHandler } = require('./api/middlewares/error-handler');
const { requestLogger, correlationId } = require('./api/middlewares/logger');
const { rateLimiter } = require('./api/middlewares/rate-limiter');
const { healthCheck } = require('./api/controllers/health-controller');
const { initializeDatabase } = require('./infrastructure/database/connection');
const { initializeCache } = require('./infrastructure/cache/redis-client');
const { initializeQueues } = require('./infrastructure/queues/queue-manager');
const { initializeSockets } = require('./infrastructure/websockets/socket-manager');
const apiRoutes = require('./api/routes');
const swaggerUi = require('swagger-ui-express');
const swaggerSpec = require('./api/contracts/openapi-spec');

const app = express();
const logger = createLogger('server');
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// Security middleware
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"]
    }
  }
}));

// CORS configuration
app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : '*',
  credentials: true,
  methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'PATCH', 'OPTIONS'],
  allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Request-ID', 'X-Correlation-ID']
}));

// Compression
app.use(compression());

// Body parsing
app.use(express.json({ limit: '10mb' }));
app.use(express.urlencoded({ extended: true, limit: '10mb' }));

// Correlation ID middleware
app.use(correlationId);

// Request logging
app.use(requestLogger);

// Metrics middleware
app.use(metricsMiddleware);

// Rate limiting for public endpoints
app.use('/api/v1/public/', rateLimiter({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100 // limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
}));

// Health check endpoint (no auth, no rate limit)
app.get('/health', healthCheck);

// API Documentation
app.use('/api-docs', swaggerUi.serve, swaggerUi.setup(swaggerSpec));

// API Routes
app.use('/api/v1', apiRoutes);

// 404 handler
app.use((req, res) => {
  res.status(404).json({
    error: 'Not Found',
    message: `Cannot ${req.method} ${req.path}`,
    correlationId: req.correlationId
  });
});

// Global error handler
app.use(errorHandler);

// Graceful shutdown
const gracefulShutdown = async (signal) => {
  logger.info(`Received ${signal}. Starting graceful shutdown...`);
  
  try {
    // Close HTTP server
    server.close(() => {
      logger.info('HTTP server closed');
    });
    
    // Close database connections
    await require('./infrastructure/database/connection').close();
    
    // Close Redis connections
    await require('./infrastructure/cache/redis-client').close();
    
    // Close queues
    await require('./infrastructure/queues/queue-manager').close();
    
    logger.info('Graceful shutdown completed');
    process.exit(0);
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Error during graceful shutdown:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
};

// Initialize and start server
const startServer = async () => {
  try {
    // Initialize infrastructure
    await initializeDatabase();
    await initializeCache();
    await initializeQueues();
    await initializeMetrics();
    
    // Start server
    const server = app.listen(PORT, () => {
      logger.info(`DIYAPP V11 Backend running on port ${PORT}`);
      logger.info(`API Documentation available at http://localhost:${PORT}/api-docs`);
      logger.info(`Health check at http://localhost:${PORT}/health`);
    });
    
    // Configure graceful shutdown
    process.on('SIGTERM', () => gracefulShutdown('SIGTERM'));
    process.on('SIGINT', () => gracefulShutdown('SIGINT'));
    
    // Handle uncaught exceptions
    process.on('uncaughtException', (error) => {
      logger.error('Uncaught Exception:', error);
      gracefulShutdown('UNCAUGHT_EXCEPTION');
    });
    
    process.on('unhandledRejection', (reason, promise) => {
      logger.error('Unhandled Rejection at:', promise, 'reason:', reason);
      gracefulShutdown('UNHANDLED_REJECTION');
    });
    
    return server;
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Failed to start server:', error);
    process.exit(1);
  }
};

// Start the server if this file is run directly
if (require.main === module) {
  startServer();
}

module.exports = { app, startServer };
```
