```typescript
// src/design-system/ThemeProvider.tsx
import React, { createContext, useContext, useEffect, useState } from 'react';
import { tokens, ThemeTokens } from './tokens';

type ThemeMode = 'light' | 'dark';

interface ThemeContextType {
  mode: ThemeMode;
  toggleTheme: () => void;
  tokens: ThemeTokens;
}

const ThemeContext = createContext<ThemeContextType | undefined>(undefined);

export const useTheme = () => {
  const context = useContext(ThemeContext);
  if (!context) {
    throw new Error('useTheme must be used within ThemeProvider');
  }
  return context;
};

interface ThemeProviderProps {
  children: React.ReactNode;
  defaultMode?: ThemeMode;
}

export const ThemeProvider: React.FC<ThemeProviderProps> = ({
  children,
  defaultMode = 'light',
}) => {
  const [mode, setMode] = useState<ThemeMode>(() => {
    const saved = localStorage.getItem('theme-mode');
    return (saved as ThemeMode) || defaultMode;
  });

  useEffect(() => {
    localStorage.setItem('theme-mode', mode);
    document.documentElement.setAttribute('data-theme', mode);
  }, [mode]);

  const toggleTheme = () => {
    setMode((prev) => (prev === 'light' ? 'dark' : 'light'));
  };

  const value = {
    mode,
    toggleTheme,
    tokens,
  };

  return (
    <ThemeContext.Provider value={value}>
      <div className={`theme-${mode}`}>
        {children}
      </div>
    </ThemeContext.Provider>
  );
};
```

```typescript
// src/design-system/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { useTheme } from './ThemeProvider';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

export type ButtonVariant = 'primary' | 'secondary' | 'outline' | 'ghost' | 'danger';
export type ButtonSize = 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';

interface ButtonProps extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement> {
  variant?: ButtonVariant;
  size?: ButtonSize;
  isLoading?: boolean;
  fullWidth?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
}

const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(({
  children,
  variant = 'primary',
  size = 'md',
  isLoading = false,
  fullWidth = false,
  leftIcon,
  rightIcon,
  disabled,
  className = '',
  ...props
}, ref) => {
  const { mode } = useTheme();
  const isDark = mode === 'dark';

  const baseStyles = {
    display: 'inline-flex',
    alignItems: 'center',
    justifyContent: 'center',
    fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.semibold,
    fontFamily: tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans,
    border: '1px solid transparent',
    borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.md,
    cursor: disabled || isLoading ? 'not-allowed' : 'pointer',
    transition: 'all 150ms ease-in-out',
    width: fullWidth ? '100%' : 'auto',
    opacity: disabled ? 0.6 : 1,
  };

  const sizeStyles = {
    sm: {
      padding: `${tokens.spacing.xs} ${tokens.spacing.sm}`,
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
      gap: tokens.spacing.xs,
    },
    md: {
      padding: `${tokens.spacing.sm} ${tokens.spacing.md}`,
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.base,
      gap: tokens.spacing.sm,
    },
    lg: {
      padding: `${tokens.spacing.md} ${tokens.spacing.lg}`,
      fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.lg,
      gap: tokens.spacing.md,
    },
  };

  const variantStyles = {
    primary: {
      backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[600],
      color: tokens.colors.text.inverse,
      borderColor: tokens.colors.primary[600],
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[700],
        borderColor: tokens.colors.primary[700],
      },
      '&:focus-visible': {
        outline: '2px solid',
        outlineColor: tokens.colors.primary[300],
        outlineOffset: '2px',
      },
    },
    secondary: {
      backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.background['card-dark'] : tokens.colors.background.card,
      color: isDark ? tokens.colors.text.inverse : tokens.colors.text.primary,
      borderColor: isDark ? '#334155' : '#e2e8f0',
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? '#334155' : '#f1f5f9',
      },
    },
    outline: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: isDark ? tokens.colors.text.inverse : tokens.colors.text.primary,
      borderColor: isDark ? '#475569' : '#cbd5e1',
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.02)',
      },
    },
    ghost: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      color: isDark ? tokens.colors.text.inverse : tokens.colors.text.primary,
      borderColor: 'transparent',
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: isDark ? 'rgba(255,255,255,0.05)' : 'rgba(0,0,0,0.02)',
      },
    },
    danger: {
      backgroundColor: tokens.colors.error,
      color: tokens.colors.text.inverse,
      borderColor: tokens.colors.error,
      '&:hover:not(:disabled)': {
        backgroundColor: '#dc2626',
        borderColor: '#dc2626',
      },
    },
  };

  const styles = {
    ...baseStyles,
    ...sizeStyles[size],
    ...variantStyles[variant],
  };

  return (
    <button
      ref={ref}
      style={styles}
      disabled={disabled || isLoading}
      className={`button button-${variant} button-${size} ${className}`}
      aria-busy={isLoading}
      {...props}
    >
      {isLoading && (
        <span className="button-spinner" aria-hidden="true">
          <svg
            style={{
              width: '1em',
              height: '1em',
              animation: 'spin 1s linear infinite',
            }}
            viewBox="0 0 24 24"
          >
            <circle
              cx="12"
              cy="12"
              r="10"
              stroke="currentColor"
              strokeWidth="4"
              fill="none"
              strokeDasharray="31.4 31.4"
              strokeLinecap="round"
            />
          </svg>
        </span>
      )}
      {!isLoading && leftIcon && (
        <span className="button-icon-left" aria-hidden="true">
          {leftIcon}
        </span>
      )}
      <span className="button-content">{children}</span>
      {!isLoading && rightIcon && (
        <span className="button-icon-right" aria-hidden="true">
          {rightIcon}
        </span>
      )}
    </button>
  );
});

Button.displayName = 'Button';

export default Button;
```

```typescript
// src/design-system/Card.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, HTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { useTheme } from './ThemeProvider';
import { tokens } from './tokens';

interface CardProps extends HTMLAttributes<HTMLDivElement> {
  variant?: 'default' | 'elevated' | 'outline';
  padding?: 'none' | 'sm' | 'md' | 'lg';
}

const Card = forwardRef<HTMLDivElement, CardProps>(({
  children,
  variant = 'default',
  padding = 'md',
  className = '',
  ...props
}, ref) => {
  const { mode } = useTheme();
  const isDark = mode === 'dark';

  const baseStyles = {
    borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.lg,
    fontFamily: tokens.typography.fontFamily.sans,
    transition: 'all 200ms ease',
  };

  const variantStyles = {
    default: {
      backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.background['card-dark'] : tokens.colors.background.card,
      border: `1px solid ${isDark ? '#334155' : '#e2e8f0'}`,
    },
    elevated: {
      backgroundColor: isDark ? tokens.colors.background['card-dark'] : tokens.colors.background.card,
      border: `1px solid ${isDark ? '#334155' : '#e2e8f0'}`,
      boxShadow: tokens.shadows.lg,
      '&:hover': {
        boxShadow: tokens.shadows.xl,
        transform: 'translateY(-2px)',
      },
    },
    outline: {
      backgroundColor: 'transparent',
      border: `2px dashed ${isDark ? '#475569' : '#cbd5e1'}`,
    },
  };

  const paddingStyles = {
    none: { padding: 0 },
    sm: { padding: tokens.spacing.sm },
    md: { padding: tokens.spacing.md },
    lg: { padding: tokens.spacing.lg },
  };

  const styles = {
    ...baseStyles,
    ...variantStyles[variant],
    ...paddingStyles[padding],
  };

  return (
    <div
      ref={ref}
      style={styles}
      className={`card card-${variant} ${className}`}
      {...props}
    >
      {children}
    </div>
  );
});

Card.displayName = 'Card';

export default Card;
```

```typescript
// src/features/premium/components/PremiumFeatureCard.tsx
import React from 'react';
import Card from '../../design-system/Card';
import Button from '../../design-system/Button';
import { useTheme } from '../../design-system/ThemeProvider';
import { tokens } from '../../design-system/tokens';

interface PremiumFeatureCardProps {
  title: string;
  description: string;
  icon: React.ReactNode;
  price: string;
  period?: 'monthly' | 'yearly';
  features: string[];
  isPopular?: boolean;
  onSubscribe: () => void;
  isLoading?: boolean;
}

const PremiumFeatureCard: React.FC<PremiumFeatureCardProps> = ({
  title,
  description,
  icon,
  price,
  period = 'monthly',
  features,
  isPopular = false,
  onSubscribe,
  isLoading = false,
}) => {
  const { mode } = useTheme();
  const isDark = mode === 'dark';

  return (
    <Card
      variant={isPopular ? 'elevated' : 'default'}
      padding="lg"
      style={{
        position: 'relative',
        overflow: 'hidden',
        borderColor: isPopular ? tokens.colors.primary[500] : undefined,
        borderWidth: isPopular ? '2px' : undefined,
      }}
    >
      {isPopular && (
        <div
          style={{
            position: 'absolute',
            top: 0,
            right: 0,
            backgroundColor: tokens.colors.primary[500],
            color: tokens.colors.text.inverse,
            padding: `${tokens.spacing.xs} ${tokens.spacing.lg}`,
            fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
            fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.bold,
            borderBottomLeftRadius: tokens.borderRadius.md,
            textTransform: 'uppercase',
            letterSpacing: '0.05em',
          }}
        >
          Popular
        </div>
      )}

      <div
        style={{
          display: 'flex',
          flexDirection: 'column',
          gap: tokens.spacing.md,
          paddingTop: isPopular ? tokens.spacing.xl : 0,
        }}
      >
        <div
          style={{
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'center',
            gap: tokens.spacing.sm,
          }}
        >
          <div
            style={{
              width: '48px',
              height: '48px',
              borderRadius: tokens.borderRadius.md,
              backgroundColor: isDark
                ? 'rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.1)'
                : 'rgba(14, 165, 233, 0.05)',
              display: 'flex',
              alignItems: 'center',
              justifyContent: 'center',
              color: tokens.colors.primary[500],
            }}
          >
            {icon}
          </div>
          <div>
            <h3
              style={{
                fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.xl,
                fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.bold,
                color: isDark ? tokens.colors.text.inverse : tokens.colors.text.primary,
                margin: 0,
              }}
            >
              {title}
            </h3>
            <p
              style={{
                fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
                color: tokens.colors.text.secondary,
                margin: 0,
                marginTop: tokens.spacing.xs,
              }}
            >
              {description}
            </p>
          </div>
        </div>

        <div
          style={{
            display: 'flex',
            alignItems: 'baseline',
            gap: tokens.spacing.xs,
          }}
        >
          <span
            style={{
              fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize['3xl'],
              fontWeight: tokens.typography.fontWeight.bold,
              color: isDark ? tokens.colors.text.inverse : tokens.colors.text.primary,
            }}
          >
            {price}
          </span>
          <span
            style={{
              fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
              color: tokens.colors.text.secondary,
            }}
          >
            /{period === 'monthly' ? 'month' : 'year'}
          </span>
        </div>

        <ul
          style={{
            listStyle: 'none',
            padding: 0,
            margin: 0,
            display: 'flex',
            flexDirection: 'column',
            gap: tokens.spacing.sm,
          }}
        >
          {features.map((feature, index) => (
            <li
              key={index}
              style={{
                display: 'flex',
                alignItems: 'center',
                gap: tokens.spacing.sm,
                fontSize: tokens.typography.fontSize.sm,
                color: isDark ? tokens.colors.text.inverse : tokens.colors.text.primary,
              }}
            >
              <svg
                style={{
                  width: '16px',
                  height: '16px',
                  color: tokens.colors.success,
                  flexShrink

### [Sessão Paralela: SRE]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Infraestrutura Cloud Auto-Healing

## Arquitetura de Infraestrutura Cloud para V11

### 1. Estrutura do Projeto
```
diyapp-v11-infra/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   ├── outputs.tf
│   ├── kubernetes.tf
│   └── monitoring.tf
├── kubernetes/
│   ├── namespaces/
│   ├── deployments/
│   ├── services/
│   ├── configmaps/
│   ├── secrets/
│   ├── hpa/
│   └── istio/
├── scripts/
│   ├── deploy.sh
│   ├── health-check.sh
│   └── chaos-test.sh
├── monitoring/
│   ├── prometheus/
│   ├── grafana/
│   └── alerts/
├── logs/
│   └── audit/
├── index.html
└── README.md
```

### 2. Terraform - Provisionamento Cloud (main.tf)

```hcl
# terraform/main.tf
terraform {
  required_version = ">= 1.5.0"
  required_providers {
    google = {
      source  = "hashicorp/google"
      version = "~> 5.0"
    }
    kubernetes = {
      source  = "hashicorp/kubernetes"
      version = "~> 2.23"
    }
    helm = {
      source  = "hashicorp/helm"
      version = "~> 2.11"
    }
  }
  backend "gcs" {
    bucket = "diyapp-v11-tf-state"
    prefix = "terraform/state"
  }
}

provider "google" {
  project = var.project_id
  region  = var.region
  zone    = var.zone
}

# VPC Network
resource "google_compute_network" "v11_network" {
  name                    = "v11-network"
  auto_create_subnetworks = false
  routing_mode           = "REGIONAL"
}

resource "google_compute_subnetwork" "v11_subnet" {
  name          = "v11-subnet"
  ip_cidr_range = "10.0.0.0/16"
  region        = var.region
  network       = google_compute_network.v11_network.id
  
  secondary_ip_range {
    range_name    = "pods-range"
    ip_cidr_range = "10.1.0.0/16"
  }
  
  secondary_ip_range {
    range_name    = "services-range"
    ip_cidr_range = "10.2.0.0/20"
  }
}

# GKE Cluster
resource "google_container_cluster" "v11_cluster" {
  name     = "diyapp-v11-cluster"
  location = var.region
  
  remove_default_node_pool = true
  initial_node_count       = 1
  
  network    = google_compute_network.v11_network.name
  subnetwork = google_compute_subnetwork.v11_subnet.name
  
  ip_allocation_policy {
    cluster_secondary_range_name  = "pods-range"
    services_secondary_range_name = "services-range"
  }
  
  private_cluster_config {
    enable_private_nodes    = true
    enable_private_endpoint = false
    master_ipv4_cidr_block  = "172.16.0.0/28"
  }
  
  master_authorized_networks_config {
    cidr_blocks {
      cidr_block   = "0.0.0.0/0"
      display_name = "all"
    }
  }
  
  release_channel {
    channel = "REGULAR"
  }
  
  workload_identity_config {
    workload_pool = "${var.project_id}.svc.id.goog"
  }
  
  addons_config {
    horizontal_pod_autoscaling {
      disabled = false
    }
    http_load_balancing {
      disabled = false
    }
    istio_config {
      disabled = false
      auth     = "AUTH_MUTUAL_TLS"
    }
  }
  
  maintenance_policy {
    daily_maintenance_window {
      start_time = "03:00"
    }
  }
}

# Node Pools
resource "google_container_node_pool" "core_nodes" {
  name       = "core-node-pool"
  location   = var.region
  cluster    = google_container_cluster.v11_cluster.name
  
  autoscaling {
    min_node_count = 3
    max_node_count = 10
  }
  
  management {
    auto_repair  = true
    auto_upgrade = true
  }
  
  node_config {
    machine_type = "e2-standard-4"
    disk_size_gb = 100
    disk_type    = "pd-ssd"
    
    oauth_scopes = [
      "https://www.googleapis.com/auth/cloud-platform"
    ]
    
    workload_metadata_config {
      mode = "GKE_METADATA"
    }
    
    labels = {
      role = "core"
    }
    
    taint {
      key    = "role"
      value  = "core"
      effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
    }
  }
}

resource "google_container_node_pool" "ai_nodes" {
  name       = "ai-node-pool"
  location   = var.region
  cluster    = google_container_cluster.v11_cluster.name
  
  autoscaling {
    min_node_count = 2
    max_node_count = 6
  }
  
  management {
    auto_repair  = true
    auto_upgrade = true
  }
  
  node_config {
    machine_type = "n2-standard-8"
    disk_size_gb = 200
    disk_type    = "pd-ssd"
    
    oauth_scopes = [
      "https://www.googleapis.com/auth/cloud-platform"
    ]
    
    workload_metadata_config {
      mode = "GKE_METADATA"
    }
    
    labels = {
      role = "ai"
    }
    
    taint {
      key    = "role"
      value  = "ai"
      effect = "NO_SCHEDULE"
    }
  }
}

# Cloud SQL for PostgreSQL
resource "google_sql_database_instance" "v11_postgres" {
  name             = "diyapp-v11-postgres"
  database_version = "POSTGRES_15"
  region           = var.region
  
  settings {
    tier              = "db-custom-4-16384"
    disk_size         = 100
    disk_type         = "PD_SSD"
    availability_type = "REGIONAL"
    
    backup_configuration {
      enabled    = true
      start_time = "02:00"
    }
    
    maintenance_window {
      day  = 7
      hour = 4
    }
    
    ip_configuration {
      ipv4_enabled    = false
      private_network = google_compute_network.v11_network.id
    }
  }
  
  deletion_protection = false
}

resource "google_sql_database" "v11_database" {
  name     = "diyapp_v11"
  instance = google_sql_database_instance.v11_postgres.name
}

resource "google_sql_user" "v11_user" {
  name     = "diyapp_user"
  instance = google_sql_database_instance.v11_postgres.name
  password = random_password.db_password.result
}

# Redis Memorystore
resource "google_redis_instance" "v11_redis" {
  name           = "diyapp-v11-redis"
  tier           = "STANDARD_HA"
  memory_size_gb = 10
  region         = var.region
  
  authorized_network = google_compute_network.v11_network.id
  
  redis_version = "REDIS_7_0"
  display_name  = "DIYApp V11 Cache"
  
  persistence_config {
    persistence_mode = "RDB"
    rdb_snapshot_period = "TWELVE_HOURS"
  }
  
  maintenance_policy {
    weekly_maintenance_window {
      day = "SUNDAY"
      start_time {
        hours   = 2
        minutes = 0
      }
    }
  }
}

# Cloud Storage for ML Models
resource "google_storage_bucket" "ml_models" {
  name          = "${var.project_id}-ml-models"
  location      = var.region
  force_destroy = false
  
  uniform_bucket_level_access = true
  
  versioning {
    enabled = true
  }
  
  lifecycle_rule {
    condition {
      age = 30
    }
    action {
      type = "Delete"
    }
  }
}

# Service Accounts
resource "google_service_account" "v11_sa" {
  account_id   = "diyapp-v11-sa"
  display_name = "DIYApp V11 Service Account"
}

resource "google_project_iam_member" "v11_sa_roles" {
  for_each = toset([
    "roles/cloudsql.client",
    "roles/redis.editor",
    "roles/storage.objectAdmin",
    "roles/logging.logWriter",
    "roles/monitoring.metricWriter",
    "roles/stackdriver.resourceMetadata.writer"
  ])
  
  project = var.project_id
  role    = each.value
  member  = "serviceAccount:${google_service_account.v11_sa.email}"
}

# Random password for DB
resource "random_password" "db_password" {
  length  = 32
  special = true
}

output "cluster_endpoint" {
  value = google_container_cluster.v11_cluster.endpoint
}

output "db_connection_name" {
  value = google_sql_database_instance.v11_postgres.connection_name
}

output "redis_host" {
  value = google_redis_instance.v11_redis.host
}
```

### 3. Kubernetes Manifests - Deployments Auto-Healing

```yaml
# kubernetes/namespaces/namespaces.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: diyapp-core
  labels:
    name: diyapp-core
    istio-injection: enabled
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: diyapp-ai
  labels:
    name: diyapp-ai
    istio-injection: enabled
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: monitoring
  labels:
    name: monitoring
```

```yaml
# kubernetes/deployments/api-deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp-core
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
    version: v11
    component: api
spec:
  replicas: 3
  minReadySeconds: 30
  revisionHistoryLimit: 10
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp-api
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp-api
        version: v11
        component: api
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "9090"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
        sidecar.istio.io/inject: "true"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: diyapp-sa
      nodeSelector:
        role: core
      tolerations:
      - key: "role"
        operator: "Equal"
        value: "core"
        effect: "NoSchedule"
      containers:
      - name: api
        image: gcr.io/${PROJECT_ID}/diyapp-api:v11
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8080
          name: http
        - containerPort: 9090
          name: metrics
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: LOG_LEVEL
          value: "info"
        - name: DB_HOST
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: db-secrets
              key: host
        - name: DB_PASSWORD
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: db-secrets
              key: password
        - name: REDIS_HOST
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: redis-secrets
              key: host
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "2Gi"
            cpu: "1000m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 8080
            scheme: HTTP
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 8080
            scheme: HTTP
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 1
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /startup
            port: 8080
            scheme: HTTP
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
          failureThreshold: 30
        lifecycle:
          preStop:
            exec:
              command: ["/bin/sh", "-c", "sleep 30"]
      - name: istio-proxy
        image: auto
        resources:
          requests:
            cpu: 100m
            memory: 128Mi
          limits:
            cpu: 2000m
            memory: 1024Mi
        securityContext:
          runAsUser: 1337
          runAsGroup: 1337
---
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-hpa
  namespace: diyapp-core
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: diyapp-api
  minReplicas: 3
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 70
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: memory
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 80
  - type: Pods
    pods:
      metric:
        name: http_requests_per_second
      target:
        type: AverageValue
        averageValue: 100
  behavior:
    scaleDown:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 300
      policies:
      - type: Percent
        value: 50
        periodSeconds: 60
    scaleUp:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 60
      policies:
      - type: Percent
        value: 100
        periodSeconds: 30
```

```yaml
# kubernetes/deployments/llm-gateway-deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: llm-gateway
  namespace: diyapp-ai
  labels:
    app: llm-gateway
    version: v11
    component: ai
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: llm-gateway
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: llm-gateway
        version: v11
        component: ai
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "9091"
        sidecar.istio.io/inject: "true"
    spec:
      serviceAccountName: diyapp-sa
      nodeSelector:
        role: ai
      tolerations:
      - key: "role"
        operator: "Equal"
        value: "ai"
        effect: "NoSchedule"
      containers:
      - name: llm-gateway
        image: gcr.io/${PROJECT_ID}/llm-gateway:v11
        imagePullPolicy: Always
        ports:
        - containerPort: 8081
          name: http
        - containerPort: 9091
          name: metrics
        env:
        - name: OPENAI_API_KEY
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: llm-secrets
              key: openai-api-key
        - name: ANTHROPIC_API_KEY
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: llm-secrets
              key: anthropic-api-key
        - name: GOOGLE_API_KEY
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: llm-secrets
              key: google-api-key
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "2Gi"
            cpu: "1000m"
            nvidia.com/gpu: 1
          limits:
            memory: "8Gi"
            cpu: "4000m"
            nvidia.com/gpu: 1
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 8081
            scheme: HTTP
          initialDelaySeconds: 60
          periodSeconds: 15
          timeoutSeconds: 10
        readinessProbe:
          exec:
            command:
            - /bin/sh
            - -c
            - curl -f http://localhost:8081/ready || exit 1
          initialDelaySeconds: 20
          periodSeconds: 10
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /startup
            port: 8081
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          failureThreshold: 30
        volumeMounts:
        - name: model-cache
          mountPath: /cache/models
      volumes:
      - name: model-cache
        emptyDir: {}
---
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: llm-gateway-hpa
  namespace: diyapp-ai
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: llm-gateway
  minReplicas: 2
  maxReplicas: 6
  metrics:
  - type: Resource

  "name": "diyapp-v11-tests",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "description": "Test suite for DIYAPP Evolution V11 Core",
  "scripts": {
    "test:e2e": "playwright test",
    "test:e2e:ui": "playwright test --ui",
    "test:e2e:headed": "playwright test --headed",
    "test:e2e:auth": "playwright test authentication.spec.js",
    "test:e2e:projects": "playwright test project-management.spec.js",
    "test:e2e:ai": "playwright test ai-features.spec.js",
    "test:performance": "k6 run k6-load-tests/smoke-test.js",
    "test:load": "k6 run k6-load-tests/load-test.js",
    "test:stress": "k6 run k6-load-tests/stress-test.js",
    "test:spike": "k6 run k6-load-tests/spike-test.js",
    "test:all": "npm run test:e2e && npm run test:load",
    "report:generate": "playwright show-report",
    "report:performance": "node generate-performance-report.js"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "@playwright/test": "^1.40.0",
    "@types/node": "^20.0.0",

    "fs-extra": "^11.0.0",

## 3. CONFIGURAÇÃO PLAYWRIGHT

```javascript
// playwright.config.js
const { defineConfig, devices } = require('@playwright/test');

module.exports = defineConfig({
  testDir: './e2e-tests/specs',
  fullyParallel: true,
  forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI,
  retries: process.env.CI ? 2 : 1,
  workers: process.env.CI ? 4 : 3,
  reporter: [
    ['html', { outputFolder: 'reports/e2e/html' }],
    ['json', { outputFile: 'reports/e2e/results.json' }],
    ['junit', { outputFile: 'reports/e2e/junit.xml' }],
    ['list']
  ],
  
  use: {
    baseURL: process.env.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
    trace: 'on-first-retry',
    screenshot: 'only-on-failure',
    video: 'retain-on-failure',
    actionTimeout: 15000,
    navigationTimeout: 30000,
  },

  projects: [
    {
      name: 'chromium',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Chrome'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'firefox',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Firefox'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'webkit',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Safari'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'Mobile Chrome',
      use: { ...devices['Pixel 5'] },
    },
    {
      name: 'Mobile Safari',
      use: { ...devices['iPhone 12'] },
    },
  ],

  timeout: 60000,
  expect: {
    timeout: 10000
  }
});
```

## 4. TESTES E2E - ESPECIFICAÇÕES

### 4.1 Autenticação e Segurança

```javascript
// e2e-tests/specs/authentication.spec.js
const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');
const { LoginPage } = require('../pages/LoginPage');

test.describe('Autenticação e Segurança V11', () => {
  let loginPage;

  test.beforeEach(async ({ page }) => {
    loginPage = new LoginPage(page);
    await loginPage.navigate();
  });

  test('CT-001: Login bem-sucedido com credenciais válidas', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const credentials = {
      email: 'test@diyapp.com',
      password: 'SecurePass123!'
    };

    // Act
    await loginPage.login(credentials);
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(/dashboard/);
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="user-menu"]')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="welcome-message"]')).toContainText('Bem-vindo');
  });

  test('CT-002: Login falha com credenciais inválidas', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const invalidCredentials = {
      email: 'invalid@test.com',
      password: 'wrongpass'
    };

    // Act
    await loginPage.login(invalidCredentials);
    
    // Assert
    await expect(loginPage.errorMessage).toBeVisible();
    await expect(loginPage.errorMessage).toContainText('Credenciais inválidas');
    await expect(page).not.toHaveURL(/dashboard/);
  });

  test('CT-003: Bloqueio após 5 tentativas falhas', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const wrongPassword = 'wrongpass';
    
    // Act
    for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
      await loginPage.login({ email: 'test@diyapp.com', password: wrongPassword });
      await expect(loginPage.errorMessage).toBeVisible();
    }
    
    // Assert
    await loginPage.login({ email: 'test@diyapp.com', password: 'SecurePass123!' });
    await expect(loginPage.errorMessage).toContainText('Conta temporariamente bloqueada');
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="reset-password-link"]')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('CT-004: Recuperação de senha funcional', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const testEmail = 'test@diyapp.com';
    
    // Act
    await loginPage.clickForgotPassword();
    await loginPage.fillRecoveryEmail(testEmail);
    await loginPage.submitRecovery();
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="recovery-success"]')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="recovery-success"]'))
      .toContainText('Email de recuperação enviado');
  });

  test('CT-005: Logout seguro', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    await loginPage.login({
      email: 'test@diyapp.com',
      password: 'SecurePass123!'
    });
    
    // Act
    await page.locator('[data-testid="user-menu"]').click();
    await page.locator('[data-testid="logout-button"]').click();
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(/login/);
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="login-form"]')).toBeVisible();
    
    // Tentar acessar página protegida sem autenticação
    await page.goto('/dashboard');
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(/login/);
  });

  test('CT-006: Sessão expira após 30 minutos de inatividade', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    await loginPage.login({
      email: 'test@diyapp.com',
      password: 'SecurePass123!'
    });
    
    // Act - Simular 31 minutos de espera
    await page.evaluate(() => {
      localStorage.setItem('lastActivity', Date.now() - 31 * 60 * 1000);
    });
    
    await page.reload();
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(/login/);
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="session-expired"]')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('CT-007: Autenticação OAuth com Google', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    await loginPage.clickGoogleLogin();
    
    // Act - Mock do fluxo OAuth
    await page.route('**/oauth/google/callback*', route => {
      route.fulfill({
        status: 200,
        contentType: 'application/json',
        body: JSON.stringify({
          token: 'mock-oauth-token',
          user: { email: 'google@test.com', name: 'Google User' }
        })
      });
    });
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(/dashboard/);
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="user-email"]')).toContainText('google@test.com');
  });

  test('CT-008: Autenticação com 2FA', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    await loginPage.login({
      email: '2fa@diyapp.com',
      password: 'SecurePass123!'
    });
    
    // Assert - Deve mostrar tela de 2FA
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="2fa-form"]')).toBeVisible();
    
    // Act - Inserir código válido
    await page.fill('[data-testid="2fa-code"]', '123456');
    await page.click('[data-testid="2fa-submit"]');
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(/dashboard/);
  });

  test('CT-009: Proteção contra XSS no login', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const xssPayload = '<script>alert("XSS")</script>';
    
    // Act
    await loginPage.fillEmail(xssPayload);
    await loginPage.fillPassword(xssPayload);
    await loginPage.submit();
    
    // Assert - Não deve executar script
    const pageContent = await page.content();
    expect(pageContent).not.toContain('<script>alert');
    // Deve mostrar erro de validação
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="validation-error"]')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('CT-010: Rate limiting no endpoint de login', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const requests = [];
    
    // Act - Fazer 100 requisições rápidas
    for (let i = 0; i < 100; i++) {
      const request = page.waitForResponse('**/api/auth/login');
      await loginPage.submit();
      requests.push(request);
    }
    
    const responses = await Promise.all(requests);
    const statusCodes = responses.map(r => r.status());
    
    // Assert - Algumas devem retornar 429 (Too Many Requests)
    expect(statusCodes.filter(code => code === 429).length).toBeGreaterThan(0);
  });
});
```

### 4.2 Gerenciamento de Projetos

```javascript
// e2e-tests/specs/project-management.spec.js
const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');
const { ProjectPage } = require('../pages/ProjectPage');

test.describe('Gerenciamento de Projetos V11', () => {
  let projectPage;

  test.beforeEach(async ({ page }) => {
    // Login antes de cada teste
    const loginPage = new (require('../pages/LoginPage'))(page);
    await loginPage.navigate();
    await loginPage.login({
      email: 'test@diyapp.com',
      password: 'SecurePass123!'
    });
    
    projectPage = new ProjectPage(page);
    await projectPage.navigate();
  });

  test('CT-011: Criar novo projeto com sucesso', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const projectData = {
      name: 'Meu Novo Projeto',
      description: 'Descrição do projeto de teste',
      template: 'react-typescript'
    };

    // Act
    await projectPage.createProject(projectData);
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="project-title"]')).toContainText(projectData.name);
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="project-description"]')).toContainText(projectData.description);
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="project-status"]')).toContainText('Ativo');
  });

  test('CT-012: Validação de campos obrigatórios', async ({ page }) => {
    // Act - Tentar criar projeto sem nome
    await projectPage.clickCreateProject();
    await projectPage.fillDescription('Descrição sem nome');
    await projectPage.submitProject();
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="name-error"]')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="name-error"]')).toContainText('obrigatório');
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="project-form"]')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('CT-013: Editar projeto existente', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const projectId = 'test-project-123';
    const updatedName = 'Projeto Atualizado';
    
    // Act
    await projectPage.openProject(projectId);
    await projectPage.clickEdit();
    await projectPage.updateProjectName(updatedName);
    await projectPage.saveChanges();
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="project-title"]')).toContainText(updatedName);
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="update-success"]')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('CT-014: Excluir projeto com confirmação', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const projectId = 'project-to-delete';
    
    // Act
    await projectPage.openProject(projectId);
    await projectPage.clickDelete();
    
    // Assert - Modal de confirmação deve aparecer
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="delete-confirmation"]')).toBeVisible();
    
    // Act - Confirmar exclusão
    await page.click('[data-testid="confirm-delete"]');
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page).toHaveURL(/projects/);
    await expect(page.locator(`[data-testid="project-${projectId}"]`)).not.toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="delete-success"]')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('CT-015: Cancelar exclusão de projeto', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const projectId = 'project-to-keep';
    
    // Act
    await projectPage.openProject(projectId);
    await projectPage.clickDelete();
    await page.click('[data-testid="cancel-delete"]');
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="delete-confirmation"]')).not.toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('[data-testid="project-title"]')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('CT-016: Buscar projetos por nome', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const searchTerm = 'React';
    
    // Act
    await projectPage.searchProjects(searchTerm);
    
    // Assert
    const projectCards = await page.locator('[data-testid^="project-card-"]').all();
    for (const card of projectCards) {
      const title = await card.locator('[data-testid="project-name"]').textContent();
      expect(title.toLowerCase()).toContain(searchTerm.toLowerCase());
    }
  });

  test('CT-017: Filtrar projetos por status', async ({ page }) => {
    // Act
    await projectPage.filterByStatus('active');
    
    // Assert
    const statusBadges = await page.locator('[data-testid="project-status"]').all();
    for (const badge of statusBadges) {
      await expect(badge).toContainText('Ativo');
    }
    
    // Act - Mudar filtro
    await projectPage.filterByStatus('archived');
    
    // Assert
    const archivedBadges = await page.locator('[data-testid="project-status"]').all();
    for (const badge of archivedBadges) {
      await expect(badge).toContainText('Arquivado');
    }
  });

  test('CT-018: Ordenar projetos por data de criação', async ({ page }) => {
    // Act
    await projectPage.sortBy('createdAt');
    
    // Assert - Verificar ordem
    const dates = [];
    const dateElements = await page.locator('[data-testid="project-created"]').all();
    
    for (const element of dateElements) {
      const dateText = await element.textContent();
      dates.push(new Date(dateText));
    }
    
    // Verificar se está em ordem decrescente
    for (let i = 0; i < dates.length - 1; i++) {
      expect(dates[i] >= dates[i + 1]).toBeTruthy();
    }
  });

  test('CT-019: Paginação de projetos', async ({

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Threat Modeling Analysis

## 1. Análise de Arquitetura V11

### 1.1 Componentes Principais Identificados
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                     DIYAPP V11 Architecture                 │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│ 1. Frontend Web App (React/Vue + PWA)                       │
│ 2. API Gateway (Node.js/Express)                            │
│ 3. Microserviços:                                           │
│    - Auth Service (JWT, OAuth2, MFA)                        │
│    - User Profile Service                                   │
│    - Content Service (DIY Projects)                         │
│    - Chat/Community Service                                 │
│    - Payment Service                                        │
│    - AI Assistant Service (LLM Integration)                 │
│ 4. Banco de Dados:                                          │
│    - PostgreSQL (dados estruturados)                        │
│    - Redis (cache, sessões)                                 │
│    - MongoDB (conteúdo não estruturado)                     │
│ 5. Serviços Externos:                                       │
│    - WhatsApp API (Baileys)                                 │
│    - Email Service (SendGrid/Resend)                        │
│    - Storage (S3/Cloud Storage)                             │
│    - CDN (assets estáticos)                                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

## 2. Threat Modeling STRIDE por Componente

### 2.1 API Gateway
```javascript
// security/gateway-threats.js
/**
 * STRIDE Analysis - API Gateway
 */
const gatewayThreats = {
  spoofing: [
    {
      id: "GATEWAY-SPOOF-001",
      threat: "Token JWT falsificado ou roubado",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "Validação assinatura JWT com chave RSA 2048+",
        "Verificação de issuer e audience",
        "Blacklist de tokens revogados no Redis",
        "Rate limiting por IP e usuário"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    },
    {
      id: "GATEWAY-SPOOF-002",
      threat: "API Keys vazadas de serviços externos",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Baixo",
      controls: [
        "Rotação automática de chaves a cada 90 dias",
        "Armazenamento em HashiCorp Vault/AWS Secrets Manager",
        "Log de uso de chaves com alerta de anomalia"
      ],
      sla: "Alto"
    }
  ],
  
  tampering: [
    {
      id: "GATEWAY-TAMP-001",
      threat: "Manipulação de requests no client-side",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Alto",
      controls: [
        "Validação de schema com Zod/Joi em todas as entradas",
        "Content-Type enforcement",
        "Request signing para operações críticas"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    }
  ],
  
  repudiation: [
    {
      id: "GATEWAY-REPU-001",
      threat: "Negação de operações administrativas",
      impact: "Médio",
      probability: "Baixo",
      controls: [
        "Log estruturado com correlation ID",
        "Armazenamento imutável em SIEM",
        "Assinatura digital de logs críticos"
      ],
      sla: "Médio"
    }
  ],
  
  informationDisclosure: [
    {
      id: "GATEWAY-INFO-001",
      threat: "Vazamento de dados sensíveis em logs",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "Mascaramento automático de PII em logs",
        "Redaction de tokens, emails, CPF/CNPJ",
        "Níveis de log diferenciados por ambiente"
      ],
      sla: "Alto"
    }
  ],
  
  denialOfService: [
    {
      id: "GATEWAY-DOS-001",
      threat: "Ataque DDoS na API Gateway",
      impact: "Crítico",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "WAF com regras OWASP Top 10",
        "Rate limiting por IP: 100 req/min",
        "Rate limiting por usuário: 1000 req/min",
        "Circuit breaker para serviços downstream"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    }
  ],
  
  elevationOfPrivilege: [
    {
      id: "GATEWAY-ELEV-001",
      threat: "Bypass de autorização via parâmetros manipulados",
      impact: "Crítico",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "Policy-based access control (PBAC)",
        "Verificação de ownership em todos os endpoints",
        "Validação de escopo de token JWT"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    }
  ]
};
```

### 2.2 Auth Service
```javascript
// security/auth-threats.js
/**
 * STRIDE Analysis - Authentication Service
 */
const authThreats = {
  spoofing: [
    {
      id: "AUTH-SPOOF-001",
      threat: "Credential stuffing com senhas vazadas",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Alto",
      controls: [
        "MFA obrigatório para todas as contas",
        "HaveIBeenPwned API integration",
        "Detecção de IPs suspeitos (TOR, data centers)",
        "Delay progressivo após falhas"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    },
    {
      id: "AUTH-SPOOF-002", 
      threat: "Session hijacking via XSS",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "HttpOnly, Secure, SameSite cookies",
        "Token binding (jti claim vinculado ao device fingerprint)",
        "Reautenticação para operações sensíveis"
      ],
      sla: "Alto"
    }
  ],
  
  tampering: [
    {
      id: "AUTH-TAMP-001",
      threat: "Manipulação de fluxo OAuth2",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "PKCE obrigatório para todos os clients",
        "Validação de redirect_uri exata",
        "State parameter com HMAC"
      ],
      sla: "Alto"
    }
  ],
  
  informationDisclosure: [
    {
      id: "AUTH-INFO-001",
      threat: "Enumeração de usuários via timing attack",
      impact: "Médio",
      probability: "Baixo",
      controls: [
        "Tempo de resposta constante para login válido/inválido",
        "Rate limiting agressivo em endpoints de recuperação",
        "CAPTCHA após 3 tentativas"
      ],
      sla: "Médio"
    }
  ]
};
```

### 2.3 AI Assistant Service (LLM Integration)
```javascript
// security/ai-threats.js
/**
 * STRIDE Analysis - AI Assistant Service
 * Riscos específicos de LLM/IA
 */
const aiThreats = {
  spoofing: [
    {
      id: "AI-SPOOF-001",
      threat: "Prompt injection para impersonation",
      impact: "Crítico",
      probability: "Alto",
      controls: [
        "Separação rígida: system prompt ≠ user input",
        "Validação de intenção antes da execução",
        "User context isolation por tenant"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    }
  ],
  
  tampering: [
    {
      id: "AI-TAMP-001",
      threat: "Manipulação de output do modelo para XSS",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "Sanitização HTML obrigatória (DOMPurify)",
        "Content Security Policy estrita",
        "Escape de caracteres especiais"
      ],
      sla: "Alto"
    }
  ],
  
  informationDisclosure: [
    {
      id: "AI-INFO-001",
      threat: "Data exfiltration via prompt engineering",
      impact: "Crítico",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "Não incluir dados sensíveis no contexto do LLM",
        "PII redaction antes do envio ao modelo",
        "Log de prompts suspeitos para análise"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    },
    {
      id: "AI-INFO-002",
      threat: "Vazamento de system prompt",
      impact: "Médio",
      probability: "Alto",
      controls: [
        "Prompt design resistente a extração",
        "Monitoramento de outputs que repetem o prompt",
        "Rotação periódica de system prompts"
      ],
      sla: "Médio"
    }
  ],
  
  denialOfService: [
    {
      id: "AI-DOS-001",
      threat: "Prompt flooding para esgotar créditos da API",
      impact: "Alto",
      probability: "Baixo",
      controls: [
        "Rate limiting por usuário: 50 req/hora",
        "Custo máximo por sessão: $0.50",
        "Circuit breaker na integração com OpenAI/Anthropic"
      ],
      sla: "Alto"
    }
  ],
  
  elevationOfPrivilege: [
    {
      id: "AI-ELEV-001",
      threat: "Indirect prompt injection via conteúdo externo",
      impact: "Crítico",
      probability: "Médio",
      controls: [
        "Sanitização de URLs e arquivos antes do processamento",
        "Sandbox para execução de código gerado",
        "Approval workflow para ações destrutivas"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    }
  ]
};
```

// security/whatsapp-threats.js
/**

const whatsappThreats = {

        "Access logging para todas as consultas"
      ],
      sla: "Crítico"
    }

      threat: "Negação de envio/recebimento de mensagem",

      probability: "Baixo",

      ],

## 3. Requisitos de Segurança por Categoria

### 3.1 Autenticação e Autorização
```javascript
// security/requirements/auth-requirements.js
/**
 * Requisitos de Segurança - Autenticação
 */
const authRequirements = {
  mandatory: {
    mfa: {
      description: "MFA obrigatório para todas as contas",
      implementation: "TOTP (Google Authenticator) ou WebAuthn",
      exceptions: "Nenhuma",
      validation: "Teste automatizado de fluxo MFA"
    },
    
    tokenManagement: {
      description: "Gestão segura de tokens JWT",
      implementation: [
        "Access token: 15 minutos expiry",
        "Refresh token: 7 dias expiry, single-use, revogável",
        "JWT signature: RS256 com chave 2048+ bits",
        "Token binding com device fingerprint"
      ],
      validation: "Penetration testing em endpoints auth"
    },
    
    sessionSecurity: {
      description: "Proteção contra session hijacking",
      implementation: [
        "HttpOnly, Secure, SameSite=Strict cookies",
        "Session timeout: 8 horas de inatividade",
        "Maximum session duration: 30 dias",
        "Logout em todos os dispositivos ao alterar senha"
      ]
    }
  },
  
  authorization: {
    rbac: {
      description: "Role-Based Access Control granular",
      roles: ["user", "premium_user", "content_creator", "moderator", "admin"],
      implementation: "PBAC (Policy-Based) com regras JSON",
      validation: "Unit tests para todas as combinações de permissões"
    },
    
    dataOwnership: {
      description: "Verificação de ownership em todas as operações",
      implementation: "Middleware de autorização por recurso",
      pattern: "user_id no token JWT deve match com resource owner"
    }
  }
};
```

### 3.2 Proteção de Dados
```javascript
// security/requirements/data-protection-requirements.js
/**
 * Requisitos de Segurança - Proteção de Dados
 */
const dataProtectionRequirements = {
  encryption: {
    atRest: {
      description: "Criptografia de dados em repouso",
      implementation: [
        "PostgreSQL: TDE (Transparent Data Encryption)",
        "MongoDB: Encryption at rest habilitado",
        "S3: SSE-S3 ou SSE-KMS",
        "Backups: criptografados com chave separada"
      ],
      algorithm: "AES-256-GCM"
    },
    
    inTransit: {
      description: "Criptografia de dados em trânsito",
      implementation: [
        "TLS 1.3 obrigatório",
        "HSTS com preload",
        "Perfect Forward Secrecy habilitado",
        "Certificate pinning para mobile apps"
      ],
      validation: "SSL Labs A+ rating"
    }
  },
  
  piiHandling: {
    classification: {
      level1: ["senha_hash", "tokens", "chaves_privadas"],
      level2: ["cpf", "cnpj", "rg", "cartao_credito"],
      level3: ["email", "telefone", "endereco", "nome_completo"]
    },
    
    controls: {
      level1: "Criptografia determinística para busca",
      level2: "Criptografia com rotação de chaves trimestral",
      level3: "Mascaramento em logs e interfaces administrativas"
    },
    
    retention: {
      default: "7 anos para dados fiscais",
      messages: "30 dias para conteúdo, 1 ano para metadata",
      logs: "90 dias para acesso, 1 ano para auditoria"
    }
  }
};
```

### 3.3 Segurança de APIs
```javascript
// security/requirements/api-security-requirements.js
/**
 * Requisitos de Segurança - APIs
 */
const apiSecurityRequirements = {
  inputValidation: {
    description: "Validação rigorosa de todas as entradas",
    implementation: [
      "Schema validation com Zod em todas as rotas",
      "Maximum payload size: 10MB",
      "Content-Type enforcement",
      "SQL parameterization obrigatória"
    ],
    libraries: ["zod", "express-validator", "pg-parameterize"]
  },
  
  outputEncoding: {
    description: "Encoding apropriado para todos os outputs",
    implementation: [
      "HTML: escape/DOMPurify",
      "JavaScript: hex encoding",
      "CSS: validate URLs",
      "JSON: Content-Type application/json"
    ]
  },
  
  rateLimiting: {
    tiers: {
      anonymous: "100 requests/hour por IP",
      authenticated: "1000 requests/hour por usuário",
      premium: "5000 requests/hour por usuário"
    },
    implementation: "Redis-based sliding window",
    headers: "X-RateLimit-Limit, X-RateLimit-Remaining, X-RateLimit-Reset"
  },
  
  cors: {
    description: "Controle estrito de Cross-Origin Resource Sharing",
    implementation: [
      "Origin whitelist explícita",
      "Credentials apenas para origens confiáveis",
      "Preflight caching: 86400 segundos"
    ]
  }
};
```

## 2. docker-compose.yml

```yaml
version: '3.8'

services:
  # Data Warehouse
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_data
      POSTGRES_USER: data_engineer
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: ${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
      - ./scripts/init.sql:/docker-entrypoint-initdb.d/init.sql
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U data_engineer"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  # Message Queue for Real-time
  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    command: redis-server --appendonly yes

  # Orchestration
  airflow:
    build: ./airflow/docker
    environment:
      AIRFLOW__CORE__EXECUTOR: CeleryExecutor
      AIRFLOW__DATABASE__SQL_ALCHEMY_CONN: postgresql+psycopg2://airflow:airflow@postgres:5432/airflow
      AIRFLOW__CELERY__RESULT_BACKEND: db+postgresql://airflow:airflow@postgres:5432/airflow
      AIRFLOW__CELERY__BROKER_URL: redis://redis:6379/0
    volumes:
      - ./airflow/dags:/opt/airflow/dags
      - ./dbt:/opt/airflow/dbt
      - ./src:/opt/airflow/src
    ports:
      - "8080:8080"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_started

  # Monitoring
  grafana:
    image: grafana/grafana:10.2.0
    environment:
      GF_SECURITY_ADMIN_PASSWORD: ${GRAFANA_PASSWORD}
    volumes:
      - grafana_data:/var/lib/grafana
      - ./dashboards/grafana:/etc/grafana/provisioning/dashboards
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"

  # API Server
  api:
    build:
      context: .
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.api
    environment:
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://data_engineer:${POSTGRES_PASSWORD}@postgres:5432/diyapp_data
    ports:
      - "8000:8000"
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  grafana_data:
```

  - "dbt_packages"

  diyapp_v11:
    staging:
      +materialized: view
      +schema: staging
      +tags: ['staging']

      +materialized: table
      +schema: marts
      +tags: ['marts']
      mart_product:
        +tags: ['product', 'pm']

        +tags: ['ai', 'llm', 'aiops']

        +tags: ['ops', 'sre']

    +materialized: table

tests:

    data_quality:
      +severity: error
    business_logic:
      +severity: warn

## 4. dbt/models/staging/schema.yml

```yaml
version: 2

models:
  - name: stg_app_events
    description: "Cleaned application events from raw events table"
    columns:
      - name: event_id
        description: "Unique event identifier"
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: user_id
        description: "User who triggered the event"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: event_type
        description: "Type of event (click, view, api_call, etc)"
        tests:
          - not_null
          - accepted_values:
              values: ['click', 'view', 'api_call', 'error', 'session_start', 'session_end']
      - name: feature_name
        description: "Which feature was used"
      - name: event_timestamp
        description: "When the event occurred"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: metadata
        description: "Additional event data in JSON format"
      - name: session_id
        description: "User session identifier"
      - name: app_version
        description: "Application version"
        tests:
          - not_null

  - name: stg_user_sessions
    description: "Cleaned user sessions data"
    columns:
      - name: session_id
        description: "Unique session identifier"
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: user_id
        description: "User identifier"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: session_start
        description: "Session start timestamp"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: session_end
        description: "Session end timestamp"
      - name: session_duration_seconds
        description: "Calculated session duration"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: page_views
        description: "Number of pages viewed"
      - name: features_used
        description: "Array of features used in session"

  - name: stg_llm_metrics
    description: "Cleaned LLM metrics from gateway logs"
    columns:
      - name: request_id
        description: "Unique LLM request identifier"
        tests:
          - unique
          - not_null
      - name: model_name
        description: "LLM model used"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: provider
        description: "Model provider (openai, anthropic, etc)"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: feature_called
        description: "Which feature triggered the LLM call"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: input_tokens
        description: "Number of input tokens"
        tests:
          - not_null
          - relationships:
              to: ref('stg_app_events')
              field: feature_name
      - name: output_tokens
        description: "Number of output tokens"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: total_tokens
        description: "Total tokens consumed"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: cost_usd
        description: "Calculated cost in USD"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: latency_ms
        description: "Request latency in milliseconds"
        tests:
          - not_null
      - name: timestamp
        description: "When the request was made"
        tests:
          - not_null
```

## 5. dbt/models/staging/stg_app_events.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='view',
        schema='staging',
        tags=['staging', 'events']
    )
}}

WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT
        id AS event_id,
        user_id,
        event_type,
        feature_name,
        CAST(event_timestamp AS TIMESTAMP) AS event_timestamp,
        metadata::JSONB AS metadata,
        session_id,
        app_version,
        ingested_at
    FROM {{ source('raw', 'app_events') }}
    WHERE event_timestamp >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '90 days'
),

cleaned_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        user_id,
        LOWER(TRIM(event_type)) AS event_type,
        TRIM(feature_name) AS feature_name,
        event_timestamp,
        metadata,
        session_id,
        app_version,
        ingested_at,
        -- Data quality flags
        CASE 
            WHEN user_id IS NULL THEN 1 
            ELSE 0 
        END AS missing_user_id,
        CASE 
            WHEN event_timestamp IS NULL THEN 1 
            ELSE 0 
        END AS missing_timestamp
    FROM raw_events
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    user_id,
    event_type,
    feature_name,
    event_timestamp,
    metadata,
    session_id,
    app_version,
    ingested_at,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS transformed_at
FROM cleaned_events
WHERE missing_user_id = 0 
  AND missing_timestamp = 0
  AND event_timestamp IS NOT NULL
```

## 6. dbt/models/marts/mart_product/daily_active_users.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='marts',
        tags=['product', 'pm', 'kpi'],
        post_hook=[
            "GRANT SELECT ON {{ this }} TO pm_role",
            "{{ create_alert_on_kpi_change('daily_active_users', 'product') }}"
        ]
    )
}}

WITH daily_users AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS date,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS active_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS total_sessions,
        COUNT(*) AS total_events
    FROM {{ ref('stg_app_events') }}
    WHERE event_type IN ('click', 'view', 'api_call', 'session_start')
    GROUP BY 1
),

rolling_metrics AS (
    SELECT
        date,
        active_users,
        total_sessions,
        total_events,
        AVG(active_users) OVER (ORDER BY date ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS weekly_avg_users,
        AVG(total_sessions) OVER (ORDER BY date ROWS BETWEEN 6 PRECEDING AND CURRENT ROW) AS weekly_avg_sessions,
        LAG(active_users, 7) OVER (ORDER BY date) AS active_users_week_ago,
        LAG(active_users, 1) OVER (ORDER BY date) AS active_users_yesterday
    FROM daily_users
)

SELECT
    date,
    active_users,
    total_sessions,
    total_events,
    weekly_avg_users,
    weekly_avg_sessions,
    active_users_week_ago,
    active_users_yesterday,
    -- KPI calculations
    ROUND(
        (active_users - COALESCE(active_users_week_ago, active_users)) * 100.0 / 
        NULLIF(COALESCE(active_users_week_ago, active_users), 0), 
        2
    ) AS wow_growth_pct,
    ROUND(
        (active_users - COALESCE(active_users_yesterday, active_users)) * 100.0 / 
        NULLIF(COALESCE(active_users_yesterday, active_users), 0), 
        2
    ) AS dod_growth_pct,
    -- Quality flags
    CASE 
        WHEN active_users < weekly_avg_users * 0.7 THEN 'BELOW_EXPECTATION'
        WHEN active_users > weekly_avg_users * 1.3 THEN 'ABOVE_EXPECTATION'
        ELSE 'NORMAL'
    END AS kpi_health_status,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP AS calculated_at
FROM rolling_metrics
WHERE date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
ORDER BY date DESC
```

## 7. dbt/models/marts/mart_ai/llm_cost_by_feature.sql

```sql
{{
    config(
        materialized='table',
        schema='marts',
        tags=['ai', 'llm', 'aiops', 'cost'],
        post_hook=[
            "GRANT SELECT ON {{ this }} TO aiops_role",
            "{{ create_cost_alert('llm_cost_by_feature', 1000) }}"
        ]
    )
}}

WITH hourly_cost AS (
    SELECT
        DATE_TRUNC('hour', timestamp) AS hour_start,
        feature_called,
        model_name,
        provider,
        COUNT(*) AS request_count,
        SUM(input_tokens) AS total_input_tokens,
        SUM(output_tokens) AS total_output_tokens,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS total_tokens,
        SUM(cost_usd) AS total_cost_usd,
        AVG(latency_ms) AS avg_latency_ms,
        PERCENTILE_CONT(0.95) WITHIN GROUP (ORDER BY latency_ms) AS p95_latency_ms
    FROM {{ ref('stg_llm_metrics') }}
    WHERE timestamp >= CURRENT_TIMESTAMP - INTERVAL '7 days'
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

feature_daily AS (
    SELECT
        DATE(hour_start) AS date,
        feature_called,
        model_name,
        provider,
        SUM(request_count) AS daily_requests,
        SUM(total_input_tokens) AS daily_input_tokens,
        SUM(total_output_tokens) AS daily_output_tokens,
        SUM(total_tokens) AS daily_total_tokens,
        SUM(total_cost_usd) AS daily_cost_usd,
        AVG(avg_latency_ms) AS daily_avg_latency,
        AVG(p95_latency_ms) AS daily_p95_latency
    FROM hourly_cost
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

cost_trends AS (
    SELECT
        date,
        feature_called,
        model_name,
        provider,
        daily_requests,
        daily_input_tokens,
        daily_output_tokens,
        daily_total

### [Sessão Paralela: AI Ops]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V11 Core - Sistema de Monitoramento Proativo com IA

Vou implementar um sistema completo de monitoramento proativo com IA que detecta anomalias, prevê falhas e auto-otimiza a infraestrutura. O sistema será totalmente autônomo e integrado ao contexto da squad.

                                <div class="metric-card">

                                <i class="bi bi-trash"></i> Limpar
                            </button>
